Svayambhu Purāṇaprathama adhyāyasvayambhūdharmadhātusamutpatti nidānakathāom namaḥ śrī dharmadhātuvāgīśvarāya sarva buddhadharmabodhisattvebhyaḥ śrīmatā yena saddharmastrailoke saṃprakāśitaḥ śrīghanaṃ taṃ mahābuddhaṃ vandekahaṃ śaraṇāśritaḥ  SvayambhuP natvā trijagadīśānaṃ dharmadhātujinālayaṃ tatsvayambhūsamuddeśaṃ vakṣāmi śṛṇutādarāt  SvayambhuP śraddhayā yaḥ śṛṇotīmāṃ svayambhūtpattisatkathāṃ pariśuddhatrikāyāḥ sa bodhisattvo bhaved dhruvaṃ  SvayambhuP tadyathā bhūtpurābhijñaḥ jayaśrī sugatātmajaḥ bodhimaṇḍavihāre sa bijahāra sasāṃdhikaḥ  SvayambhuP tatra jineśvaro nāma bodhisattva mahāmatiḥ śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatvā jayaśrīyaṃ upāśrayet  SvayambhuP tadā dhīmānjayaśrīḥ sa sarvasattva hitārthavit saddharmasamupādeṣṭuṃ sabhāsane samāśrayet  SvayambhuP tatra sarve mahāsattvā bodhisattvā jinātmajāḥ arhanto bhikṣavaścāpi brahmacāriṇaḥ śrāvakāḥ  SvayambhuP bhikṣuṇyo brahmacāriṇyo bratinaścāpyupāsakāḥ upāsikāstathānye pi gṛhasthaśca mahājanāḥ  SvayambhuP brāhmaṇāstirthīkāścāpi yatayaśca tapasvinaḥ rājāno mantriṇomātyāḥ sainyādhipatiśca paurikāḥ  SvayambhuP grāmyā janapadāścāpi tathānyavāsino janāḥ tatsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ śraddhayā samupāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP tatra sabhāsanāsīnaṃ tamarhataṃ jayaśrīyaṃ abhyarcya sādaraṃ natvā tatsabhāyāṃ yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP kṛtāṃjalipuṭāḥ sarve parivṛtya samantataḥ puraskṛtya samudvikṣya samāśrayan samāhitāḥ  SvayambhuP tān sarvān samupāsīnān saddharma śravaṇotsukān dṛṣṭvā jinaśrī bodhisattvaḥ samutthitaḥ  SvayambhuP udvahannuttarāsaṃgaṃ sāṃjali samupāśritaḥ jānubhyāṃ bhūtale dhṛtvā sampaśyannevamavravīt  SvayambhuP bhadantoharṣamicchāmi carituṃ bodhisaṃvaraṃ tadādau kiṃ vrataṃ dhṛtvā saṃcareya samāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP tad bhavān samupādisya sarvānasmān prabodhayan bodhimārge samāyujya cārayituṃ śubherhati  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śrutvā ca sugatātmajaḥ jayaśrīstaṃ mahāsattvaṃ sabhāmantraivamādiśat  SvayambhuP śṛṇu vatsāsti te vāṃchā sambodhisaṃvare yadi yathākramaṃ pravakṣāmi saṃbodhivratasādhanaṃ  SvayambhuP yo vāṃchā tatra saṃsāre carituṃ bodhisaṃvaraṃ sa ādau śaraṇaṃ gatvā sadguruṃ samupāśrayeta  SvayambhuP tadupadeśamāsādya yathāvidyi samāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP tīrthe snātvā viśuddhātmā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ yathāvidhi samabhyarcya saṃbodhi nihitāśayaḥ  SvayambhuP upoṣadhaṃvratamādhāya samācarejjagaddhite evaṃ yaścarate nityaṃ saṃbodhimānasaḥ sudhīḥ  SvayambhuP pariśuddha trikāyaḥ sa bodhisattve bhaved bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvvasattva hitārthabhṛt  SvayambhuP kramātsaṃbodhi saṃbhāraṃ saṃpūrayet samāhitaḥ etatpuṇyābhiyuktātmācaturbrahma vihāradhṛk  SvayambhuP niḥkleśo nirjjayanmārona saṃbodhiḥ samavāpnuyāt  SvayambhuP evaṃ sarvatra lokeṣu saddharma saṃprakāśayan samāpya saugataṃkārya sunirvṛtimavāpnuyāt  SvayambhuP tato rhaṃ sugato bhūtvā sarvvānsattvānpravodhayan bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya saṃvṛttau saṃpracārayet  SvayambhuP evaṃ sarve pi saṃbuddhāḥ yetītā apyanāgatāḥ varttamānāśca te hayetad vratapuṇya vipākataḥ  SvayambhuP bodhiprāpya jinā āsanbhaviṣyanti bhavantyapi evaṃ sarve mahāsattvā bodhisattvā jinātmajāḥ  SvayambhuP arhanto pi thā sarve pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ bodhiṃ prāpya sunirvāṇaṃ yātā yāsyanti yāntyataḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ yūyaṃ parijñāya yadecchatha sunivṛtiṃ triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatvā saṃcaradhvamidaṃ vrataṃ  SvayambhuP iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa sugatātmajaḥ jineśvaraṃ tamarhantaṃ sampaśyannevamavravīt  SvayambhuP bhadanta śrotumichāmi tad vratasthānamuttamaṃ etad vrataṃ caretkutra taddeśaṃ samupādiśat  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthite tena jayaśrīḥ sa mahāmatiḥ jineśvaraṃ mahāsattvaṃ taṃ paśyannevamādiśat  SvayambhuP śṛṇu vatsa samādhāyaṃ vratasthānasamuttamaṃ munīśvarairyathākhyātaṃ tathā vakṣāmi te dhunā  SvayambhuP puṇyakṣetreṣu tīrtheṣu vihāre sugatāśrame buddhānāṃ nivṛtānāṃca caityeṣu pratimāsu ca  SvayambhuP buddhakṣetreṣu sarvatra vratasthānaṃ samuttamaṃ eteṣvami samākhyātaṃ svayambhūcaityaṃ uttamaṃ  SvayambhuP evaṃ vijñāya yo dhīmānvrataṃ caritumicchati sa svayambhū jinakṣetraṃ āśritya caratāṃ vrataṃ  SvayambhuP svayambhūkṣetramāśritya yaścarati vrataṃ mudā sa labhet tanmahat puṇyamakṣayaṃ bodhisādhanaṃ  SvayambhuP etat puṇyaṃ viśuddhātmā bhadraśrī sadguṇāśrayaḥ bodhisattvo mahābhijñā bhavajjinātmajo dhruvaṃ  SvayambhuP durgatiṃ na brajet kvāpi saṃsāre sa kadācana sadā sadgatisaṃjāto bodhicaryāvrataṃ caret  SvayambhuP evaṃ sa saṃsaralloke kṛtvā sarvatra bhadratā saṃbodhi praṇidhiṃ dhṛtvā saṃcare tadjagaddhite  SvayambhuP evaṃ ca bodhi saṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ trividhāṃ bodhimāsādyaḥ nirvṛtipadamāpnuyāt  SvayambhuP evaṃ yūyaṃ parijñātvāḥ svayambhūsthāna āśritā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatvā saṃcaratha vratottamaṃ  SvayambhuP etattenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa sugatātmajaḥ jayaśriyaṃ tamarhantaṃ sampaśyannevamabravīt  SvayambhuP bhadanta bhavatā diṣṭaṃ śrutvā me rocate manaḥ svayambhūcaityamārādhya carituṃ vratamābhavaṃ  SvayambhuP svayambhū caityarājaḥ śrīdharmadhātu jinālayaḥ kutrāstyatra mahīloke tat samādeṣṭumarhati  SvayambhuP iti saprārthitaṃ tena śrutvāṃ so rhan yatiḥ sudhīḥ jayaśrī staṃ mahāsattva samālokyaivamādiśata  SvayambhuP vidyate tra mahīloke uttarasyāṃ himālaye nepāla iti vikhyāteḥ gopucchākhyernagottamaḥ  SvayambhuP tadgirernāma cāturdhya caturyugeṣu vartate tadyathābhūdyuge satye padmagiririti smṛtaḥ  SvayambhuP tretāyāṃ vajrakūṭākhyo gośṛṃgo dvāpare smṛtaḥ idānīṃ tu kalau sau gopuccha iti viśrutaḥ  SvayambhuP so piśailo idānītu lokai nepāla deśakaiḥ sāmheguriti vikhyāta stathāsaṃprasthito bhuvi  SvayambhuP sa sarvadhāturalādi sarvadravyamayoktamaḥ aśvattha pramukhairsavairpādapaiḥ saṃpraśobhitaḥ  SvayambhuP sarvatra kusumairkāntaḥ saṃrvoṣadhiphaladrumaiḥ sarvapakṣivirāvaiścaḥ bhramadbhramaranisvanaiḥ  SvayambhuP jantubhiḥ sakalaḥ sneha nivaddhamaitramānasaiḥ tapasvivaddhayā bhadracāribhiḥ saniṣevitaḥ  SvayambhuP aṣṭāṃga guṇasaṃpanna saṃśuddhāmṛtanirjharaiḥ śobhitaḥ puṣpagaṃdhādhi saṃvāsitaiḥ samīraṇaiḥ  SvayambhuP saṃsevitaḥ sadā divya mahotsāhairvivājitaḥ sarvalokādhipairnityaṃ saṃsevitaḥ samādaraiḥ  SvayambhuP tatra ratnamaya padmaḥ karṇṇikāyāṃ samāśritaḥ divya sphaṭikaratnābhajyotirūpo nirañjanaḥ  SvayambhuP ekahastaḥ pramānoccaścaityarūpo jināśrayaḥ svayambhūḥ sarvalokānāṃ bhadrārtha samavasthitaḥ  SvayambhuP brahma śakrādibhirdevaiḥ sarvaillokādhipairapi sarvairdaityādhipaiścāpi nāgendraiḥ garuḍairapi  SvayambhuP siddhai vidyādharaiḥ sādhyairūryakṣagandharvakinnaraiḥ rākṣasendraiśca rudraiśca grahaistārāgaṇairapi  SvayambhuP vasubhiścāpsarobhiścaḥ sarvaiśva tridaśādhipaiḥ ṛṣibhiryatibhiḥ sarvai yogibhi brahmacāribhiḥ  SvayambhuP sarvaiśca tīrthikai vijñaistāpasaiścāpisajjanaiḥ divāniśaṃ catuḥ saṃdhyaṃ dṛṣṭvā smṛtvā pravanditaḥ  SvayambhuP nityakālaṃ samāgate samabhyarcya samādarāt saṃstutibhiḥ mahotsāhaiḥ saṃmānitābhivanditaḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ sa trijagannāthaḥ svayambhū dharmadhātukaḥ sarvaloka hitārthena saṃbhāṣayansamāsthitaḥ  SvayambhuP idānīntu kalau lokā duṣṭāḥ krūrāśayā śaṭhāḥ dṛṣṭavedaṃ dharmadhātuṃ hi hariṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ  SvayambhuP ityasau śilayāchādya gupti kṛtvā prakāśitaḥ tadupariṣṭīkābhiśca vidhāya caityamuttama  SvayambhuP chātradhvajapatākābhiralaṃkṛtyādhyatiṣṭhataṃ tatrāpi sarvalokaiśca sarvalokādhipairapi  SvayambhuP samāgatya samārādhya samabhyarcyābhivanditaḥ satkāraiśca mahotsāhaiḥ stutipradakṣiṇādibhiḥ  SvayambhuP praṇāmaiśca samārādhya sevito mānito rcitaḥ evaṃ sa trijagannātho dharmadhātu jinālayaḥ  SvayambhuP sarvasattva śubhārthena saṃśobhitā vyavasthitaḥ tatra ye śaraṇaṃ gatvā yānti śuddhayā mudā  SvayambhuP durggatiṃ te na gachanti saṃsāre tra kadācana sadgatāveva saṃjātā dharmmaśrī saṃghaśobhitā  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ bhadraśrī sadguṇadhārā sarvasattva hitaṃkarāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhicaryāvrataṃ dhṛtvā saṃcare jagaddhite evaṃ yūyamapi jñātvā śraddhayā śaraṇa gatāḥ  SvayambhuP svayambhūcaityamārādhya saṃcaradhvaṃ vrataṃ sadā evaṃ kṛtvātra saṃsāre bhadraśrī sadguṇāśrayā  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvā jinātmajā bhaviṣyathaḥ tataḥ saṃbodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP trividhāṃ bodhimāsādya saṃbuddhapadamāpsyathaḥ iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ niśaṃmya sa mahāmatiḥ  SvayambhuP śāstāraṃ taṃ samālokya punarevamavocata bhadanta śrotumicchāmi yatsvayambhū jinālayaḥ  SvayambhuP kadā svayaṃ samutpannaḥ kathaṃ ca tadupādiśa iti saṃprārthita tena śrutvā so rhan yatiḥ sudhīḥ  SvayambhuP jayaśrīstaṃ mahāsattvaṃ saṃpaśyannevamādiśat sādhu śṛṇu mahābhāga yathā mayā śrutaṃ guroḥ  SvayambhuP tathāhaṃ te pravakṣāmi svayambhūtpattisatkathāṃ tadyathā pāṭalīputre pure śoko narādhipaḥ  SvayambhuP saddharma sādhanotsāhī triratnasevako bhavat sa tatra kukkuṭārāme vihāre sugatāśrame  SvayambhuP upaguptaṃ mahābhijñaṃ vandituṃ samupācaret tadā so rhan mahābhijñaḥ sarvasaṃghapuraskṛtaḥ  SvayambhuP sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnastasthau dhyātvā samāhitaḥ tamarhataṃ sabhāsīnaṃ sarvasaṃghapuraskṛtaḥ  SvayambhuP dṛṣṭvāśokaḥ sa bhūmīndro muditaḥ samupācarat tatra sa sahasopetya sāñjalirarhato yatīn  SvayambhuP sarvānnatvopaguptaṃ tamaṣṭāṃgaiḥ prāṇamanmudā tatastaṃ gurumarhantaṃ mahotsāhaiḥ yathāvidhiṃ  SvayambhuP samabhyarcya praṇatvā ca dharmaṃ śrotumupāśrayat tathā tatmantriṇaḥ sarve sāmātyasacivo janāḥ  SvayambhuP tamarhantaṃ yatinnatvā tatraikāntamupāśrayat tataḥ so rhan mahābhijño dṛṣṭvā sarvā samāśritān  SvayambhuP ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ saddharmasamupādiśat tatsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ pravodhitāḥ  SvayambhuP dharmaviśeṣamājñāya saṃbodhivratamīcchire tataḥ so pi mahārājaḥ śrutvā taddharmamuttamaṃ  SvayambhuP saṃbodhisādhanocaryā saṃcarituṃ samaicchata tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā sāñjaliḥ samupāśritaḥ  SvayambhuP tamarhantaṃ mahāsattvaṃ natvā paśyaṃ mudāvadat bhadanta śrotumicchāmi saṃbodhisādhanaṃ vrataṃ  SvayambhuP kutra puṇyatamaṃ kṣatraṃ yatrāśu sidhyate vrataṃ tad bhavān samupādiśya sarvāṃllokān prabodhayan  SvayambhuP bodhimārge samāyujya saṃcārayitumarhati iti saṃprārthite rājñā śrutvā so rhan mahāmatiḥ  SvayambhuP tamaśokaṃ mahīpālaṃ sampaśyannevamabravīt sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ  SvayambhuP tathāhaṃ te pravakṣāmi bodhivrataṃ yadīcchasi sarvakṣatrottamo rājannuttarasyāṃ himālaye  SvayambhuP nepāle iti vikhyāto yatrāśu sidhyate vrataṃ tatrāpyati mahatpuṇyakṣatraṃ buddhaiḥ praśaṃsitaṃ  SvayambhuP svayambhūcaityarājasya dharmadhātoḥ samāśrayaṃ tatra yadyatkṛtaṃ karma tattatsaṃsidhyate dutaṃ  SvayambhuP iti sarvai mahāsattvaiḥ saṃsevitaṃ jinairapi iti vijñāya rājendra sambodhiṃ yadi vāñchasi  SvayambhuP taccaityaśaraṇaṃ gatvā saṃcarasva susaṃvaraṃ etatpuṇyaviśuddhātmā bhadraśrī sadguṇarddhimān  SvayambhuP bodhisattvo mahābhijño bhaveḥ sarvahitārthabhṛt tataḥ kramena sambodhiṃ saṃbhāraṃ paripūrayan  SvayambhuP niḥkleśo rhañjagannāthāḥ sambuddhapadamāpsyasi iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ niśamya sa nṛpo mudā  SvayambhuP upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā papracchaivaṃ samādarāt bhadanta śrotumichāmi svayambhūtpatti satkathāṃ  SvayambhuP kadā svayaṃ samutpannaṃ statsamādeṣṭumarhati iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so rhan yatiḥ surdhīḥ  SvayambhuP aśokaṃ taṃ mahīpālaṃ sampaśyannevamādiśat sādhu rājan yathādiṣṭaṃ guruṇā me śrutaṃ mayā  SvayambhuP tathāhaṃ saṃpravakṣāmi śṛṇuṣva tatsamāhitaḥ tadā cāsau jagacchāstā śākyamunistathāgataḥ  SvayambhuP sarvajño dharmarājo rhan munīśvaro vināyakaḥ sa sarvaḥ sāṃdhikaiḥ sārddhaṃ janapadeṣu saṃcaran  SvayambhuP ekasmin samaye tatra nepāle samupācarat gopucchaparvvatapārśve paścime śrīsvayambhūvaḥ  SvayambhuP pucchāgro bhidha caityasyasaṃnnidhau sugatāśrame sarvasattvahitārthena pūrṇanduriva bhāsayan  SvayambhuP saddharmma samupārdeṣṭuṃ vijahāra sasāṃdhikaḥ yadā sa bhagavāñchāstān sattvānāṃ dharmma vṛddhaye  SvayambhuP saddharmma samupādeṣṭuṃ sabhāsane samāśrayat taṃ dṛṣṭvā tadā tatra mañjuśriyaḥ mamāśrame  SvayambhuP vihāre vāsinī cūḍābhidhānī brahmacāriṇī arhantī bhikṣuṇī bhadrā saddharmmaguṇavāñchinī  SvayambhuP suprasannāśrayā śuddhā kāṣāya cīvarāvṛtā divyapūjopacārāṇi samādāya pramoditā  SvayambhuP tatsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ tatrāśu samupācarat tadā tatra mahāsattvā bodhisattvā jinātmajāḥ  SvayambhuP maitreyapramukhāḥ sarve taddharma śrotumāgatāḥ arhanto bhikṣavaścāpi śrāvakā brahmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP bhikṣuṇyo brahmacāriṇyaḥ cailakā vratino pi ca triratnaśaraṇāsīnāścopāsakā upāsikāḥ  SvayambhuP bauddhabhaktiratāḥ sarve taddharmaśrotumāgatāḥ sarve te samupāyātāstatra sabhāsanāśritaṃ  SvayambhuP saṃbuddhaṃ taṃ samālokya muditāḥ samupācaran te sarve bhyarcya taṃ nāthaṃ natvā sāñjalayormudā  SvayambhuP tatsaddharmāmṛta pātuṃ tatsabhāyāṃ samāśrayan brahmaśakrādayā devāḥ sarve lokādhipā api  SvayambhuP grahāstārāgaṇāścāpi siddhā vidyādharā api sādhyā rudrāśca gandharvā yakṣaguhyakakinnarāḥ  SvayambhuP daityendrā rākṣasendrāca nāgendrā garuḍā api evamanyepi lokendrāḥ sarve tatra mudāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP taṃ munīndraṃ samabhyarcya natvā tatra samāśrayan hāritī yakṣiṇī cāpi bodhisattvānupālinī  SvayambhuP sā bhavantaṃ tamānasya tatsabhāyāṃ samāśrita atha sa bhagavānañchāstā dṛṣṭvā sarvān samāśritān  SvayambhuP maitreyaṃ samupāmantrya sampaśyannevamādiśat maitreyemaṃ jagannāthaṃ svayambhūvaṃ jinālayaṃ  SvayambhuP dharmadhātuṃ triratnāyaṃ paśyadhvaṃ yūyamādarāt bhajadhvaṃ śraddhayā nityaṃ gatvātra śaraṇaṃ mudā  SvayambhuP bodhicaryāvrataṃ dhṛtvā saṃcarante jagaddhite śraddhayā ye bhajantyatra śaraṇaṃ samupāśritāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhicaryāvrataṃ dhṛtvā saṃcarante jagaddhite sarve vimuktapāpāste pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahābhijñāḥ bhaveyuḥ sadguṇāśrayāḥ bhadraśrīsukhasampannaścaturbrahmavihārikāḥ  SvayambhuP sarvasattva hitodyuktāḥ saṃbodhivratacāriṇaḥ na kvāpi durgatiṃyāyuḥ sadā sadgatisaṃbhavāḥ  SvayambhuP triratnabhajanotsāhāḥ saddharmmasādhanodyamāḥ tataḥ pravrajyā saṃbuddhaśāsane śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  SvayambhuP brahmacaryāṃ vrataṃ dhṛtvā saṃcareran samāhitāḥ tataste nirmalātmāno niḥkleśāḥ vijitendriyāḥ  SvayambhuP trividhāṃ bodhimāsādha sambuddhapadmāpnuyuḥ evaṃ vijñāya ye martyā vāñchanti saugataṃ padaṃ  SvayambhuP te bhajantu sadātraiva śraddhayā śaraṇāśritāḥ ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa niśamya te sabhāśritāḥ  SvayambhuP sarve lokāḥ pramodantastathā bhajitumīcchīre maitreyaḥ sa tato dhīmān bodhisattva hi moditaḥ  SvayambhuP samutthāya munīndrasya purataḥ samupācaran udvahannuktarāsaṃgaṃ praṇatvā taṃ munīśvaraṃ  SvayambhuP jānubhyāṃ bhuvi saṃghāya sāñjaliretamavravīta bhagavān nāthaḥ sarvajña dharmadhātujinālayaḥ  SvayambhuP kadāyaṃ svayaṃmutpanna stansamādeṣṭumarhati iti saṃprārthite tena maitreyeṇa mahātmanā  SvayambhuP bhagavantaṃ mahāvijñaṃ saṃpaśyannevamādiśata sādhu śṛṇu samādhāya maitreyo sya svayambhūvaḥ  SvayambhuP samutpattikathāṃ vakṣe sarvalokābhibodhane purāsmin bhadrakalpe bhūd vipaśvī nāma sarvavit  SvayambhuP jagachāstā munīndro rhan dharmmarājastathāgataḥ aśīti varṣa sāhasra paramāyūṃṣi yadā nṛṇāṃ  SvayambhuP tadāhaṃ satya dharmmākhyā bodhisattvābhavaṃt kila yadā sa bhagavāñchāstā vandhumatyāḥ puro ntike  SvayambhuP vihāre dharmmamādiśca vijahāra sasāṃdhikaḥ tadāhaṃ taṃ jagannāthamārādhya samupasthitaḥ  SvayambhuP tadātrā bhūtsaptakośa vyāyāmavistaro hradaḥ tadanuśāsanāṃ dhṛtvā prācaraṃ bodhi samvaraṃ  SvayambhuP aṣṭāṃga guṇa sampannaḥ jalāśrayo nagāvṛtaḥ padmotpalādi saugandhi nānā puṣpa praśobhitaḥ  SvayambhuP haṃsa sārasa kāḍamba pramukha pakṣimaṇḍitaḥ tīropāntanagāruha sarvarttu puṣpitairdrumaiḥ  SvayambhuP phalauṣadhādi bṛkṣaiśca samantāt parimaṇḍitaḥ mīnakacchapamaṇḍūkapramukha jalavāsināṃ  SvayambhuP jantūnāṃ nilayo gādhaḥ sarvanāgādhipālayaḥ tatra sarvāhirājendraḥ karkkoṭakābhidho mahān  SvayambhuP evaṃ tadā mahā tīrthaḥ puṇyāmṛtāśrayo vabhau sadā tratridaśāḥ saddharmapsarobhiḥ pramoditāḥ  SvayambhuP snātvā saṃkrīḍamānāḥ satsaukhyaṃ bhuktvā divaṃ yayuḥ tathā brahmādayaḥ sarve maharṣayastapaśvinaḥ  SvayambhuP snāna saṃdhyādikaṃ karmma kṛtvā saṃsevire sadā evaṃ lokādhipāścāpi snātvātra sarvadā mudā  SvayambhuP svasva kule samabhyarcya mahotsāhairnisevire evaṃmanyepi lokāśca vratino brahmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP snātvātra saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvāḥ pūtātmāno divaṃ yayuḥ bodhisattvā tathānaike snānadānavrataṃ mudā  SvayambhuP kṛtvātra vimalātmānaḥ samācārañjagaddhite evaṃ sarve munīndraiśca snāna vratādi bījaṃphalaṃ  SvayambhuP mahatpuṇyataraṃ śreṣṭhamākhyātaṃ bodhisādhanaṃ yatra snātvā triratnānāṃ śaraṇe samupāśritāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhicaryā vrataṃ dhṛtvā prācaranta jagaddhite te āśu vimalātmāno bhadraśrīsatguṇānvitāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvāḥ mahāsattvā vabhūvuḥ sugatātmajāḥ kecinniḥ kleśitātmāno bhavasaṃcāre nispṛhāḥ  SvayambhuP śrāvakabodhisattvamāsādya babhūvu brahmacāriṇaḥ kecicca nirmalātmāno saṃsāre viratāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP pratyekabodhimāsādya sunirvṛtiṃ samāyayuḥ kecit saṃbodhicittaṃ ca prāpya saddharmalālasāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhicaryāvrataṃ dhṛtvā samācarañjagaddhite kecit sarve bhuktvā divyakāmasukhānyapi  SvayambhuP saddharmaguṇasaṃraktāḥ prācaran sarvadā śubhe kecit sarve mahīpālāḥ sunīti dharmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP kṛtvā sattvahitārthāni yayurante jinālayaṃ ahamapi tadā tatra snātvācaraṃ vrataṃ sadā  SvayambhuP etatpuṇyaviśuddhātmā drutaṃ sambodhimāptavān yaiścāpyasya jalaṃ pītaṃ te pi nirmuktapātakāḥ  SvayambhuP pariśuddhāśayā bhadrā babhūvu bodhibhāginaḥ evamasau mahātīrthaḥ sarvairapi munīśvaraiḥ  SvayambhuP samadhiṣṭhāpito dyāpi praśaṃsito mahītale tatra paścāt svayaṃ dharmadhāturutpatsyate dhruvaṃ  SvayambhuP ityādiśya munīndrau sau bhūyā erevaṃ samādiśat tadā tatra samupanne dharmadhātau jinālaye  SvayambhuP nirutpātaṃ śubhotsāhaṃ pravartiṣyati sarvadā sarve lokāśca taṃ dṛṣṭvā dharmadhātuṃ svayambhūvaṃ  SvayambhuP śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatvā prabhajiṣyanti sarvadā tadetatpuṇyaliptāste sarve lokāḥ śubhendriyāḥ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrī satsukhaṃ bhuktvā yāsyantyante jinālayaṃ ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa vipaśvinā niśamyate  SvayambhuP sarve sabhāśritā lokāḥ prābhyanandan pravodhitāḥ iti vipaśvinā śāstā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā  SvayambhuP tathā yuṣmatprodhārtha samākhyātaṃ pravuddhyatāṃ ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrīghanena niśamyate  SvayambhuP maitreyādi samālokāḥ sarve pi saṃprasedire iti svayambhūdharmadhātu samutpatti nidānakathā prathamo dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ dvitīya adhyāya pūjāphalavarṇano nāmaatha dhīmān mahāsattvo maitreyaḥ sa jinātmajaḥ bhagavantaṃ punarnatvā sāñjalirevamabravīt  SvayambhuP bhagavacchrotumicchāmi svayambhūtpatti satkathāṃ tadbhavānsamupākhyātuṃ lokānāṃ saṃpravodhane  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena maitreyeṇa sudhīmatā bhagavānstān sabhālokān sampaśyannevamādiśat  SvayambhuP sādhu maitreya sarve pi sabhālokāḥ samādarāt śṛṇudhvaṃ saṃpravakṣāmi svayambhūtpattisatkathāṃ  SvayambhuP tadyathā nirvṛtiṃ yāte vipaśvini munīśvare cirakālāntareṇātra jagacchāstābhavat punaḥ  SvayambhuP śikhi nāma munīndro rhan dharmarājastathāgataḥ sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ sarvavidyādhipo vināyakaḥ  SvayambhuP tadā saptativarṣāṇāṃ sahasrāryunṛṇāmabhūt ahaṃ kṣemaṃkaro nāma bodhisattvo bhavaṃ kila  SvayambhuP yadā sa bhagavāñchāstā śikhidharmādhipo jinaḥ aruṇākhyapuropānte vyaharat saugatāśrame  SvayambhuP tadā sarve mahāsattvā bodhisattvā jinātmajāḥ śikhinastasya śāstuḥ saṃprābhajan samupasthitāḥ ahamapi tathā tasya śikhinastrijagadguroḥ  SvayambhuP śaraṇe samupasthāya prābhajaṃ sarvadā mudā tatraika samaye so rhan bhagavān sarvavicchikhī  SvayambhuP saddharma samupādeṣṭuṃ sabhāsane samāśrayet tadvīkṣya bhikṣavaḥ sarve śrāvakā brahmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP bhikṣuṇyo vratinaḥ sarve upāsakā upāsikāḥ tatsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ samupāgatya taṃ muniṃ  SvayambhuP natvā sāñjalayastatra parivṛtya samāśrayet tadā brahmāmarendrādi tridaśāḥ sarve āgatāḥ  SvayambhuP sarve lokādhipāścāpi dharma śrotuṃ samāgatāḥ siddhā vidyādharā sādhyā yakṣagandharvakinnarāḥ  SvayambhuP garuḍā rākṣasendrāśca daityā nāgādhipā api ṛṣayo brāhmaṇāścāpi tīrthikāścāpi tapasvinaḥ  SvayambhuP yatayo yoginaścāpi nirgranthāśca digambarāḥ rājāno kṣatriyā vaiśyā amātyā mantriṇo janāḥ  SvayambhuP śilpino vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhādayo mahājanāḥ paurā jānapadā grāmyāstathānyadeśavāsinaḥ  SvayambhuP tatsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ saṃharṣitāḥ samāgatāḥ tatra te samupāgatya samīkṣya taṃ munīśvaraṃ  SvayambhuP yathākramaṃ samabhyarcya kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇāṃ kṛtvāñjali puṭo natvā parivṛtya samantataḥ  SvayambhuP puraskṛtya samudvīkṣya samādarādupāśrayan tān sarvān samupāsīnāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavāñchikhī  SvayambhuP ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ saddharma samupādiśat tatsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ pravodhitāḥ  SvayambhuP saddharmasādhanodyuktā vabhūvu bodhibhāginaḥ tasminneva samaye tatra puṇyajalāśraye hrade  SvayambhuP maṇinālaṃ mahaddīptihīrakeśaramuttama pañcaratnamayaṃ divyasarojarājakarṇṇikaṃ  SvayambhuP prādurbhūtaṃ mahāpadmaṃ sahasradalakāśitaṃ tasya ratnasarojasya karṇṇikāmadhyamaṇḍale  SvayambhuP svayambhūtsamutpanno dharmmadhāturjinālayaḥ ekahastapramāṇāṃśuḥ śubhraratnamayojjvalaḥ  SvayambhuP sambodhiśrīguṇādhāraḥ sarvalakṣaṇamaṇḍitaḥ jyotirūpo jagajjeṣṭha pañcatathāgatāśrayaḥ  SvayambhuP jagadīśo jagat vandyo jagatpūjyo jagatprabhuḥ anādinidhano jīrṇṇo mānyaḥ sarvaśubhārthabhṛt  SvayambhuP samantabhadrarūpo graḥ śreṣṭhaḥ saddharmaratnabhṛt trailokyasadguṇādhīśaścaturvarggaphalapradaḥ  SvayambhuP tasmiṃścaitye samutpanne sāvdhinagā rasācalat  SvayambhuP divyasugandhipuṣpāṇi saṃnipetuḥ surālayāt suradundubhayo neduḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ prasedire  SvayambhuP vahnayo dakṣiṇāvarttā bhadrābhāḥ saṃprajahvalaḥ suśītalāḥ sugandhyādyā dhīraṃ vavuḥ samīraṇāḥ  SvayambhuP vavarṣuḥ surasāmbūni meghā gambhīranisvanāḥ graha tārenducandrābhāḥ sabhāsitā virejire  SvayambhuP stutimaṅgalasaṃgītiśabdā vyomni pracerire sarvatrāpi sumāṅgalyamahotsāhaṃ nirantaraṃ  SvayambhuP subhikṣaṃ śrīguṇorbhāvaṃ saddharma bhadrasādhanaṃ nirutpātaṃ śubhācāraṃ prāvarttata samantataḥ  SvayambhuP tamevaṃ svayambhūtpannaṃ dharmmadhātuṃ jinālayaṃ samīkṣyeśādayaḥ sarve ārupya bhuvanāśritāḥ  SvayambhuP yogadhyāna mahānanda saukhye pi viratotsavāḥ svayambhuvaṃ tamīśānaṃ vandituṃ samupācaran  SvayambhuP tathā brahmādayaḥ sarve munayo brahmacāriṇaḥ evaṃ svayambhuvaṃ draṣṭuṃ muditā samupācaran  SvayambhuP evaṃ śakrādayaḥ sarve tridaśāḥ sāpsaro gaṇāḥ pūjāṅgāni samādāya draṣṭumenaṃ mudā yayuḥ  SvayambhuP tathāgnidharmarājo pi naiṛto varuṇo marut śrīdo bhūtādhipaścaivaṃ sarve lokādhipā api  SvayambhuP svasvaparijanaiḥ sārddha mahotsāhaiḥ pramoditāḥ evaṃ svayambhuvaṃ caityaṃ saṃdraṣṭuṃ samupāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP dhṛtarāṣṭro mahārājo gandharvaiḥ saha moditaḥ saṃgītivādanotsāhaiḥ sahainaṃ draṣṭumāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP viruḍhako mahārājaḥ kumbhāṇḍasahitā mudā svayambhuvaṃ tamālokya mudā vanditumāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP virupākṣo pi nāgendraiḥ sarvai nāgādhipaiḥ saha ratnapūjopahārāṇi dhṛtvainaṃ draṣṭumāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP kuvero yakṣarājo pi yakṣaṇībhiḥ samanvitaḥ nānādravyopahārāṇi dhṛtvainaṃ draṣṭumāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP vajrapāṇiśca guhyendrasarvaguhyakasaṃyutaḥ divyabhogyāpahārāṇi dhṛtvainaṃ draṣṭumāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP drumaḥ kinnararājo pi sarvaiḥ saha hyānanaiḥ tūryasaṃghoṣaṇotsāhaiḥ sahinaṃ draṣṭumāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP tathā sarvārthasiddhākhyaḥ sarvavidyādharādhipaḥ divyapūjopahārāṇi dhṛtvainaṃ draṣṭumāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP garuḍaḥ pakṣirājo pi sarvaiḥ pakṣigaṇaiḥ saha svasvarddhiśrīmahotsāhairenaṃ saṃdraṣṭumāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ siddhāśca sādhyāśca vasavaśca grahā api sarvāstārāganāścāpi sarvāścāpyapsarogaṇāḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ daityādhipāḥ sarve svasvaparijanaiḥ saha mahāsamṛddhiprātsāhaiḥ sahasā samupācaran  SvayambhuP evaṃ lokādhipāḥ sarve daśadikṣu vyavasthitāḥ dṛṣṭvā taṃ svayambhūtpannaṃ vandituṃ sahasācaran  SvayambhuP sarve pi te samāgatya dṛṣṭvā taṃ jagadīśvaraṃ saṃharṣitāśayā dūrāt praṇatvā samupācaran  SvayambhuP tataste jagannātha sarve bhyarcya yathākramaṃ aṣṭāṃgaiḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā prābhajanta samādarāt  SvayambhuP keciddavyasugandhaistaṃ prābhilipyābhajan mudā kecinnānāvidhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ keciddhūpairmanoharaiḥ  SvayambhuP kecicca puṣpamālābhiḥ kecicca divyacīvaraiḥ kecicca dīpamālābhiḥ kecidāratidīpanaiḥ  SvayambhuP keciddivyāmṛtaiḥ bhogyaiḥ keciddivyauṣadhairapi kecinnānāvidhairdivyaratnālaṃkārābhūṣaṇaiḥ  SvayambhuP kecicchatradhvajaivalivyajanaiśca vitānakaiḥ kecit saṃgītisaṃvādyairmṛdaṅgamurajādibhiḥ  SvayambhuP kecit tauryatrikai vaṃśaiḥ śaṃkhaiḥ śṛgaiśca kecana kāhāraiśca tathā kecit vīṇādītatavādanaiḥ  SvayambhuP tālādighanavādyaiśca bheryānakamardalaiḥ tathā nānāvidhairmaḍḍurḍiṇḍimajharjharādibhiḥ  SvayambhuP kecitnṛtyaiśca gītaiśca hāhākāraiśca kecana evaṃ nānāvidhotsāhaiḥ prābhajanstaṃ jinālayaṃ  SvayambhuP kecit pradakṣiṇānyeva kṛtvā bhajan sahasraśaḥ kecicca dhāraṇīvidyājapastotrādibhirmudā  SvayambhuP evaṃ nānāprakāraiste sarve lokā dvijādayaḥ śraddhayā samupāśritya prābhajanstaṃ svayambhuvaṃ  SvayambhuP etaddivyamahotsāhaiḥ saṃpravṛttiṃ prasāritāṃ śrutvā sarve sabhālokā vismayaṃ samupāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP tat samīkṣya mahāsattvā ratnapāṇiḥ purogataḥ śikhinaṃ taṃ muniṃ natvā sāñjalirevamabravīt  SvayambhuP bhagavan yatmahī sarvā kampitā divyamutsavaṃ prasāritaṃ ca kasyedaṃ hetu tat samupādiśa  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena sudhiyā ratnapāṇinā sa śikhi bhagavān paśyan ratnapāṇiṃ tamabravīt  SvayambhuP sādhu śṛṇu mahāsattva yat sarvā calitā mahī divyotsāhaiḥ pravṛttaṃ ca taddhetuṃ saṃnigadyate  SvayambhuP tadyathātrāsti bhūloka uttarasyāṃ himālaye aṣṭāṅgaguṇasampannapuṇyajalāśrayo hradaḥ  SvayambhuP tatra ratnamaye padme sarojarājakarṇṇike svayameva samutpanno dharmadhātujinālayaḥ  SvayambhuP tadutpanne mahī sarvā racitā saṃpramoditāḥ sarvatrāpi śubhotsāhaṃ prāvrarttate bhavālaya  SvayambhuP taṃ samīkṣya maheśānabrahmāśakrādayo marāḥ grahāstārāśca siddhāśca sādhyā vidyādharā api  SvayambhuP maharṣaśca sarve pi savismayapramoditāḥ sarve lokādhipāścāpi daityā nāgāḥ khageśvarāḥ  SvayambhuP yakṣakinnaragandharvvaguhyakarākṣasā apiḥ etatprabhṛtayaḥ sarve samīkṣya taṃ svayaṃbhuvaṃ  SvayambhuP saṃharṣitāḥ samāgatya prabhajante mahotsavaiḥ etatpūjāmahotsāhasaṃpravṛttiḥ prasārita  SvayambhuP etasyedaṃ mahadbhanimittaṃ saṃprajāyate ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śikhinā saṃnisaṃmya saḥ  SvayambhuP ratnapāṇimahāsattvāḥ savismayapramoditaḥ suprabuddhamukhāmbhojā mahāsaṃharṣitāśayaḥ  SvayambhuP bhūyastaṃ śikhinaṃ natvā sāñjalirevabravīt bhagavan taddhijānīyādyanmano me samīcchate  SvayambhuP tadanujñāṃ pradatvātra saṃprasādayatumarhati ahamapi jagacchāstaḥ svayambhuvaṃ tamīśvaraṃ  SvayambhuP śraddhayā samupāśritya prabhajāmi mahotsavaiḥ iti saṃprārthite tena śrutvā sa bhagavāñchikhi  SvayambhuP ratnapāṇiṃ mahāsattvaṃ saṃpaśyannevamādiśat kulaputra prayāhi tvaṃ yadyāśu bodhimicchasi  SvayambhuP śraddhayā samupāśritya prabhaja taṃ jinālayaṃ ye tatra samupāśritya bhajeyuḥ śraddhayā mudā  SvayambhuP teāśu prāpya saṃbodhiṃ sambuddhapadamāpnuyuḥ ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa ratnapāṇi niśamya saḥ  SvayambhuP sāñjalistaṃ muniṃ natvā muditaḥ prācarat tataḥ tatastena sahāneke bodhisattvā jinātmajāḥ  SvayambhuP śrāvakā bhikṣavaścāpi bhikṣuṇyaścāpyupāsikāḥ upāsakā bhaktimanto vratinaḥ puṇyalālasāḥ  SvayambhuP ṛṣayo brāhmaṇāścāpi yatayo yogino pi ca tīrthikāstāpasāścāpi nirgranthā brahmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP rājānaḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā amātyā mantriṇo janāḥ śilpino vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāścāpi mahājanāḥ  SvayambhuP paurā jānapadā grāmyastathānyadeśavāsinaḥ evamanyepi lokāśca saddharmaguṇavāñchinaḥ  SvayambhuP sarve tatra mahotsāhaistena sārddha mudā carat evaṃ sa ratnapāṇistaiḥ sarvaiḥ lokai samanvitaḥ  SvayambhuP pūjāṅgāni samādāya mahotsāhai mudācarat evaṃ sa pravarañchrīmān sarvāṃllokān vinodayan  SvayambhuP sahasā tatra prāgatya dadarśemaṃ jinālayaṃ dṛṣṭvainaṃ sa mahāsattvaḥ muditaḥ samupāsaran  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya praṇatvā prābhajanmudā evaṃ sarve pi te lokāḥ sahāyāstasyamaharṣayaḥ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya mahotsāhai mudābhajan evaṃ te sakalā lokā stutvā japtvā ca dhāraṇī  SvayambhuP pradakṣiṇāni kṛtvoṣṭa praṇatvā prābhajan mudāḥ evamanye mahāsattvā bodhisattvā jinātmajāḥ  SvayambhuP daśadigbhyaḥ samāgatya prābhajannimamīśvaraṃ ahamapi tadā tena sahetya ratnapāṇinā  SvayambhuP śraddhayā samupāśritya prābhajanimamīśvaraṃ etatpuṇyānubhāvena bodhiṃ prāpya kalāvapi  SvayambhuP jitvā māragaṇān sarvān dharmādhipo bhavāmyahaṃ ye yesya samupāśritya bhajeyuḥ śraddhayā mudā  SvayambhuP te te sarve pi saṃbodhiṃ prāpya syuḥ sugatā drutaṃ evaṃ mahattaraṃ puṇyasya sevāsamudbhavaṃ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrīsadguṇāpannaṃ sambodhijñānasādhanaṃ iti sarvai munīndraiśca samākhyātaṃ samantataḥ  SvayambhuP yūyamapi parijñāya bhajatāsya samādarāt munīndrā api sarve sya catuḥsandhyaṃ divāniśaṃ  SvayambhuP dṛṣṭvā dhyātvā smṛtiṃ dhṛtvā prābhajantaṃ samādarāt bhajanti sāmprataṃ sarve buddhāḥ sarve digāśritāḥ  SvayambhuP anāgatāśca sarve pi bhajiṣyanti tathā sadā asya darśanamātreṇa praduṣṭā api pāpinaḥ  SvayambhuP nirmukta pātakā hyāśu bhaveyu nirmalendriyāḥ tataste nirmalātmāno niḥkleśo brahmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP durgati naiva gaccheyuḥ kutrāpi hi kadācana saṅgatāveva saṃjātā bhadraśrīsadguṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhaveyuḥ sugatātmajāḥ tataste bodhisambhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP trividhāṃ bodhimāsādya nirvṛtiṃ padamāpnuyuḥ iti natvā sadāpyasya kṛtvā darśanamādarāt  SvayambhuP anumodyābhyanusmṛtvā dhyātvānubhāvya sarvadā nāmāpi ca samuccārya śraddhayā bodhivāchibhiḥ  SvayambhuP yathāśakti prakarttavyā bhaktisevā sadādarāt ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrīghanena niśamyate  SvayambhuP maitreyapramukhāḥ sarve sabhālokāḥ prabodhitāḥ tathetyabhyanumodanto dharmmadhāto svayambhuvaḥ  SvayambhuP śraddhayā samupāśritya saṃbhajituṃ samīcchire atha sarvve sabhālokā dharmmadhātoḥ svayambhuvaḥ  SvayambhuP pūjāphalaviśeṣāṇi saṃśrotuṃ punarīcchireḥ tanmatvā sa mahāsattvo maitreyaḥ sugatātmaja  SvayambhuP bhagavantaṃ munīndrantaṃ prārthayadevamānataḥ bhagavannasya pūjāyā viśeṣaphalavistaraṃ  SvayambhuP sarvve ime sabhālokāḥ śrotumicchanti sāmprataṃ tadbhagavān samupādiśya pūjāphalaviśeṣatāṃ  SvayambhuP imāṃ sarvān sabhāsīnāṃ saṃbodhayitumarhati iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena maitreyeṇa niśamya saḥ  SvayambhuP bhagavānstān sabhālokān sampaśyanaivamādiśat śṛṇudhvaṃ sakalā lokā asya pūjāphalaṃ mahat  SvayambhuP viśeṣeṇa pravakṣyāmi sarve lokābhibodhane pañcāmṛtaiḥ sahāmbhobhiḥ saṃśobhitasunirmmalaiḥ  SvayambhuP ye mudā snāpayantimaṃ dharmmadhātuṃ jinālayaṃ mandākinyāṃ sadā snātvā te viśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ  SvayambhuP divyasukhāni bhuṃjāno prānte yāni jinālayaṃ saurabhya dravyasaṃyukti yatra caityai svayambhuvi  SvayambhuP modayanto jagaccittaṃ dhūpayanti mudā sadāḥ te sugaṃdhitasaumyāṅgā mānyā devā surairapi  SvayambhuP śrīmantaḥ susvasaṃpannā bhavanti ratnasannibhāḥ pañcagandhairmudā yatra dharmmadhāto jinālaye  SvayambhuP liptārādhya samāśritya prabhajanti sadādarāt saptaratnasametāste bhadraśrīsadguṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP sarvve lokā hitodyuktā bhavanti kṣitipādhipāḥ ye cātra munirājendrā vicitra cīvarāmbaraiḥ  SvayambhuP pravārya śraddhayā bhaktyā saṃbhajante samādarāt te divyadṛṣya kauśeya ratnābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ  SvayambhuP sujñā dharmādhipāḥ santo bhavanti bhadracāriṇaḥ ye caimaṃ kusumaiḥ sarvvai jalajai sthalajairapi  SvayambhuP arccayitvā samāśritya saṃbhajante pramoditāḥ mahīndraśrīsamṛddhāste śakrādhikaprabhānvitāḥ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrīsukhasaṃpannā bhavanti bodhibhāginaḥ yacainaṃ puṣpamālābhi racitābhirmanoharaiḥ  SvayambhuP sarvvapuṣpaiḥ pralambābhiḥ śobhayitvā bhajanti ca bhavanti śrīsamṛddhāste dharmmakāmāḥ suradhipāḥ  SvayambhuP satkīrttirguṇasaṃraktāḥ śubhagā bodhicāriṇaḥ ye ca puṣpāṇi sarvāṇi mudātra sugatālaye  SvayambhuP avakīrya samārādhya bhajanti śaraṇāśritāḥ te pi devādhipā svarge gatā mahyāṃ nṛpādhipāḥ  SvayambhuP mahacchrīguṇasampannā bhavanti bodhibhāginaḥ dhṛtasugandhitailādisaṃpradīptāṃ tamopahāṃ  SvayambhuP jvālayanti mudā ye smiṃ dharmmadhātau jinālaye suduṣṭayaḥ surupāste jñānadīpatamopahāḥ  SvayambhuP bhūpārcitapadāmbhojā bhavanti bodhibhāginaḥ praṇītaṃ surasaṃbhojyaṃ valbhagandhasamanvitaṃ  SvayambhuP ye cāsminnupaḍhaukitvā prabhajanti samādarāt ṛddhimanto nṛpeṃdrāste saptaratnasamanvitā  SvayambhuP svargge devādhipāścāpi bhavanti bodhibhāginaḥ ye cāsmiṃ surasaṃpānaṃ suvarṇṇagandhasaṃyutaṃ  SvayambhuP upaḍhaukya samārādhya prabhajante samāhitāḥ te valiṣṭhā mahīpendrāḥ śrīsamṛddhā nirogiṇaḥ  SvayambhuP svarge gatāśca devendrā bhavanti bodhibhāginaḥ ye cāsmiṃ skandamūlāni bījapatraphalāni ca  SvayambhuP śraddhayā samupasthāpya saṃbhajante samāśritāḥ te prabhuktvā yathākāmaṃ bhogyāni vividhānyapi  SvayambhuP saddharmmasādhanā raktāḥ saṃyāntyante jinālayaṃ ye cāsmiṃ sugatādhāre pathyauṣadhagaṇānyapi  SvayambhuP samarpya śraddhayā nityaṃ prasevyante samādarāt te valiṣṭhā supuṣṭāṅgāḥ saumyendriyā nirāmayāḥ  SvayambhuP rājyaśrīsukhamābhujya saṃyātyante sukhāvatī ye cāpyatra jinādhāre dharmmadhātau svayambhuvi  SvayambhuP vitatyoccai vitānaṃ ca sasevyante samādarāt dhanyāste guṇino vaṃdyāḥ śuddhavaṃśā vicakṣaṇāḥ  SvayambhuP sarvvārthasiddhisampannāḥ prayāntyante jinālayaṃ ye cāsmin sugatāvāse vicitrānucchritāndhvajān  SvayambhuP avaropya mahotsāhaiḥ saṃbhajante bhinanditā śrīsadguṇasukhadhārā bhūtvā bhūpādhipā bhuvi  SvayambhuP svarge devādhipāścānte saṃprayānti jinālayaṃ sauvarṇṇaratnapuṣpādi chatrāṇi vividhāni ye  SvayambhuP āropyatra mahotsāhaiḥ saṃbhajante pramoditāḥ te narendrāḥ surendrāśca chatropamāḥ sadā bhave  SvayambhuP mahatsukhāni bhuktvānte saṃprayānti jinālayaṃ ye cāsmiṃ sugatāvāse patākāḥ pañcaraṅgikāḥ  SvayambhuP samāvalaṃvayitvāpi saṃbhadrante mahotsavaiḥ te bhūtvātra mahīpālāḥ sadā devādhipā api  SvayambhuP bhadraśrīsatsukhaṃ bhuktvā saṃyātyante jinālayaṃ ye cāsmin vividhairvādyaiḥ saṃgītimurujādibhiḥ  SvayambhuP tauryai vaṃśādibhiścāpi saṃsevyante mahotsavaiḥ te manojñasvanādivyaśrīśrīśrīsadguṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP saddharmmasādhanaṃ kṛtvā vrajanti sugatālayaṃ salājākṣatapuṣpāṇi ye cāsmiṃ sugatālaye  SvayambhuP prakṣipya śraddhayā bhaktyā saṃbhajante samādarāt durgatinte na gacchanti saṃjātāḥ saṅgatau sadā  SvayambhuP sarvasattvahitaṃ kṛtvā saṃprayānti jinālayaṃ sadhātudravyaratnādi dakṣiṇānyatra ye mudā  SvayambhuP śraddhayā pariḍhaukitvā saṃbhajante sadādaraṃ divyaśrīsukhabhuṃjānā bhadraśrī sadguṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP sarvasattvahitaṃ kṛtvā saṃprayānti jinālaye ye cāpi stutibhistathyairenaṃ buddhālayaṃ mudā  SvayambhuP padyairgadyamayaiścāpi stutvā bhajanti sādaraṃ bahuratnasamṛddhāste sarvvavidyāvicakṣaṇāḥ  SvayambhuP bhūpāḥ svargādhipāścāpi bhūtvānte yānti saugataṃ śraddhayainaṃ jagannāthaṃ samāśrayaṃ svayambhūvaṃ  SvayambhuP natvāṣṭāṃgaiḥ prasannā ye saṃbhajante samādaraṃ saptaratnasametāste nṛpādhipā mahardhikāḥ  SvayambhuP saddharmmasādhanāraktā bhavanti bodhicāriṇaḥ ye cainaṃ caityarājendramanekaśaḥ pradakṣiṇāṃ  SvayambhuP kṛtvā dhyātvāpyanusmṛtvā nāmoccārya bhajantyapi jātismarāścirāyuṣkā matimantaḥ suvarṇṇinaḥ  SvayambhuP vandyāḥ pūjyāśca mānyāste bhaveyurbodhicāriṇaḥ śuddhāśca bhasmasaṃkṣālaiḥ samālipya samantataḥ  SvayambhuP samabhyarcyamahotsāhai ye bhajantyenamīśvaraṃ śokakleśāgnisaṃtāpavivarjitāścirāyuṣaḥ  SvayambhuP nīrogāḥ sukhino devā bhaveyu bhūmipāśca te ye ca nirmālyamākṛṣya śodhayitvātra sarvataḥ  SvayambhuP śramupāśritya sevyante sambuddhabhaktimānasāḥ nirmuktikleśaśokāste darśanīyāḥ śubhendriyāḥ  SvayambhuP śrīmantaḥ puṇḍarīkāsyā bhaveyurbodhicāriṇaḥ jīrṇe śīrṇe vibhagne smin pratisaṃskṛtya ye mudā  SvayambhuP pratiṣṭhāpya mahotsāhaiḥ saṃbhajante samādarāt sarvasampatsamṛddhāste puṣṭendriyā nirāmayāḥ  SvayambhuP dharmakāmāḥ śubhācārā bhaveyurbodhicāriṇaḥ jalpitvā yasya mantrāṇi dhāraṇīśca samāhitāḥ  SvayambhuP dhyātvā smṛtvā samuccārya nāmāpi prabhajanti ca te pi sarve mahāsattvāḥ pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrīsadguṇādhārā bhaveyurbodhicāriṇaḥ evaṃ mahattaraṃ puṇyamasmiṃ dharmmādhipālaye  SvayambhuP śraddhābhajanasaṃbhūtamityādiṣṭaṃ munīśvaraiḥ mayaitatpuṇyasaṃkṣiptamātraṃ tu kathyate dhunā  SvayambhuP samagraṃ vistarenātra samākhyātuṃ na śakyate evaṃ matvāsya satkārapūjāphalaṃ mahattaraṃ  SvayambhuP śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatvā kartavyaṃ bhajanaṃ sadā yepyasmiṃñcharaṇaṃ gatvā śraddhayā samupāśritāḥ  SvayambhuP suprasannāśayā bhaktyā bhajanti bodhimānasāḥ na te gacchanti kutrāpi durgatiṃ ca kadācana  SvayambhuP saṃjātāḥ sadgatiṣveva bhaveyurbodhicāriṇaḥ sadā te sukule jātā bodhisattvā vicakṣaṇāḥ  SvayambhuP sarvasattva hitā dhānaṃ careyurvratamābhavaṃ tataste bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP trividhāṃ bodhimāsādya nirvṛtipadamāpnuyuḥ na hicitta prasādaspa svalpābhavati dakṣiṇā  SvayambhuP tathāgateṣu saddharmma saṃbuddha śrāvakeṣvapi evaṃ hyacintyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ buddha dharmāśca nirmalāḥ  SvayambhuP acintyohi prasannānāṃ vipākaśca mahāphala evaṃ matvā triratneṣu bhaktipūjā phalaṃ mahat  SvayambhuP kāryābhaktiṣu sadātraiva dharmmadhātau jinālaye ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndrena śrutvā sarve samāśritāḥ  SvayambhuP lokāstatheti vijñapya prātyananda pravodhitāḥ iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutamayā tathocyate  SvayambhuP tvamapyevaṃ sadā rājan bhaja tatra jinālaye tatpuṇyena te bhadraṃ nirutpātaṃ sadābhavet  SvayambhuP bodhicitta rasaṃ ca saṃprāpya bodhisattvo bhaverapi tataḥ sambodhi saṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā tathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP mārānnirjjitya saṃbodhi prāpya buddhapadaṃ labheḥ iti śāstārhatā diṣṭaṃ samyakanarādhipaḥ  SvayambhuP aśokaḥ sasabhālokaḥ prābhyanandaṃ prabodhitaḥ iti śrī svayambhūtpatti kathāyā śrī svayambhū bhaṭṭārakoddeśa pūjāvarṇanā nāma dvītīyo dhyāya samāpta tṛtīya adhyāya mahāhradaśoṣaṇadharmadhātupadmagiri sampratiṣṭhāpanno nāmaathāśoko mahīpālaḥ sāñjaliḥpura āśritaḥ tamarhantaṃ yatiṃ natvā prārthayedevamādarāt  SvayambhuP bhadanta śrotumicchāmi tad bhūmi satkathāṃ tatsamyak samupādiśya saṃbodhayituṃ no bhavān  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthite rājñā so rhanyatirmahāmatiḥ upagupto narendraṃ taṃ sampaśyannevamādiśat  SvayambhuP sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi sarvalokābhivodhane  SvayambhuP tadyathātha mahāsattvo maitreyaḥ sa jinātmajaḥ bhagavantaṃ punarnatvā sāṃjalirevamabravīt  SvayambhuP bhagavannāvāsosaumahā jalāśrayo hradaḥ kadā bhūmi pradeśo tra kathaṃ jalāśrayo bhavet  SvayambhuP kasya ca samaye deśāgrāmādayaḥ pravarttitāḥ tatsarvaṃ samupādiśyansarvānasmānpravodhayan  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthite tena maitreyena saḥ sarvavit bhagavānstaṃ mahāsattvaṃ sampaśyannaivamādiśat  SvayambhuP sādhu śṛṇu mahāsattvaṃ yadatrābhūt mahītale tatpravṛttiṃ samākhyāmi sarvalokābhibodhane  SvayambhuP tadyathā bhūvilokānāṃ varṣa ṣaṣṭī sahasrakā purābhūt bhagavāñchāstā viśvabhūrnnāmasarvavit  SvayambhuP dharmarājo munīndro rhastathāgato vināyakaḥ sarva vidyādhipastāpī saṃbuddha sugato jinaḥ  SvayambhuP so nupamānāma pūryāṃ upakaṇṭhe jināśrame sarvasattva hitārthena vijahāra sasāṃdhikaḥ  SvayambhuP maitreyo haṃ tadā bhūvaṃ viśvabhū upāsakaḥ parvatākhyo mahāsattvo bodhisattvo hitārthabhṛt  SvayambhuP tatra sa bhagavāñchāstā saṃbhāsayaṃ sudhāśuvata saddharmma samupādeṣṭuṃ sabhāsane sabhāśrayat  SvayambhuP taṃ dṛṣṭā bhikṣavo sarve śrāvakāḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ pratyeka sugatāścāpi bodhisattvāścacailakāḥ  SvayambhuP bhikṣuṇyā brahmacāriṇyoyatayo yogino pica triratna bhajanāraktā upāsaka upāsikāḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ manyepi lokāśca saddharmma guṇalālasāḥ bhadraśrī sabhāṇāraktā saṃbuddha darśaṇotsukā  SvayambhuP tatsudharmmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ samatyena munīśvaraṃ yathākramaṃ samabhyarcya natvā sāñjalāya mudā  SvayambhuP parivṛtya puraskṛtya samudvikṣya samādarāt tatsabhāyāṃ samāśritya saṃniṣedu samāhitāḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ brahmādayaḥ sarve ṛṣayo brahmacāriṇaḥ tīrthikā api sarve tatsaddharmaṃ śrotumāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP śakrādayoyidāvāśca sarvalokādhipā api grahāstārāgaṇāḥ siddhāḥ sādhyā vidyādharā api  SvayambhuP sarve pi te sasāgatya bhagavantaṃ yathākramaṃ samabhyarcya praṇatvā tata sabhāyāṃ samupāśrayat  SvayambhuP evaṃ ca brāhmaṇā vijñā rājāna kṣatriyā api vaiśyāśca mantriṇo mātyā gṛhasthāśca mahājanāḥ  SvayambhuP śilpino vaṇijaścāpi sārthavāhāśca paurikāḥ grāmyā jānapadāścāpi tathā nye deśavāsinaḥ  SvayambhuP sarve te samupāgatya bhagavanta yathākramaṃ samabhyarcya praṇatvā ca kṛtvā pradakṣiṇānyapi  SvayambhuP guru kṛtya puraskṛtya parivṛtya samantataḥ tatsadharmmāmṛtaṃ pātumupatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  SvayambhuP tāndṛṣṭvā samupāsīnān viśvabhūrbhagavāṃjinaḥ ādi madhyānta kalyāṇaṃ saddharma samupādiśat  SvayambhuP tatsaddharmmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ sabhāśritāḥ dharmmaviśeṣamājñāya prāpyananda pravodhitāḥ  SvayambhuP tasminkṣaṇe mahī sarvā ca cāraddhi saparvatāḥ suprasannā diśaḥ sarvā rejuravīndra vahnyaḥ  SvayambhuP suradundubhayo nendurnipetuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭayaḥ nirutpātaṃ mahotsāhaṃ prāvarttata samantataḥ  SvayambhuP tad vilokya sabhālokāḥ sarve te vismayānvitāḥ śrotuṃ taddhetu sarvajñamudvīkṣya tasthurāditāḥ  SvayambhuP tadā gaganagañjākhyo bodhisattvaḥ samutthitaḥ uddhahannuttarāsaṃga purataḥ samupāśrita  SvayambhuP sarvajñaṃ taṃ mahābhijñaṃ dharmmarājaṃ vināyakaṃ viśvabhuvaṃ muninnatvā sāṃjalirevamabravīt  SvayambhuP bhagavantadranaimityaṃ kasyedaṃ jāyate dhunā tadbhavānsamupādiśya saṃbodhayatu no guroḥ  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavānsa munīśvaraḥ gaganagaṃjamālokya taṃ sabhācaivamabravīt  SvayambhuP kulaputra mahad bhadra nimittamidamācarat tadahaṃ sapravakṣāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ yūyamādarāt  SvayambhuP tadyathā triguṇābhijñā mañjuśrīḥ sugatātmajaḥ uttarasyāṃ mahācīne viharati nagāśrame  SvayambhuP tasya bhāryā ubhejyeṣṭākeśinī śrīvarapradā vidyā sadguṇa saṃbhartrī dvitīyāḥ copakeśinī  SvayambhuP ekasmin samaye tatra maṃjuśrīḥ sadguṇodadhiḥ lokaṃ saṃdarśana nāma samādhiṃ vidadhe mudā  SvayambhuP dhyāna dṛṣṭā dadarśātra mahāhradasaroruhe ratnamayaṃ samutpannaṃ dharmmadhātuṃ jinālayaṃ  SvayambhuP svayaṃbhuvaṃ tamālokya maṃjudevaṃ susanmatiḥ saṃharṣitaḥ purnadhyātvā manasaivaṃ vyacintayet  SvayambhuP aho svayaṃ samudbhūto dharmmadhātu jinālayaḥ nirjane jalamaye jyotirūpaḥ saṃbhāṣayan sthitaḥ  SvayambhuP tat tathāhaṃ kariṣyāmi gatvā tatra mahāhrade śoṣayitvā tadambhānsi yathā pṛthvītalo bhavat  SvayambhuP tadā tatra mahībhūtre nirjale supratiṣṭhite śiloccaye pratiṣṭhāpya bhajiṣyāmi tamīśvaraṃ  SvayambhuP tathā tatra mahībhūte grāmādi vasatirbhaveta tadā sarve pi lokāśyaḥ bhajeyustaṃ jinālayaṃ  SvayambhuP tathā tat puṇya bhāvena sarvadā tatra maṃgalaṃ nirutpātaṃ bhavennūnaṃ lokāśca syūḥ subhāvinaḥ  SvayambhuP tataste mānavāḥ sarve tasyaiva śaraṇāśritāḥ yathāśakti mahotsāhaiḥ prabhajeyuḥ sadā mudā  SvayambhuP tatastatpuṇyaśuddhāste saddharma guṇalālasāḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvāścareyurbodhisaṃvaraṃ  SvayambhuP tataste bodhisaṃbhāraṃ purayitvā yathākramaṃ trividhāṃ vidhimāsādya nivṛtipadamāpnuyuḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ kṛtvā mahatpuṇyaṃ prāpyāhaṃ trijagatsvapi kṛtvā dharmmamayaṃ bodhiprāpya nivṛttipadamāpnuyāṃ  SvayambhuP iti dhyātvā viniścitya mañjuśrīḥ sajinātmajaḥ mañjudevābhidhācāryarūpaṃ dhṛtvā maharddhimān  SvayambhuP keśinī varadā nāma mokṣadākhyo pakeśinī bhūtvānekaiḥ mahāsattvaiḥ sahasarve pinecarat  SvayambhuP tataścaran sabhāryāsau mañjudevaḥ sasāṃdhikaḥ sarvatra bhadratāṃ kṛtvā mahotsārhaiḥ samācarat  SvayambhuP tatra te samupāgatya dūrataḥ saṃprabhāsvaraṃ mahāhradāvjamadhyasthaṃ dadṛśustaṃ jinālayaṃ  SvayambhuP tatra te taṃ samālokya jyotirūpaṃ samujvalaṃ praṇatvā sahasopetyaḥ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāni ca  SvayambhuP tattīre parvate ramye sarve pi te samāśritāḥ taṃ caityameva saṃvīkṣya nyavasanta pramoditāḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ prātaḥ samutthāya mañjudevaḥ sa ṛddhimān bhaktayā paramayāstauṣijjinālayaṃ svayaṃbhuvaṃ  SvayambhuP jyotirūpāya caitanyarūpāya bhavate namaḥ anādi nidhanāya śrīdātre praṇavarūpiṇe  SvayambhuP viśvatomukha rūpāya svāhāsvadhārūpiṇe pṛthvyādibhūtanirmātre mahāmahasvarūpiṇe  SvayambhuP jagatsraṣṭe jagatpātre jagad dhartre namo namaḥ jagat vaṃdyāya jagatamārādhāya ca te namaḥ  SvayambhuP atisthūlāya sūkṣmāya vikārāya vikāriṇe nirākṛtikṛte tubhyaṃ saccidānaṃdamūrttayai  SvayambhuP vaṣaṭkāra svarūpāya hutabhuje svayaṃ namaḥ hotre havana rūpāya homadravyāya te namaḥ  SvayambhuP bhaktilabhyāya somyāya bhaktavatsalāya te namaḥ dhyānagamyāya dhyeyāya catuvargapradāyine  SvayambhuP agraratnāya niḥsīmamahimne sarvadā namaḥ guṇātītāya yogāya yogine ca sadā namaḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ stutvā mañjudevaḥ punaḥ kṣamārthatāṃ vyadhāt prasīda bhagavan yadahaṃ hadaṃ saṃśoṣituṃ yate  SvayambhuP ityuktvā candrahāsaṃ sa sajjīkṛtya samaṃ tataḥ tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samantato vyalokayat  SvayambhuP vilokya sa mahāsattvo yāmya diśāvṛtaṃ nagaṃ candrahāsena khaḍgena chitvā jalāśrayaṃ vyadhāt  SvayambhuP tacchinnaśailamārgeṇa tajjalāni samantataḥ pranirgatyāśu sarvāṇi gaṃgāsaṃgamamāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP tadārabhya nadā nadyo babhūvurbhūtale hradāḥ digvidikṣu malāṃbhobhistad dvīpaiḥ paripūritāḥ  SvayambhuP tatra nirudhya ye mvuni yatra ye śilāḥ sthitāḥ tatra tatra satānsarvāśchitvā svūnica cārayet  SvayambhuP evaṃ sa sarvataḥ chitvā kṛtvā tajjalanirgamaṃ trirātreṇāpi na jalāni sarvāṇi niracārayet  SvayambhuP tajjalā dhānamekantu hradaṃ dhanādahābhidhaṃ karkkoṭakanāgasya samasthāpa yadāśramaṃ  SvayambhuP siṃhenopadrutā yad vada gajendrobhaya vihvalāḥ mahārāvai rudanto vai vidravanto diśo daśaḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ tajjalasaṃghātaścandrahāsāsichedanāt mārgāntarānniragamata paṃkaśeṣaṃ yathābhavat  SvayambhuP tajjalādhānamekentu hradaṃ dharādrahābhidhaṃ karkkotakasya nāgasya samasthāpayadāśrayaṃ  SvayambhuP tatastasmin jale śuṣkeyadādhārasaroruhaṃ tadeva parvatābhūya dharmadhātorvyavasthitaḥ  SvayambhuP mañjudevānubhāvena sa sarvaparvatoktamaḥ abhedyā vajravaktena vajrakūṭa iti smṛtaḥ  SvayambhuP tadāsau bhūtaloramyaḥ samantato nagāvṛtaḥ upachandoha ityākhyā himāla yo picocyate  SvayambhuP sudurjayā svarūpābhūḥ prajñā jñānānubhāvinī herukamaṇḍalākārā bhūtvā samavatiṣṭhate  SvayambhuP tatrāpi ca pradhānā śrī mahādevī khagānanā dharmmodayā samuhutā saṃtiṣṭhate jagaddhite  SvayambhuP taṃ dṛṣṭvā sa mahācaryā mañjudevo maharddhimāna bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ pratyatyānandito bhavat  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa tāṃ mahādevī samālokya pramoditaḥ urasā śirasā dṛṣṭayā vacasā manasā tathā  SvayambhuP padbhyāṃ karābhyāṃ jānubhyāṃ aṣṭāṃgo pi iti smṛtaḥ aṣṭāṃgai praṇītā kṛtvā sāṃjaliḥ samupāśrayan  SvayambhuP suprasanna mukhāmbhojaḥ suprabuddho śayāmbujaḥ saṃpaśyastāṃ mahādevīṃ stotrairevaṃ mudābhajaṃ  SvayambhuP bhagavati mahādevī bhavatyāḥ śaraṇaṃ vraje vande pādāmvuje nityaṃ bhajāmi tanprasīdatu  SvayambhuP jananī sarvabuddhānāṃ tvameva bodhidāyinī sarveṣāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mātāhitānupālinī  SvayambhuP sarvahitārtha saṃbhakti sarvapāpaviśodhanī duṣṭa māragaṇākṣobha mahānanda sukhapradā  SvayambhuP saddharmmasādhanotsāhavalavīrya guṇapradā niḥkleśastimitedhyāna samādhi sukhadāyinī  SvayambhuP prajñāguṇa mahāratna śrī samṛddhi pradāyinī tad bhaktyāḥ padāmbhoja śaraṇastho bhajāmyaham  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthya sa prājño mañjudeva sa samvarī tasyā bhaktī prasannātmā samārādhitumaicchat  SvayambhuP atha tatra sa ācāryaḥ sagaṇaḥ saṃpramoditaḥ mārga śīrṣaiśitaiḥ pakṣai navamyāṃ ravivāsare  SvayambhuP prātaḥ snātvā viśuddhātmā śucivastrāvṛtaḥ sudhīḥ poṣadhasamvaraṃ dhṛtvā devīmārādhayaṃ sthitaḥ  SvayambhuP rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kṛtvā dhāraṇī mantrajalpanaiḥ stutibhiśca samārādhyaṃ prābhajatāṃ jineśvarīṃ  SvayambhuP tataḥ prātaḥ daśamyāṃ sa snātvā gandhodakairmudā datvā dānaṃ yathākāmaṃ pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalaḥ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhisamabhyarcya tāṃ devīṃ parameśvarīṃ mahotsāhaiḥ stutiṃ kṛtvā tridhā pradakṣiṇāni ca  SvayambhuP suprasanna mukhāmbhojaḥ saddharmaguṇamānasaḥ bhūyo ṣṭāṃgaiḥ praṇatvaivaṃ prārthayātsāṃjalimudrā  SvayambhuP prasīdatu jaganmātarbhavatyāḥ samupāśritaḥ saṃbodhi sādhanotsau bhajāmi sarvadā mudāṃ  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthya saṃprājñau natvāṣṭāṃgairmudā ca tāṃ tatpadmāmṛtamādāya tridhyamañjulinā pivet  SvayambhuP tadamṛtaṃ nipīyāsau saṃviśuddhatrimaṇḍalaṃ aṣṭākṣaṇavinirmuktaḥ saṃbuddhakṣaṇamāpnuvān  SvayambhuP evaṃ kṛtvā sa ācārya devyā bhaktiparāyaṇaḥ saṃbuddhakṣaṇamāsādya sarva dharmmādhipo bhavat  SvayambhuP tataḥ śrīmān sa ācāryo bodhisattva jagaddhite sa saṃghānyavasat tatra dharmadhātaurūpāśramaiḥ  SvayambhuP tatsamabhyaṣitatvāt saṃpradeśaḥ śrī manoharaḥ syātsarvatrāpi mañjuśrīparvata iti viśrutaḥ  SvayambhuP tatra śritaḥ sadāpyaspa dharmmadhātorūpāsakaḥ sarvasattva hitārthena prābhajansa jinātmajaḥ  SvayambhuP tatsamīkṣāmalā sarvebrahmendrapramukhāapi sarvelokādhipāścāpi mudā tatra samāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP tatraivo poṣaḍhaṃ dhṛtvā kṛtvā jāgaraṇaṃ niśi uṣitvā dhāraṇī mantraḥ dhyātvā tāṃ śrī jineśvarīṃ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāni ca kṛtvāṣṭāṃga praṇāmāni stutibhiścā bhajaṃ mudā  SvayambhuP evaṃ tasyāmahādevyāḥ sarve tai śaraṇāśritāḥ dharmaśrīguṇasaṃpatti maharddhisiddhimāpnuvan  SvayambhuP tataste cāmarāḥ sarve sendra brahmādayādhipāḥ vajrakūṭaṃ nagāvjaṃ taṃ samīkṣyante jinālayaṃ  SvayambhuP anumodyābhinandante stasyāpi śaraṇe gatāḥ mahotsāhaiḥ samabhyarcya prabhajanta samādaraṃ  SvayambhuP tataḥ sarve marāstaica sarvailokādhipāśca te asyāpi mañjuedevasya vajrācāryasya sadguroḥ  SvayambhuP śaraṇe samupāsṛtya divya pūjopahārakaiḥ samabhyarcya mahotsāhaiḥ prābhajanta pramoditāḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ manvādayaḥ sarve manuyopiyaḥmaharṣayaḥ yatayoginaścāpi bhikṣavo brahmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP cailakā bodhisattvāśca mahāsattvā jinātmajāḥ te sarve samupāgatya tasyā devyā upāsakāḥ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya prābhajanta pramoditāḥ tataste dharmmadhātauśca sarve pi śaraṇāśritāḥ  SvayambhuP samabhyarcya mahotsāhaiḥ natvā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ suprasanna mukhāmbhojānta pramoditanaḥ  SvayambhuP tataste ca mahāsattva mañjudevaṃ mahaddhiṃkim ācārya samutsāhaiḥ samarcayaṃ pramoditāḥ  SvayambhuP pratyeka sugatāścāpi sarve tatra samāgatāḥ tāṃ devī dharmmadhātuṃ tamācāryaṃ ca samārcayaṃ  SvayambhuP sarve tathāgatāścāpi pūjāmeghasarjanaiḥ tāṃ devīṃ dharmadhātuṃ tamācāryaṃ ca samācaryaṃ  SvayambhuP evaṃmanyepi lokāśca praduṣṭvā samupāgatāḥ tāṃ devīṃ dharmadhātuṃ ca tamācāryaṃ ca prābhajan  SvayambhuP etatpuṇyānubhāvena calitā sāvdhinagā mahī puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ śubhotsāhaṃ pravarttate samantataḥ  SvayambhuP ityādiṣṭa munīndreṇa viśvabhūvā niśamyate sarve samāśritā lokā vismayaṃ samupāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ sarve pi te lokāstāṃ devīṃ śrīmaheśvarī dharmmadhātutamācāryaṃ draṣṭumabhiva vāñchire  SvayambhuP tadāśayaṃ parijñāyaḥ gagaṇagañja utthitaḥ bhagavantantamānaspaśyannevamavravīt  SvayambhuP bhagavan sarvamicchanti draṣṭuṃ tāṃ sugeśvarīṃ dharmmadhātuṃ tamācāryaṃ tadanujñāṃ dadātu naḥ  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena bhagavānsa munīśvaraḥ gagaṇagañjamātmajña taṃ paśyannevamādiśat  SvayambhuP sādhu sādhyāmahādevīṃ khagānanājineśvarīṃ dharmadhātuṃ tamācāryamapirdaṣṭuṃ yadīcchatha  SvayambhuP tatra himālaye gatvā tāṃ śrī devīṃ khagānanāṃ dharmadhātuṃ tamācāryaṃ saṃbhajadhvaṃ yathā vidhi  SvayambhuP ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa viśvabhuvā niśamyate sarve lokā mahotsāhai ratrāyayuḥ pramoditāḥ  SvayambhuP ahamapi munīndrasya prāpyānujñāṃ pramoditaḥ taiḥsārddhaṃ prasthitau dūrātpaśyannimaṃmāyayau  SvayambhuP atra prāpno haṃ samālokya dharmmadhātunnimaṃ mudā samabhyarcya mahotsāhaistai lokaiḥ prābhajaṃ saha  SvayambhuP śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatvā kṛtvā cainaṃ pradakṣiṇāṃ stutvāṣṭāṃgaiḥ praṇatvā ca prārthayaṃ bodhisamvaraṃ  SvayambhuP tato haṃ mañjudevākhyaṃ tamācārya samīkṣya ca samabhyarcya mahotsāhaiḥ prābhajadhvaṃ sahānujaiḥ  SvayambhuP tatastasyopadeśa tāṃ śrīdevīṃ khagānanāṃ yathāvidhi samārādhya mahotsāhaiḥ samarcayaṃ  SvayambhuP kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ cāpi natvāṣṭāṅgaiḥ pramoditaḥ stutvā dhyātvā ca saṃbodhiṃ saṃprārthaya jagaddhite  SvayambhuP etatpuṇyānubhāvena pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ aṣṭākṣaṇa vinirmukto bodhisattvo bhavaṃ kṛtī  SvayambhuP tataḥ sambodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ jitvā māragaṇān arhan kalāvapi jinobhave  SvayambhuP evamasyā mahādevyāḥ ye ye śaraṇa āśritāḥ yathāvidhi samārādhya bhajeyu bodhimānasāḥ  SvayambhuP te te sarve mahāsattvāḥ pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ bodhisattvā mahābhijñā bhaveyu striguṇādhipāḥ  SvayambhuP kutrāpi te nagacchet durggatiñca kadācana sadāsaṅgatisaṃjāta bhaveyuḥ śrī guṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP yathābhivācchitaṃ dravyaṃ datvārthibhyo samādarāt yathākāmaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā sañcarerañjagaddhite  SvayambhuP tato viśuddhaśīlāste caturbrahma vihāriṇaḥ bodhisattvasamvaramādhāya saṃcareran sadā śubhe  SvayambhuP tataste syu rmahāsattvāḥ saddharmma sukhalālasāḥ svaparātmahitādhārakṣāntivratasamāratāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste sadguṇādhārā vīryavanto vicakṣaṇāḥ saddharmma sādhanodyuktā bhaveyu striguṇādhipāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste sudhiyo dhīrā niḥkleśā vijitendriyāḥ samādhi guṇasampannā bhaveyubodhiyoginaḥ  SvayambhuP tataste vimalātmānaḥ sarvavidyā guṇādhipāḥ prajñāśrī ratna saṃprāpto bhaveyuḥ sugatātmajāḥ  SvayambhuP tataśca te sahāsattvāḥ sarve sattvā hitotsukāḥ sarvāpāya vidhi prājñā bhaveyuśtriguṇādhipāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste bodhisaṃbhāra praṇidhiratnasāgarāḥ sarvasattvahitaṃ kṛtvā saṃcareraṃ sadāśubhe  SvayambhuP tataśca te mahābhijñāḥ bhadraśrī satguṇānvitāḥ valiṣṭhā duṣṭa jetāro bhaveyu stribhaveśvarāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste trividhāṃ bodhimāsādya bhadracāriṇaḥ sambodhijñānasadrantasamṛddhāḥ syu rmunīśvarāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste sugatāḥ buddhāḥ daśabhūmīśvarājināḥ bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya kūryuḥ sarvānsudharmmiṇaḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ dharmamayaṃ kṛtvā sarvatra bhuvaneṣvapi sunivṛrtipadaṃ prāpya saṃprayāyurjinālayaṃ  SvayambhuP evamasyā mahādevyā bhajano hūtamuktamaṃ puṇyaṃ mahattaraṃ siddhaṃ sambuddhapadasādhanaṃ  SvayambhuP iti satyaṃ samākhyātaṃ sarvai rapi munīśvaraiḥ vijñāyāsyā mahādevyā bhajadhvaṃ śaraṇe sthitā  SvayambhuP asyāpi dharma dhātauśca bhajanodbhūtamuktamaṃ puṇyaṃ mahattaraṃ siddhaṃ sambuddhapadasādhanaṃ  SvayambhuP asyāpi mañjudevasyaḥ bhajanod bhūtamuktamaṃ puṇyaṃ mahattaraṃ siddhaṃ sambuddhapadasādhanaṃ  SvayambhuP matveti yadi vo vāṃcchā vidyate saugate pade sarve yūyaṃ samādhāya bhajatāntra jinālaye  SvayambhuP khagānanāsyāyā mahādevyāḥ śaraṇe ca samāśritāḥ dhyātvā smṛtvā samuccārya nāmāpi bhajatābhavaṃ  SvayambhuP ya eṣāṃ śaraṇe sthitvā dhyātvā smṛtvā samāhitāḥ nāmāpi samudāhṛtya bhajanti sarvadābhave  SvayambhuP te sabhadrā nagacchanti durggatiṃ ca kadācana sadā sadgati saṃjātā bhaveyuḥ śrī guṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvā saddharma bodhi cāriṇaḥ sarvasattva hitodyuktā bhaveyuḥ sugatātmajāḥ  SvayambhuP evanteṣāṃ mahatsaukhyaṃ bhadraśrī sadguṇānvitaṃ sarvadāpi nirutpātaṃ pravarktate samāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP daivotpātabhayanteṣāṃta vidyate samantataḥ yaktāndṛṣṭvā surāḥ sarve rakṣantīndrādayomudā  SvayambhuP agnyutpātaṃbhayaṃ teṣāṃ vidyate na kadācana yat tāndṛṣṭvā prasīdanto rakṣeyurvahnayaḥ sadā  SvayambhuP akāla maraṇād bhītisteṣānnavidyate kvacit yadyamopi samalokya rakṣati tāṃ prasāditaḥ  SvayambhuP rākṣasasyābhayaṃ teṣāṃ vidyate na samantataḥ yad vāyavo pi tā vījya rakṣeyuḥ sarvadānugāḥ  SvayambhuP yakṣasyāpi bhayaṃ teṣāṃ vidyate na sadā kvacit yakṣā samīkṣya rakṣeyuḥ sarve yakṣādhipā api  SvayambhuP bhūtebhyo pi bhayanteṣāṃ vidyate na samantataḥ yadīśānopi tānpaśya saṃrakṣetsaṃpramoditāḥ  SvayambhuP gandharvotpati to bhītisteṣānnavidyate kvacit dhṛtarāṣṭo pi tānpaśyat saṃrakṣetsaṃ prasāditaḥ  SvayambhuP kumbhāṇḍebhyo pi nāstyevaṃ bhayanteṣāṃ kadācana viruḍhakohitān paśyanabhirakṣan prasādataḥ  SvayambhuP nāgebhyo pi bhayanteṣāṃ vidyate na sadā kvacita virupākṣo hi samyaśyantānrakṣansamprasāditaḥ  SvayambhuP yakṣebhyo pi sadā teṣāṃ vidyate na bhayaṃ kvacita kuvero hi samālokya saṃrakṣastān prasāditaḥ  SvayambhuP bhayaṃ na kinnarebhyopi teṣāmasti kadācana drumo hitān mahāsattvā saṃvīkṣavat prasāditaḥ  SvayambhuP guhyakebhyopi nāstyeva bhayanteṣāṃ sudharmmaṇāṃ vajrapāṇirhitānvīkṣya prasāditā bhavet sadā  SvayambhuP tathā vidyādharebhyo pi bhayanteṣānna vidyate yataḥ sarvārthasiddho pi samyaśyanstān vetsadā  SvayambhuP grahotpāta bhayanteṣāṃ vidyate na kadācana grahādhipāhi sarve pi samīkṣya tānavetsadā  SvayambhuP tathā tārāgaṇotpātabhayaṃ teṣānnavidyate sarvāstā rāhi tānvīkṣya sarvatrā veyurābhavaṃ  SvayambhuP siddhāḥ sādhyāścarudrāśca vīkṣyāveyuḥ sadāpi tān tattebhyopi bhayaṃ kvāpi teṣāṃ nāsti kadācana  SvayambhuP tathā ca mātṛkotpātaṃ bhayaṃ nāsti kadācana sarvāhi mātṛkān dṛṣṭvā rakṣeyu stāṃ prasāditāḥ  SvayambhuP mahākālo gaṇeśa skandaśca bhairavā api sarvadā tānsamālokya rakṣeyuḥ saṃprasāditāḥ  SvayambhuP pretā bhūtāḥ piśāścāśca vetāḍā ḍākinīgaṇāḥ api tānsarvadālokya saṃrakṣeyuḥ prasāditāḥ  SvayambhuP tebhyo pi bhayanteṣāṃ vidyate na kadācana sarve pi rtesahāyāḥ syu saṃvodhi dharmmasādhane  SvayambhuP siṃhādi sarvajantubhyoḥ pakṣibhyo pi samantataḥ sarpādi kṛmikīṭebhyo bhayanteṣāṃ sadāpi na  SvayambhuP duṣṭa pratyarthikebhyo pi taskarebhyopi sarvataḥ śatrubhyo pi bhayanteṣāṃ vidyate na samantataḥ  SvayambhuP yadetatpuṇyaliptāstāṃ samīkṣya te prasāditāḥ sarve maitrī kṛpā sneha nivaddhāḥ syuhitārthinaḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ sarve pi satvāstāndṛṣṭvā saṃprasāditāḥ snigdhaciktāprasannāsyāḥ paśyeyu maitrībhāvataḥ  SvayambhuP rājāno pi ca tāndṛṣṭvā maitrī snehasabhāvitāḥ suprasannāśayāḥ prītā mānayeyuḥ sadā mudā  SvayambhuP mantrīṇo pi sadā teṣāṃ maitrīsneha sabhāṣitāḥ mānayeyuḥyathākāmaṃ saddharmma vratasādhanaṃ  SvayambhuP brāmhaṇā api sarve ca teṣāṃ saddharmma sādhanaṃ dṛṣṭvānumoditātmāno dadhu bhadrāśivaṃ sadā  SvayambhuP ṛṣayo pi tathā sarve tāṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃprasāditāḥ paśyantaḥ kṛpayā dṛṣṭvā modayeyuḥ subhāśiṣā  SvayambhuP evaṃ ca yoginaḥ siddhā yatayo bramhacāriṇaḥ tīrthikāstāpasāścāpi vratinaścāpyupāsakāḥ  SvayambhuP cairakā bhikṣavoścāpi bhikṣuṇyaścāpyupāsikāḥ api tāṃ sudṛśālokya nandayeyuḥ śubhāśiṣāḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ ca śrāvakāḥ sarve pratyeka sugatā api bodhisatvāśca sarve pi tān dṛṣṭvā saṃprasāditāḥ  SvayambhuP kṛpayā dṛṣṭavānupaśyanto maitrī snehasubhāvinaḥ rakṣitvā bodhimārgeṣu niyājeyuḥ sadā bhavaṃ  SvayambhuP evaṃ sarve pi saṃbuddhā dṛṣṭvā tāṃ saṃprasāditāḥ sarvadā kṛpayā rakṣyucārayeyurjjagaddhite  SvayambhuP evaṃ teṣāṃ mahatpuṇyaṃ sambuddha padasādhanaṃ bhadraśrīguṇasaṃpatti samṛddhi siddhisaṃpradaṃ  SvayambhuP evaṃ yūyamapi jñātvā sarvadā śaraṇāśritāḥ yathāśakti samabhyarcya bhajataitāṃstriratnikān  SvayambhuP smṛtvā dhyātvāpi nāmāpi samuccārya sadā mudā eṣāmeva triratnānāṃ bhajadhvaṃ śaraṇe sthitā  SvayambhuP etatpuṇyaviliptā ye pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ bhadraśrīguṇasaṃpannā bhaveste śubhāśayā  SvayambhuP durgatiṃ te na gaccheyuḥ sadā sadgatisaṃbhavāḥ bodhisatvā mahāsatvā bhaveryubhadracāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP tataste sarvasatvānāṃ hitārtha sādhanodyatāḥ sudhīrā bodhisambhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP tato māragaṇāñjitvā niḥkleśā vijitendriyāḥ arhanta trividhāṃ bodhiṃprāpya yāyu jinālayaṃ  SvayambhuP etsarva mayā khyātaṃ sarvairapi munīśvaraiḥ śrutvānumodanāṃ kṛtvā pracaradhvaṃ sadāśubhe  SvayambhuP ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa niśamyate sabhāśritāḥ sarve tathānumodantaḥ prāpyānandatpravodhitāḥ  SvayambhuP iti śrī svayambhūtpattisamuddeśa mahāhrada śoṣaṇa dharmmadhātu padmagirisaṃprasthāpano nāma tṛtīyo dhyāyaḥ caturtha adhyāyaḥ śrīsvayambhūcaityasamutpattikathā vītarāgatīrtharāṣṭrapravartano nāmaathāsautha mahāsattva maitreya sugatātmajaḥ bhagavantantamānaṃmya prāhaivaṃ sāñjalimudrā  SvayambhuP kadātra bhagavān grāma nagarapaṅaktādayaḥ pravarttitā mahārāṣṭrāḥ tatsamādeṣṭumarhati  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthite tena maitreyena niśasya sa bhagavāntaṃ mahābhijñaṃ samālokyaivamādiśat  SvayambhuP sādhu śṛṇu mahāsattva maitreya tvaṃ samāhitaḥ tatkālaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yadātra vasatirabhūt  SvayambhuP yadāyuṣnṛṇāṃ varṣacatvāriśatsahasrake dharmmarājo jagannāthaḥ krakuchando munīśvaraḥ  SvayambhuP sarva vidyādhipaḥ śāstā traidhātuka vināyakaḥ sarvajño ha mābhijñestathāgato jino bhavat  SvayambhuP ma saṃbuddhā jagallokahitārthena sasāṃdhikaḥ kṣemāvatyā mahāpuryyādupārāme manorame  SvayambhuP vihāre saugatāvāse saddharmmasamupādiśat ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ vijahāra prabhāsayan  SvayambhuP tadā saṃbodhisattvo haṃ jyotipālābhidhaḥ sudhīḥ śāstārantaṃ krakucchandaṃ samārādhya sadābhajaṃ  SvayambhuP tadā sa bhagavāñchāstā krakucchando jagaddhite janapadeṣu saddharmmaṃ samupādeṣṭumaicchataḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa bhagavān śāstā sarvasaṃghaiḥ samanvitaḥ sarvatra bhadratāṃ kṛtvā saṃbhāṣayansamācarat  SvayambhuP evaṃ sa sañcarañchāstā sarvatra dharmmamādiśat krameṇehasamātaḥ sandadarśa samantataḥ  SvayambhuP dṛṣṭvemaṃ dharmmadhātuṃ saṃprajvalita jinālayaṃ sasaṃgha samupāśritya prābhajadvidhinā mudā  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa prasthitotraiva śaṃkhabhidhe śilāccayaṃ mahachuddhaśilāyāṃ ca vijahāra sa sāṃdhikaḥ  SvayambhuP tatra taṃtri jagannāthaṃ krakuchando munīśvaraṃ sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaiḥ puraskṛtaṃ  SvayambhuP samālokya mahāsattvā jinātmajāḥ tatsaddharmmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ saṃharṣitāḥ samāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP bhikṣuṇyāpi śuśīlādyā ścailakāścāpyupāsakāḥ cailakā vratinaścāpi sarve upāsikā api  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvā saddharmma guṇalālasāḥ tatsaddharmmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve te samupāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP bhagavantantaṃ samabhyarcya kṛtvā pradakṣiṇānyapi natvā sāṃjalayastatra paśyantaḥ samupāśrayan  SvayambhuP tathā brahmādayaścāpi maharṣayastapasvinaḥ yatayo yoginaścāpi munayo brahmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ śakrādayo davāḥ sarve lokādhipā api grahāstārāgaṇāḥ siddhāsādhyā vidyādharā api  SvayambhuP gandharvā kinnarā yakṣā guhyakā rākṣasā api dānavā garuḍā nāgāstathānyeha samāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP bhagavantaṃ sasaṃghantaṃ samabhyarcya pramoditāḥ natvā dharmmāmṛtaṃ pātumupatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ ca brāhmaṇā vijñā rājānaḥ kṣatriyā api vaiśyāśca mantriṇo mātyāḥ sainyā bhṛtyā janānyapi  SvayambhuP gṛhasthe dhaninaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ sādhavaśca mahājanāḥ śilpino vanijaścāpi sārthavāhaśca paurikāḥ  SvayambhuP prajā jānapadāśrāmyāḥ kārpaṭikāśca śailikāḥ evaṃmanye pi lokāścasarvadigbhyaḥ samāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP bhagavantantamālokya praṇatvā samupāgatāḥ yathākramaṃ samabhyarcya kṛtvā pradakṣiṇānyapi  SvayambhuP kṛtvāṣṭāṃga praṇāmañca kṛtāṃjali puṭo mudā tatsaddharmmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ tatsabhāyāṃ samantataḥ  SvayambhuP parivṛtya puraskṛtya samāśritya samāhitāḥ gurukṛtya munīndrantaṃ samudvīkṣya niṣedire  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa bhagavāndṛṣṭvā sarvāstānsamupasthitān āryasatyaṃ samālakṣya saddharmmaṃ samupādiśat  SvayambhuP tatsaddharmmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve pi te pravodhitāḥ bodhicaryā vrataṃ dhartuṃ samecchanta prasāditāḥ  SvayambhuP tadāśayaṃ parijñāya bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ bodhisattvātma mārmetyaḥ sampaśyannevamādiśat  SvayambhuP kulaputra mudāyepi śraddhayā saugatevṛṣe pravrajituṃ samīcchanti tatra pravrajitādritāḥ  SvayambhuP atra ye hyupachando ha sarva dharmmārthasiddhide pravrajyā śāsane bauddhe caranti bodhisaṃvaraṃ  SvayambhuP te sarve pātakā muktāḥ pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ niḥkleśā vimalātmāno bodhisattvā jitendriyāḥ  SvayambhuP jitvā māragaṇānduṣṭān hantā brahmacāriṇaḥ trividhāmbodhimāsādya sambuddhapadamāpnuyuḥ  SvayambhuP iti matvātra saṃsāre ye vāṃchanti sunirvṛtiṃ tatra pravrajyā sānbauddhaṃ carantu śraddhayā vrataṃ  SvayambhuP ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa niśamya te pravodhitāḥ sabhāsīnā mahāsattvāḥ pravrajintu samīchire  SvayambhuP tato guṇadhvajādīnāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ catuḥśataṃ tathā bhayaṃ dadānāma kṣatriyāṇāṃśatatrayaṃ  SvayambhuP tathāneka mahāsattvā vaiśyāśūdrāśca sajjanāḥ sarve pi suprasannāste pravrajituṃ samīcchire  SvayambhuP tataste sarva utthāya sāñjalayaḥ purāgatāḥ bhagavantaṃ tamānamya prārthayannevamādarāt  SvayambhuP bhagavannātha sarvajña dhṛtvājñā bhavatāṃ vayaṃ pravrajyaśāsana bauddhecartumichāmahe vrataṃ  SvayambhuP bhagavansta bhavānasmān sarvān paśyan kṛpā dṛśā samanvāgatya saddharmma niyojayitumarhati  SvayambhuP iti taiḥ prārthite sarvairbhagavānsa munīśvaraḥ sarvānstān sanmatin paśyan samāmanbhyaivamādiśat  SvayambhuP yadyatra saugate dharmma pravrajituṃ samīcchatha etat pravrajya sarvatra caradhvaṃ saugataṃ vrataṃ  SvayambhuP ityādiśya sa saṃbuddhaḥ pāṇinā tacchiraḥspṛśan tānsarvānsaugate dharme samanvāharadādarāt  SvayambhuP tato vatārya te keśān rakta cīvara prāvṛtāḥ khikhirī pātramādhāya sarve pi bhikṣuvo bhavan  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa bhagavāntebhyoḥ yatibhyo saṃmyak saṃbodhipākṣikān saddharmmānsamupādiśya pradadau bodhisamvaraṃ  SvayambhuP tataste vimalātmāno niḥkleśā vimalendriyāḥ satkāraṃ lābha niḥkāṃkṣā vītasaṃgā niraṃjanāḥ  SvayambhuP svaparātma samācārāḥ saṃsāragatiniḥspṛhāḥ māracaryā nirāsaktāḥ samaloṣṭa suvarṇṇikāḥ  SvayambhuP kleśā nirmalātmāno pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ arhanta bhadrakā cārā babhubu brahmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP tatassarve pi te bauddhā yatayo bodhicāriṇaḥ sarvasattva hitaṃ kṛtvā saṃpracāransadāśubhe  SvayambhuP tataste ti viśuddhātmāḥ pañcābhijñā maharddhikāḥ vandyāḥ pūjyāḥ sadevānāṃ lokānāṃ guravo bhavan  SvayambhuP tasmiṃśca samaye tatra gireḥ śaṃkhasya mūrddhani vajrasattva karāṅguṣṭhānniścacārāmbu nirmmalaṃ  SvayambhuP tademānvadbhuti spandaṃ puṇyatīrthamahatsarit yadabhūt sarvalokānāṃ catuvargaphalapradā  SvayambhuP bhūyo pi sādadī tasyaḥ krakuchanda spatāyinaḥ saddharmma deśanā vākyāvabhūvā ti pavitratā  SvayambhuP tenāsau sarvatīrthāgrā vāgmatītiprasiddhitā bhadraśrī guṇa saṃbhartrī sarvapāpa viśodhanī  SvayambhuP ye tatra vidhinā snātvā pitṛ devāditarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā dānādikaṃ datvā vrataṃ cāpi prakurvate  SvayambhuP te saṃghavimalātmāno bhadraśrīsadguṇānvitāḥ yathākāmaṃ sukhaṃ bhutvā saṃprayānti jinālayaṃ  SvayambhuP iti matvā sadā tatra snātvā pitrāditarppaṇaṃ dānādi saṃvaraṃ kṛtvā sacarantāṃ jagaddhite  SvayambhuP tasyā darśanamātreṇa pītāmvu vimātrake sparśanādapi naśyante sarvāṇi pātakānyapi  SvayambhuP prakṣālyāpi ca tatrāsyaṃ gaṃgā snāna phalaṃ labheta śilasiṃ ca mātreṇa śuddhānte indriyāni ṣaṭ  SvayambhuP evaṃ mahattaraṃ puṇyaṃ vāgmatī bhajanodbhavaṃ sarve tīrthottamākhyātaṃ te nāsau vāgmatī jinaiḥ  SvayambhuP iti matvātra saṃsāre icchanti ye sadāśubhaṃ vāgmatī śrī sukhādhārāṃ bhajantu sarvadāpi te  SvayambhuP bhūyopyanyā sarijjātā tasyaiva karasaṃbhavā sāpi pavitritā bhūtā krakuchandasya vākyataḥ  SvayambhuP tatra pravrajitānāṃ yat śmaśrukeśanakhāni ca kṛtvā bhāgadvayaṃ tatra bhāgamekaṃ pracikṣipuḥ  SvayambhuP tadā keśāvatītyāsītprasiddhā sā mahānadī eka bhāgantu tatraiva saṃsthāpitaṃ śilātale  SvayambhuP yāvanti śmaśru keśāni tāvantyapi śilātale prādurbhūtāni caityāni tāṃnyadyāpi vasaṃti hi  SvayambhuP sāpi nadī mahātīrtha vāgmatī va prasīddhatā teṣāṃ pravrajitānāṃ hi mahatpuṇyānubhāvataḥ  SvayambhuP teṣāṃ pravrajitānāṃca bhikṣuṇāṃ brahmacāriṇāṃ tadāpuṇya mahākīrti śabda sarvatra prāsarat  SvayambhuP tadanantaramaṣṭau ca vītarāgā nirāśrayāḥ jyotirūpā nirākārāḥ prādurbhūtā jagaddhite  SvayambhuP ekaḥ śaṃkhagireḥ pārśve maṇicūḍāśramāntike maṇiliṃga iti khyātaḥ so dyāpi saṃpratiṣṭhitaḥ  SvayambhuP dvitīyo bhucca gokarṇa sthale jyotirṣayākṛtiḥ cārugirau tṛtīyaśca kumbhatīrthe caturthakaḥ  SvayambhuP paṃcamaḥ phaṇiśailaśca ṣaṣṭhaśca gartakasthale saptamo gandhavatyāṃ ca aṣṭamo vikramasthale  SvayambhuP ete ṣṭau mahādevāḥ vītarāgā niraṃjanāḥ jyotirūpā nirāṃkārāḥ prādurbhūtā jagaddhite  SvayambhuP atraiṣāṃ vītarāgānyanubhāvāt samantataḥ manoramāmahī jātā sarva pīṭhoktamāvanau  SvayambhuP tadāyobhū mahāsvo mahāsaṃmata vaṃśajaḥ kṛpākāruṇya bhadrātmā bodhisattvo nṛpo bhavat  SvayambhuP tatra sa nṛpa rājendraḥ krakuchandena tāyinā sahātra draṣṭumāyātaḥ svayaṃbhuvaṃ khagānanāṃ  SvayambhuP dūrātsa yenamālokya svayaṃbhuvaṃ jinālayaṃ praṇatvā samupāgatya cakre pradakṣiṇātrayaṃ  SvayambhuP tato bhyarcye mahotsāhaireṇaṃ pañcajinātmakaṃ  SvayambhuP aṣṭāṃgaiśca praṇatvā ca prābhajaccharaṇāśritaḥ tatastathā ca rājendro mañjudevaṃ ca saṅguruṃ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya prābhajatsaṃpramoditaḥ tatastathā sa rājendraḥ khagānanāṃ jineśvarīṃ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya mahotsāhairmudābhajat tato ṣṭau vītarāgāśca sarvānatā tsvayaṃbhuvaḥ  SvayambhuP dṛṣṭvā samudito rājā mahotsāhaistathā bhajat etatpuṇyānubhāvaiḥ sa mahatpuṇyāśayaḥ kṛtī  SvayambhuP sarvadharmmādhi rājendraḥ sarvalokādhipo vabhau sarva vidyādhipo rājā bhadraśrī sadguṇāśrayaḥ  SvayambhuP tena dharmākaro nāmno prasiddhau bhūdvirājiteḥ tataḥ so tra mahārājaḥ saṃsthāstuṃ kāma ātmanā  SvayambhuP krakuchandaṃ munīndrantaṃ praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayat bhagavanyaha vāṃchāstā vijānīyāt mamecchitaṃ  SvayambhuP tadanujñāṃ padatvāmenugrahaṃ kartumarhati iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavānsa munīśvaraḥ  SvayambhuP dharmmākaraṃ narendraṃntaṃ sampaśyannevamādiśat sādhu rājan mahāsattva yadevaṃ tvaṃ samīcchasi  SvayambhuP tathātvamiha san sthitvā pālayaṃ bodhayan prajāḥ tathātrasakaralāllokān saṃsthāpya saṃprabodhayan  SvayambhuP bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya cārayasva sadā śubhe dharmmeṇa pālayan sarvāllokān svayaṃ samācaran  SvayambhuP yathākāma sukhaṃ tu prāsacarasva jagaddhite dharmmanītyā samādhāya kṛtvā lokahitaṃ sadā  SvayambhuP sādhayanvodhi sambhāraṃ sadeha nivasāśritāḥ sadāsya śaraṇe sthitvā dharmmadhātoḥ svayambhuvaḥ  SvayambhuP śraddhayā bhajanaṃ kṛtvā saṃcarasva jagaddhite asyāḥ khagānanāyāśca devyāḥ śaraṇa āśritaḥ  SvayambhuP sarvadā bhajanaṃ kṛtvā carasva bodhisaṃvaraṃ asyāpi mañjudevasya sadguroḥ samupāśritaḥ  SvayambhuP buddhānuśāsanaṃ dhṛtvā saddharmme saṃcaraṃsva sa eṣāṃ ca vītarāgānāmaṣṭānāmapi sarvadā  SvayambhuP śraddhayā bhajanaṃ kṛtvāḥ sādhaya dharmmamuktamaṃ vāgmatī pramukhānāñca tīrthānāṃ samupāśrayena  SvayambhuP snāna dānādikaṃ kṛtvā pittṛndevāñca toṣayan labdhā trikāya saṃśuddhiṃ dhṛtvā saṃbodhimānasaṃ  SvayambhuP sarvasattvā hitaṃ kṛtvā nivasasva yathāsukhaṃ evaṃ rājendra lokāṃśca sarvānapi pravodhayaṃ  SvayambhuP eteṣāmapi sarveṣāṃ saṃsthāpya śaraṇe sadā pūjā bhakti mahotsāhaiḥ cārayitvā samādarāt  SvayambhuP bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya cārayasva sadā śubhe evaṃ kṛtvā mahārāja saṃbodhi nihitāśrayaḥ  SvayambhuP bodhicaryāvrataṃ dhṛtvā saṃcarasva jagaddhite etatpuṇyābhiliptātmā bhaviṣyasi jinātmajaḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattva mahābhijñā bhadraśrī sadguṇāśrayaḥ kadācidapi naivatvaṃ durgatau ca kvacitsareḥ  SvayambhuP sadāsadgati saṃjātoḥ samṛddhi siddhimānsudhīḥ śrīmānsarvaguṇādhīśaḥ sarvalokādhipaḥ kṛti  SvayambhuP krameṇa bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā samāhitaṃ triratna bhajanotsāha mahānandasukhaṃ sadā  SvayambhuP bhuṃjānā nirmmalācāraścaturbrahma vihāriṇaḥ niḥkleśo nirjayan mārān sarvānarhantvamāptavān  SvayambhuP trividhāṃ bodhimāsādya saṃbuddhapadamāpnuyāḥ lokāḥ sarve pi caivaṃhi pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ sadā sadgati saṃbhavāḥ bodhicaryā vrataṃ dhṛtvā saṃcaranto jagaddhite  SvayambhuP jitvā māragaṇānsarvāśvaturbrahma vihāriṇaḥ niḥkleśā nirmmalātmānaḥ saṃsāragati niḥspṛhā  SvayambhuP arhanta trividhāsambodhiṃ prāpya buddhatvamāpnuyuḥ eṣāṃ ca vītarāgānāṃ aṣṭānāmapi sāmprataṃ  SvayambhuP pūjāphala viśeṣatvaṃ va kṣyāmi śṛṇu tannṛpaḥ vāgmatisalile yastu snātvā nityaṃ samāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP aṣṭāvetān maheśān vītarāgān sadā bhajet yatatpuṇya viśuddhātmā śrī samṛddhi sukhānvitaḥ  SvayambhuP saṃsāre sarvadā saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yāyācchivālayaṃ ghṛtena snāpayet yastu vītarāgān svayaṃbhūvaḥ  SvayambhuP śivālayaṃ vrajet so pi madhurā brahmamandiraṃ dadhnā yaḥ snāpayed devān vītarāgān svayaṃbhuvaḥ  SvayambhuP sa yāyād vaiṣṇavaṃ lokaṃ śrī samṛddhi sukhāśrayaṃ snānādikṣurasenāpi vidyādharaṃ padaṃ vrajet  SvayambhuP gandhodakena gāndharva kṣīreṇa śaśinaḥ padaṃ śītodakena śuddhātmā niṣpāpā nirmalendriyaṃ  SvayambhuP eṣāṃ pūjāṃ ca yaḥ kuryānnānāpuṣpaiḥ sugandhitaiḥ sarva kāma sukhaṃ bhuktvā modate manujādhipaḥ  SvayambhuP vilvapatrāṇi śreṣṭhāni rohaṇarccaṃ atandritaḥ śivaṃ sarvatra prāpnoti yajñānāṃ ca sahasrakaṃ  SvayambhuP naivedyaṃ ḍhokayedyaḥ sa dīrdhāyuḥ syād vali nṛpaḥ dīpamālāṃ ca yo dadyāttejasvī syātsudṛṣṭimān  SvayambhuP gugguruṃ yo dahettasya naśyate sarvapātakaṃ tilapātraṃ ca yodadyādurggati sa vrajennahi  SvayambhuP suvarṇaṃ ye pradadyācca sa yāyāt saṅgatau sadā tiladhenuṃ pradadyādyoḥ sa saṃ yāyācchivālayaṃ  SvayambhuP raupyakhurāṃ hema śṛṃgī raṇad ghaṇṭhāvalaṃ vinā savatsāṃ kapilāṃ dadyādyaḥ sa yajñaphalaṃ labhet  SvayambhuP yo ratnakaṃcukaṃ dadyāt sa bhaved bahuratnavān vastravān vastradānena bhūmidānena bhūmivān  SvayambhuP tūryasaṃgīti nṛtyādi mahotsāhaṃ pracārayet yaḥ sadivya śrutiprāptaḥ śivapārśvacaro bhavet  SvayambhuP nīlotpalārkapadmāni yo dadyāt sa śriyaṃ labhet yo rcayed vilvapatreṇa sa baliṣṭho bhavet kṛtī  SvayambhuP dhatturakena nirvārya kena vīreṇa sad vano sugandhikusumaiḥ sarvai yoṣṭāvapi samarcayat  SvayambhuP sa śrīmān subhago dhīmān bhavetsaugandhitāśraye divyātisundaraḥ kāntā bhadraśrī sadguṇāddhimān  SvayambhuP puṣpaiḥ patraiḥ phalamūlaistotrai rvā yo rcayecchivān sa devālayamāsādya bhuktvā divyasukhaṃ caret  SvayambhuP yaśca pradakṣiṇāṃ kṛtvā bhajennityaṃ samādarāt rūpavānsa bhavedante saṃprayāyācchivālayaṃ  SvayambhuP yaśca stotraiḥ prasannātmā bhajetetānmaheśvarān sa tu pitrālayaṃ gatvā mahānanda sukhaṃ labhet  SvayambhuP yaścanāma samuccārya japitvā ca samāhitaḥ so pi śrīmān mahābhijñaḥ prānte yāyācchivālayaṃ  SvayambhuP aṣṭāṃgaiḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā yo bhajet tān maheśvarān sa yāyāt saṅgatāveva durgatiṃ na kadācan  SvayambhuP smṛtvā dhyātvā samuccārya nāmapi yo bhajat sadā sa divyāmṛtabhuṃjāno ramed divi yathāsukhaṃ  SvayambhuP yaśca dṛṣṭā prasannātmā praṇamet sāṃjalirmudā so pi divyāmṛtaṃ bhuktvā ramet svarge suraiḥ saha  SvayambhuP ityeṣāṃ vītarāgāṇāmaṣṭānāṃ bhajanād dhruvaṃ viśeṣaphalamājñāya bhajasvaināṃ yathecchayā  SvayambhuP tadatra bhūtale śuddha vidhāya puramāśrayan sarvāllokān pratiṣṭhāpya pālayansarvadā vasa  SvayambhuP tadātra sarvadigbhyo pi sarvalokāḥ pramoditāḥ āgatya saṃsthiti kṛtvāni vaseyuḥ sadā mudā  SvayambhuP tadā jānapadāścātra grāmāścanagarāṇyapi nirgama paktanaṃ cāpi pravarkteyuḥ samantataḥ  SvayambhuP tathā devā surendrāścaṃ sarve lokādhipā api āgatyātra samālokya dharmadhātoḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ  SvayambhuP gandharvā guhyakā yakṣāḥ kinnarā rākṣasā api kumbhāṇḍā garuḍā nāgāḥ siddhā vidyādharā api  SvayambhuP sādhyāśca mātṛkā ścāpi sa bhairavagaṇā api ṛṣayo yoginaścāpi yataya stīrthikā api  SvayambhuP śrāvakā bhikṣavo rhanta ścailakāścāpyupāsakāḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ śaiva kaulāśca vaiṣṇavāḥ  SvayambhuP āgatyātra samālokya dharmmadhātoḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ devyāḥ khagānanāyāśca mañjudevasya saṅguroḥ  SvayambhuP eṣāṃ ca vītarāgānāṃ tīrthānāṃ cānubhāvatāṃ prasāditāḥ samāśritya bhajeyuḥ sarvadā mudā  SvayambhuP tadātra sarvadaiteṣāṃ sarvā puṇyānubhāvataḥ subhikṣaṃ maṃgalotsāhaṃ nirutpātaṃ bhaveddhruvraṃ  SvayambhuP ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa krakuchandena sapratuḥ dharmmākara samākarṇya tatheti pratibudhyata  SvayambhuP tataḥ saḥnṛpa utthāya sāñjalistaṃ munīśvaraṃ krakucchanda sa saṃghaṃ ya praṇatvevaṃ nyavedayata  SvayambhuP bhagavan bhavatāmājñāṃ dhṛtvāhamatra sarvadā puraṃ vidhāya lokānāṃ hitārthe nivase khalu  SvayambhuP tad bhavān kṛpayālokya sarvadātra himālaye sasaṃgho dharmmamādiśya viharaṃtu jagaddhite  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ dharmmākaraṃ mahāsattvaṃ taṃ paśyannevamavravīt  SvayambhuP nāhaṃ sadātra tiṣṭheyaṃ careyaṃ sarva bhūtale sarvasattva hitārtha hi bhavāmi dharmmadikṣiṇaḥ  SvayambhuP ityādiśya munīndreṇa krakuchandaḥ sa sāṃdhikaḥ tataḥ saṃprasthito nyatra deśeṃ saṃbhāṣayan yayau  SvayambhuP tato dharmākaraḥ so tra vidhāya nagaraṃ tathā rājyāṃgāni pratisthāpya rājyaṃ kṛtvādhyatiṣṭhata  SvayambhuP tadātra sarve āgatya mandireṣu samantataḥ āśritya saṃsthitiṃ kṛtvā nivasanto mudā caran  SvayambhuP tato nyepi samāyātāḥ sarvadigbhyo tra sarvataḥ jānapade purenekaṃ grāmeṣu nyavasan mudā  SvayambhuP tathā devā surādyāśca sarve lokādhipā api svasvaparijanaiḥ sārddhaṃ āgatyātra mudā vasan  SvayambhuP tathā maharṣayaścāpi yatayo brahmacāriṇaḥ yogino bhikṣavo rhanto vratinaścāpyupāsakāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvā ścailakāḥ śrāvakā api yathābhilaṣite deśe kṛtvā śramaṃ samāśrayan  SvayambhuP tathānya tīrthikāḥ śaivā vaiṣṇavāḥ kaulikā api yathābhilaṣite sthāne kṛtvāśramaṃ samāśrayan  SvayambhuP pratyeka sugatāścāpi samāgatya samantataḥ vivikte āśrame ramye samāśritya mudā vasan  SvayambhuP munīndrā api cāgatya vihṛtyātra sasāṃdhikāḥ prārya sambodhi saddharmmaṃ samādeśyan tvarāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ puṇyatamā bhūmīriyaṃ himālayāhavayā sukhāvatinibhāramyā bodhisattva samāśraya  SvayambhuP vahūni cātra tīrthāni sarvapāpaharāṇyapi jātāni santi sarvārtha samṛddhi siddhidāṇyapi  SvayambhuP tadeteṣu ca tīrtheṣu snātvā carata sadvrataṃ pāpaṃ hantuṃ śubhaṃ prāptuṃ samīchantyatra ye narāḥ  SvayambhuP ye tra tīrtheṣu sarveṣu snātvā nityaṃ samāhita japa yajñādi karmmāṇi kṛtvā caranti samvaraṃ  SvayambhuP pitṛñcāpi samabhyarcya devāñca śraddhayādarāt datvā dānaṃ samādhāya dhyātvāpīśaṃ bhajanti ca  SvayambhuP te pi sarve vikalmāṣāḥ pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ śrīmantaḥ siddhi mantaśca bhaveyuḥ sadguṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste sarva sattvānāṃ hitārthe dharma sādhakāḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ bhaveyuḥ sugatātmajāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste bodhisambhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ triratna bhajanaṃ kṛtvā saṃcarerañjagaddhite  SvayambhuP tataste vimalātmāno niḥkleśā vijitendriyāḥ arhanta strividhāṃ bodhiṃ prāpyeyuḥ saugataṃ padaṃ  SvayambhuP evaṃ matvātra tīrtheṣu sarveṣu bodhivāṃchibhiḥ nātvā dānādi karma karttavya sarvadā bhave  SvayambhuP ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ nisamya te sarva sabhāśritā lokāḥ prābhyanandan pravodhitāḥ  SvayambhuP iti śrī svayaṃbhū caitya samutpatti kathā vītarāgatīrtha rāṣṭra pravarttano nāma caturtho dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ pañcama adhyāyaḥ svayambhūtpatyaneka tīrthasaṃjātapuṇyamahātmyavarṇano nāmaathāsau ca mahāsattva maitreya sāñjalirmudā bhagavantaṃ tamānasya prārthayedevamādarāt  SvayambhuP bhagavan tatra tīrthānāṃ snātvā dānādi karmmajaṃ puṇyaphala viśeṣatvaṃ samādiśatu sāmpratam  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavānsa munīśvaraḥ maitreyaṃ taṃ mahāsattvaṃ sampaśyannevamādiśat  SvayambhuP sādhu śṛṇu mahāsattva tīrtha sevā phalodbhavaṃ puṇyaṃ tad viśeṣatvaṃ vakṣāmi sarva bodhane  SvayambhuP tadyathā mūlatīrthāni kathyante dvādaśātra hi mahāpuṇyāni sarveṣāṃ tīrthānāṃ yāni bhūtale  SvayambhuP amogha phaladāyinyāṃ vāgmatyāṃ yatra saṃgame tattīrtha śodhanaṃ khyātaṃ daśapāpaviśodhanāt  SvayambhuP tatra nāgādhipā raktastakṣakākhyaḥ sukāntimān samujvalanmahāratnaṃśrīmatphaṇā vibhūṣitaḥ  SvayambhuP yenarā śraddhayā tatra puṇyatīrthe yathāvidhiḥ snānaṃ kuryumudā yāvadeka viṃśati vāsaraṃ  SvayambhuP japa yajñādi karmmāṇi kuryuḥ saptadinānyapi pitṛn devāñca saṃpūjya kuryuḥ saṃtṛptamoditān  SvayambhuP dadyurdānānicārthibhyo yathepsitaṃ samādarāt śuddhaśīlāḥ samādhāyaiścareyuśca vrataṃ tathā  SvayambhuP etatpuṇyaviśuddhāste niḥkleśā nirmmalendriyāḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhaveyuḥ śrī guṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste bodhisambhāraṃ pūrayitvāyathākramaṃ trividhāṃ bodhimāsādya saṃvuddha padamāpnuyuḥ  SvayambhuP tataśca māradāyiṇyo vāgmatyā yatra saṃgamaḥ tacchāntatīrthamākhyātaṃ kleśa doṣa viśodhanaṃ  SvayambhuP tatranāgādhipaḥ śuklaḥ soma śikhītiviśrutaḥ vilasanmaṇiratnaśrīphaṇāmaṇḍala bhūṣitaḥ  SvayambhuP tatrāpi śānta tīrtha ca ye kleśa duḥṣitā narāḥ kuryu snānaṃ sadā yāvadekaviṃśati vāsaraṃ  SvayambhuP japa yajñādika kuryuścareyuścādhi poṣadhaṃ pitṛn devāñca saṃpūjya kuryuḥ saṃtuṣṭananditān  SvayambhuP dadyurdānāṃni cārthi bhyo yathābhilaṣitaṃ mudā śuddhaśīlā samācārāḥ dhyātvā bhajeyurīśvaraṃ  SvayambhuP etatpuṇyābhiliptāste pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhaveyuḥ śrīguṇālayāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste bodhi sambhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ arhanta strividhāmbodhi prāpyeyuḥ saugataṃ padaṃ  SvayambhuP tataśca maṇirohiṇyā vāgmatyā yatrasaṃgame tatrorddhaniḥsṛtā śuddha sphaṭikādārasaṃnnibhāṃ  SvayambhuP rudradhārā mṛtākhyātā tayā ca tatra saṃgame triveṇī saṃgame tena śaṃkara tīrtha mucyate  SvayambhuP tatra nāgādhipa śaṃkhapālo gaurāti sundaraḥ maṇirasmi samuddipta śrīmatphaṇā vibhūṣitaḥ  SvayambhuP tatra śaṃkara tīrthe ye mānavāśca yathāvidhiḥ snānaṃ kuryurmudā yāvadekaviṃśativāsaraṃ  SvayambhuP japa yajñādikarmmāṇiḥ kuryuśca saptavāsaraṃ pitṛndevāñca saṃpūjya tarppayeyuryathāvidhi  SvayambhuP dadyurdānāni cārthibhya śraddhayā bodhimānasāḥ dhyātvā bhajeyurīśaṃ casaṃcareñcapoṣaḍhaṃ  SvayambhuP etatpuṇya viśuddhātmā niḥkleśāḥ nirmmalendriyāḥ labheyuḥ śrī mahāpuṣṭiśānti guṇā ca śāntyapi  SvayambhuP durggati tena yāyuśca saṃjātāḥ saṅgatau sadā bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhaveyu bhadracāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP tataste bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ arhanta strividhāṃ bodhi prāpyeyuḥ saugataṃ padaṃ  SvayambhuP tataśca rājamañcaryā vāgmatyā yatra saṃgamaṃ tadrājatīrthamākhyātaṃ rājyārogyasukhapadaṃ  SvayambhuP tatra nāgādhipaḥ śuklaḥ surupākhyātisundaraḥ maṇiratna mahādīpti śrīprabhā maṇḍitāśrayaḥ  SvayambhuP tatra ye mānavāyā vadeka viṃśativāsaraṃ snāna dāna japa dhyānaṃ kuryu dadyuśca saṃvaraṃ  SvayambhuP etatpuṇya viśuddhāste nirdoṣā vimalendriyāḥ rājyaśvarya sadārogya bhadra saukhyama vāpnuyuḥ  SvayambhuP te pi na durggati yāyuḥ sadāsadgati saṃbhavāḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhaveyuḥ śrīguṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste bodhisambhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ arhanta strividhāṃ bodhi prāpyayāyu jinālayaṃ  SvayambhuP tathātra vimalāvatyā keśāvatyā ca saṃgameḥ manorathaṃ tadākhyātaṃ svecchālaṃkāra saṃpradaṃ  SvayambhuP tatra nāgādhipo bhīmaḥ kulikākhyo tikarvuraḥ phaṇāmaṇi samuddīpta śrīprabhāmaṇḍitāśrayaḥ  SvayambhuP tatra manorathe tīrthe manujā ye yathāvidhiḥ snāna dānādikaṃ kuryurekaviśati vāsaraṃ  SvayambhuP te pi na durgatiṃ yāyuḥ sadā sadgatisaṃbhavāḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhadraśrī sadguṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP paṭṭasuvastraratnādi svecchālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ sarvasattva hitādhāna careryurbodhisavaraṃ  SvayambhuP tataste bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ trividhāṃ bodhimāsādya saṃbuddha padamāpnuyuḥ  SvayambhuP tataśca kusumāvatyā keśāvatyāpi saṃgame nirmmalatīrthamākhyātaṃ kalpanāvighnanāśanaṃ  SvayambhuP tatra nāgo palālākhyaḥ pītavarṇṇo mahākṛtiḥ divyaratna prabhojjvāla śrīmatphaṇā vibhūṣitaḥ  SvayambhuP tatra ye mānavā yāvadekaviṃśativāsaraṃ snānadānādikaṃ kuryustathāsarve ca pūrvavat  SvayambhuP te pi na durgatiṃ yāyuḥ sadā saṅgatisaṃbhavāḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhadraśrīsadguṇāyāḥ  SvayambhuP kali vighna mala kleśa nirmukta bhadracāriṇaḥ sarvasattva hitāraktā bhaveyu brahmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP tataste bodhisaṃbhāra purayitvā yathākramaṃ arhanto bodhimāsādya sambuddhapadamāpnuyuḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ suvarṇṇavatyā ca bāgamatyā yatra saṃgame nidhānatīrthamākhyātaṃ sarva sampatidāyakaṃ  SvayambhuP tatra nāgau haritavarṇau nandaupanandanāvubhau nānā ratna prabhāddīptiḥ śrī matphaṇāvibhūṣitau
