SvayambhuP tatra ye manujā yāvadeka viṃśativāsaraṃ snānādi pūrvavatsarva karmmaṃ kuryuryathāvidhiḥ  SvayambhuP te pi na durggatiṃ yāyuḥ sadā saṅgatisaṃbhavāḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhadraśrī sadguṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP sarvasattvārtha sampannā bhaveyuḥ dharmmacāriṇaḥ tepyaivaṃ bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP arhanto bodhimāsādya saugataṃ padamāpnuyuḥ tataśca pāpa nāśinyā keśavatyābhisaṃgame  SvayambhuP jñānatīrthaṃ tadākhyātaṃ divyabhoga sukhapradaṃ tatra nāgādhipaḥ śukla vāśukirnāma bhīṣaṇaḥ  SvayambhuP divya ratna prabhāśrī matphaṇālaṃkāramaṇḍitaḥ tatra yemānavā yā vadekaviṃśativāsaraṃ  SvayambhuP snāna dānādi karmmāṇi kuryuḥ sarvāṇi purvavat te pi na durggati yāyurjātāḥ sadāpi saṅgatau  SvayambhuP sarva bhoga mahāsampatsukhavanto nirāmayāḥ bodhisattvā mahasattvāścaturbrahma vihāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrīsadguṇādhārā bhaveyu bodhicāriṇaḥ tathā te bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP arhanto bodhimāsādya sarvajña padmāpnuyuḥ bhadśrī sadguṇādhārāḥ sambuddhaguṇasādhinaḥ  SvayambhuP tataśca yatra vāgmatyāḥ keśāvatyā ca saṃgameḥ taccintāmaṇimākhyātaṃ sarvakāmārtha saṃpadam  SvayambhuP gaṃgā ca yamunācāpi tathā devī sarasvatī parva pratyāgatā tatra tena pañca samāgamā  SvayambhuP tatra nāgādhipaḥ śuklo varuṇā sarva nāgarāt divyaratna prabhāśrīmatphaṇāmaṇḍala bhūṣitaḥ  SvayambhuP tatra ye mānavā yāvadekaviṃśati vāsaraṃ snānadānādikaṃ sarve kuryuḥ pūrvavadādarāt  SvayambhuP te pi na durggatiṃ yāyuḥ sadā sadgatisaṃbhavāḥ saṃpūrṇṇa paramāyuṣkāḥ vidyādhipā vicakṣaṇāḥ  SvayambhuP susantānā mahābhogā dhammārtha kāmabhoginaḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvā ścaturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrī sadguṇādhārā bhaveyuḥ bodhicāriṇaḥ tataste bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP arhanto bodhimāsādya saṃbuddha padamāpnuyuḥ tataśca yatra vāgmatyā ratnāvatyāḥ samāgame  SvayambhuP pramodatīrthamākhyātaṃ ratiprītivaśārthadaḥ tatra nāgādhipaḥ padmo dhavaladivya sundaraḥ  SvayambhuP divyaratna mahākānti phaṇāmaṇḍala bhūṣitaḥ tatra ye mānavā yāvadekaviṃśativāsaraṃ  SvayambhuP snāna dānāni sarvāṇi kuryuḥ karmmāṇi pūrvavat te pi nadurgatīṃ yāyuḥ sadā sadgati saṃbhavāḥ  SvayambhuP rati prīti vaśānanda mahāsaukhya samanvitā bodhisattvo mahāsattvoḥ pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrī sadguṇādhārā bhaveyuḥ bodhisādhinaḥ tataste bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP arhanta śtrividhāṃ bodhiṃprāpya yāyu rjinālayaṃ tatraścayatra vāgmatyā cārumatyā samāgame  SvayambhuP tatsulakṣaṇamākhyātaṃ śrī tejo bhāgyasampadaṃ tatra nāgo mahāpadmo ti dhavalo ti sundaraḥ  SvayambhuP divyaratna prabhāśrī matphaṇāmaṇḍalamaṇḍitaḥ tatra ye mānavā yāvadekaviṃsativāsaraṃ  SvayambhuP snāna dānaṃ japa dhyānaṃ kuryuryajñaṃ ca pūrvavat te pina durgatiṃ yāyuḥ sadā sadgati saṃbhavāḥ  SvayambhuP śrītejo bhogyasaṃpannā surupālakṣaṇānvitā bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ bhadraśrīsadguṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP sarvasattva hitodyuktāḥ bhaveyuḥ bodhicāriṇaḥ tataste bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP arhanta trividhāṃ bodhi prāpyeyuḥ saugataṃ padaṃ tataśca yatra vāgmatyā prabhāmatyā samāgameḥ  SvayambhuP jayatīrtha samākhyātaṃ sarvaśatrubhayāntakṛt tatra nāgādhipaḥ śukraḥ śrīkānti divya sundaraḥ  SvayambhuP divyaratna prabhāśrī matphaṇāmaṇḍalamaṇḍitaḥ tatra ye mānavā yāvadeka viṃśativāsaraṃ  SvayambhuP snātvā yajñādi karmmāṇi kuryuḥ sarvāṇi pūrvavat te pi na durggatīṃ yāyuḥ sadā sadgati saṃbhavāḥ  SvayambhuP nirbhayā striguṇotsāhājayino nirjitārayaḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvāścaturbrahma vihāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrī sadguṇācārā bhaveyu bodhicāriṇaḥ tataste bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP arhantastrividhāṃ bodhiprāpyeyuḥ saugatapadaṃ dvādaśaitāni nāmāni tīrthāni mahāntyatra himālaye  SvayambhuP anyānyapi ca saṃtyatra tāni vakṣyāmyahaṃ śṛṇu tadyatho pari vāgmatyāḥ śrotasiddhārasaṃnidhau  SvayambhuP saundarya tīrthamākhyātaṃ saundarya guṇasaṃpadaṃ tatra yemānavā yāvadekaviṃśativāsaraṃ  SvayambhuP snāna dānāni karmmāṇi kuryuḥ sarvāṇi pūrvavat te pina durggatiṃ yāyuḥ sadā sadgatisaṃbhavāḥ  SvayambhuP surūpā lakṣaṇopetāḥ śrīmanta sadguṇānvitāḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvā caturbrahma vihāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP sarvasattva hitādhānaṃ careyu rbodhisaṃmvaraṃ tataste bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP arhanta strividhāṃ bodhisaṃprāpyeyuḥ jinālayaṃ taduparicayattīrtha agastyo na maharṣiṇā  SvayambhuP nityasnānaṃ japa dhyānaṃ kṛtvā yajñaṃ ca sevitaṃ tenāgastyaṃ mahattīrtha tadā khyāntaṃ munīśvaraiḥ  SvayambhuP tatra ye manujā snāyūste yāyuḥ paramāṃ gatiṃ dāna yajña japādiśca kuryu dhyātvāyi ceśvaraṃ  SvayambhuP toṣayayustathāpittṛndadyurdānaṃ yathepsitaṃ te sarve vimalātmānaśca caturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhaveyuḥ śrīguṇāśrayāḥ tathā te bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP arhanta strividhāmbodhiṃ prāpya buddhatvamāpnuyuḥ tatraivānantanāgena yadāśritaṃ mahāhradaṃ  SvayambhuP tena tadahradamākhyātaṃ anantatīrthamarthadaṃ tatra ye manujāyāvadekaṃviṃśati vāsaraṃ  SvayambhuP snāna dāna japa dhyānaṃ kuryuryajñaṃca pūrvavat te pi na durgatiṃ yāyuḥsadā sadgatisambhavāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvā rbhaveyuḥ śrīguṇāśrayāḥ tathā te bodhisambhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP arhanto bodhimāsādya sarvajñapadamāpnuyuḥ tatraiva ca mahattīrtha āryatārāniṣevitam  SvayambhuP tenedaṃ prāthitaṃ prāryatārā tīrtha subhāgyadaṃ tatrāpi ye narā ryāvadekaviṃśativāsaraṃ  SvayambhuP snānadānajapa dhyānaṃ yajñaṃ kuryu ryathāvidhi te pi na durgatiṃ yāyuḥ saṃjātāḥ sadgatau sadā  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ saubhāgyaśālino dhīrā bhadraśrīsadguṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP sarvasattvahitotsāhā bhaveyu rbodhicāriṇaḥ tathā te bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP arhanta strividhāṃ bodhiṃ prāpyeyuḥ saugataṃpadaṃ arddhaurddhañca vāgmantyāḥ prabhavatīrthamuktamaṃ  SvayambhuP sarveṣāmapi tīrthānāṃ pradhānamagramucyate tatraikasnāna mātreṇa gaṃgā snāna śatādhikaṃ  SvayambhuP puṇyaṃ mahattaraṃ siddhaṃ vāñchitārtha sukhapradaṃ tatra ye mānavā yāvadekaviṃsativāsaraṃ  SvayambhuP snāna dāna japa dhyānaṃ yajñaṃ kuryuryuyathāvidhiḥ śuviśuddha trikāyāste yathākāma sukhāśina ca  SvayambhuP dhamārthaṃ śrīsamṛddhāḥ syuścaturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ kvacinna durggatiṃ yāyuḥ saṃjātā sadgato sadā  SvayambhuP svaparātmahitaṃ kṛtvā saṃcarensadā śubhe tataste vimalātmāno suviśuddhendriyāśayāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ bhaveyuḥ sadguṇākarāḥ tathā te bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathāvidhiḥ  SvayambhuP arhantastrividhāṃ bodhi prāpyeyuḥ saugataṃpadaṃ taṃ śaṃkhaparvata nāma sarva śiloccayottamaṃ  SvayambhuP samārohaṇa mātreṇa niṣṇā yeḥ siddhimān bhavet tatrāpi ye samāśritya snātvā dhyātvā samāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP japa yajñādi dānaṃ ca kuryuḥ saṃbodhimānasāḥ te pi na durgatiṃ yāyuḥ sadāsadgati saṃbhavāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ niḥkleśā vimalātmānaḥ sarva sattva hitāśayāḥ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrī sadguṇādhārā bhaveyu rbrahmacāriṇaḥ tataste bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP arhanto bodhimāsādya saṃbuddhapadamāpnuyuḥ vahūni copa tīrthāni vidyante tra himālaye  SvayambhuP tāni tīrthāni sarvāṇi bhukti mukti pradānyapi yatra yatra śravantīnāma nyeṣāṃ ca samāgame  SvayambhuP tatra tatrāpi tīrthāni puṇya phala pradāni hi teṣāṃ cāpyupa tīrthānāṃ pṛthakpṛthatphalaṃ mahat  SvayambhuP pāpa saṃśodhanaṃ puṇyaṃ saddharmmasukhasādhanaṃ teṣvapi ye narāḥ snātvā careyu poṣaḍhaṃ vrataṃ  SvayambhuP dadyurdānāni cārthibhyaṃ kuryuryajñāni ca ye mudā pitṛsaṃtarpya yeyuśca pūjayeyuḥ surānapi  SvayambhuP smṛtvā dhyātvā triratnānāṃ bhajeyunemijalyanaiḥ evaṃ lokādhipānāṃ ca smṛtvā dhyātvā samāhitāḥ  SvayambhuP japitvā nāma mantrāṇi sādhayeyu ryathāvidhiḥ tāni sarvāni sidhyeyuḥ sādhitāni jagaddhite  SvayambhuP dadyuśceha śubhotsāhaṃ paratra nirvṛtaṃ padaṃ te pi na durgatiṃ yāyuḥ sadā sadgatisaṃbhavāḥ  SvayambhuP niḥkleśā vimalātmānaḥ pariśuddhā trimaṇḍalāḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvāścaturbrahma vihāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrī sadguṇādhārā bhaveyuḥ bodhicāriṇaḥ tataste bodhisambhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP arhanta bodhiṃ prāpyayāyu rjinālayaṃ ekaṃ vijñāya sarveṣāṃ tīrthānāmapisatphalaṃ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrī sadguṇātsāhaṃ saukhyasaṃbodhi sādhanaṃ sarveṣveteṣu tīrtheṣubhadraśrī guṇa vāṃchābhiḥ  SvayambhuP snāna dānādikaṃ karma karttavyaṃ bodhi prāptaye ye ye eteṣu tīrtheṣu snātvā nityaṃ yathāvidhiḥ  SvayambhuP datvā dāna vrataṃ dhṛtvā dhyātvā bhajeyurīśvaraṃ te te sarve vikalmāṣāḥ pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ  SvayambhuP niḥkleśā vimalātmāno bhaveyurbodhibhāginaḥ iti lokādhipaiḥ sarve rbrahmendra pramukhairapi  SvayambhuP sarvānyetāni tīrthāni saṃsevitāni sarvadā tathā ca munibhiḥ sarvestāpa sairbrahmacāribhiḥ  SvayambhuP yatibhiryogibhiścāpi tīrthikaiḥ śrāvakai rapi brāhmaṇai vaiṣṇavaiḥ śaivaiḥ kaulikairapi śaktikairapi  SvayambhuP devaiśca dānavaiścāpi yakṣagandharvakinnaraiḥ guhyaka siddhasādhyai śca grahaiḥ vidyādharairapi  SvayambhuP apsarobhiśca sarvābhiḥ sadā saṃsevitāni hi nāgendrai rgaruḍaiścāpi kumbhāṇḍai rākṣasairapi  SvayambhuP evamanyairapripretya sevitāni śubhārthibhiḥ grahaiścaḥ sāṃdhikaiścāpi vratiścāpyupāsakaiḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvai rmunīndraiśca sevitāni jagaddhite ahamapitathaiteṣu tīrtheṣu samupāśrayan  SvayambhuP snātvā dānāni datvā ca kṛtvā yajñaṃ yathāvidhi pitṛnsatarpayitvāpi samabhyarcya surānapi  SvayambhuP triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā prācaraṃ poṣadha vraṃtaṃ dharmmadhātuṃ samārādhya smṛtvā dhyātvā samāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP japitvā dhāraṇī mantraṃ pracaranbodhisamvaraṃ etat puṇyānubhāvena pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ  SvayambhuP niḥkleśo nirmmalātmohaṃ caturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ bhadraśrī sadguṇāddhirmān  SvayambhuP āśu saṃbodhiṃ saṃbhāra pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ jitvā māragaṇānsarvān kalāvapi jagaddhite  SvayambhuP travidhabodhimāsādya saṃbuddho dharmmarātbhuve thuyamapijñātvāni vighna bodhi prāptaye  SvayambhuP sarveṣu teṣu tīrtheṣu pravadhvaṃ yathāvidhiḥ dharmmadhātuṃ sadābhyarcya smṛtvā dhyātvā samāhitāḥ  SvayambhuP japitvā dhāraṇīmantraṃ saṃbhajadhvaṃ jagaddhite etpuṇyu prabhovaṇa pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ  SvayambhuP durggatinnaivagacheta jāyadhvaṃ saṃdgatau sadāṃ tatra sadā triratnāno śaraṇe samupasthitāḥ  SvayambhuP satkārai rbhajana kṛtvā saṃcaradhvaṃ jagaddhite teṣāṃ hi vimalātmānaścaturbrahma vihāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhaveyu bhadracāriṇaḥ tataḥ śrī sadguṇādhārāḥ sarvavidyāvicakṣaṇāḥ  SvayambhuP sarva sattvāhitādhānaṃ saṃcaradhva jagaddhite tataḥ saṃbodhiṃ saṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP āśu tribodhimāsādya prāpsyatha saugataṃ padaṃ ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sarve pravodhitāḥ  SvayambhuP maitreyādi sabhālokāḥ prāpyananda pravodhitāḥ iti śrī svayaṃbhū samutpatti kathāyāṃ aneka tīrtha saṃjāta puṇya mahātmya varṇano nāma pañcamo dhyāya ṣaṣṭhama adhyāyaḥ svayambhūdharmadhātuvāgīśvarābhidhānaprasiddhapravartano nāmaathāsau ca mahāsattvo maitreyaḥ sugatātmajaḥ munīndraṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā sāñjalirevamabravīt  SvayambhuP yadasya bhagavan dharmmadhātu vāgīśvarābhidhaṃ prasiddha hetunā kena tatsamādeṣṭumarhati  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthite tenaḥ maitreyeṇa sa sarvavit bhagavānstaṃ mahāsattvaṃ saṃpaśyannidamādiśat  SvayambhuP yenāsya hetunā dharmmadhātu vāgīśvarābhidhaṃ prasiddhiṃ tatpravakṣāmi śṛṇu maitreya sādaraṃ  SvayambhuP tadyathāyuryadā nṛṇāṃ triṃśadvarṣa sahasrike śobhāvatyāṃ mahāpūryāmudapādi tadā jinaḥ  SvayambhuP saṃbuddho rhañjagacchāstā dharmmarājo munīśvaraḥ kanaka munīrityākhyāstathāgato vināyakaḥ  SvayambhuP tadāhaṃ kulaputro sa sudharmmākhya ātmavit bodhisattvo mahāsattvo dharmmaśrī sadguṇārthabhṛt  SvayambhuP sa kanakamuneḥ śāstuḥ śāsane samupāśritaḥ triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvāḥ prācaram bodhisaṃvaraṃ  SvayambhuP yadā ca bhagavāñchāstā śobhāvatyā upāśrame vihāre śobhitārāme vijahāra sa sāṃghikaḥ  SvayambhuP tadā tatra sabhāloke brahmendra pramukhāḥ surāḥ sarvalokādhipāścāpi dharmmaṃ śrotumudāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP sarve grahāśca tārāśca sarvā vidyādharā api siddhāḥ sādhyāśca rudrāśca munayo pi maharṣayaḥ  SvayambhuP gandharvāḥ kinnarā yakṣā guhyakā rākṣasā api kumbhāṇḍā garuḍā nāgā daityāścāpi samāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP yatayo yoginaścāpi tīrthikāśca tapasvinaḥ pākhaṇḍāśca parivrājako nirgranthā brahmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP śramaṇāḥ śrāvakāścāpi vratinaścāpyupāsakāḥ tatsaddharmmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sādaraṃ samupāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP brāhmaṇā kṣatriyā ścāpi vaiśyāśca mantriṇojanāḥ gṛhādhipāśca śreṣṭāścaḥ bhṛtyāḥ sainyādhipā api  SvayambhuP śilpino vaṇijaścāpi sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ paurā jānapadā grāmyāḥ kārpaṭikāśca śairikāḥ  SvayambhuP tathānya vāsinaścāpi sarvalokāḥ prasāditāḥ tatsaddharmmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sādaraṃ samupāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP tānsarvānsamupāyātān dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavānmudā sabhā madhyāsanāsīnastasthau dhyātvā prabhāsayan  SvayambhuP taṃ munīndraṃ prabhākāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve pi sāṃdhikāḥ śravaṇāḥ śrāvakāḥ sarve bhikṣavo brahmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP bhikṣuṇyo brahmacāriṇyo upāsikāśca cailikāḥ cailakā vratinaścāpi dharmakāmā upāsakāḥ  SvayambhuP sarve pi te samāgatya praṇatvā taṃ munīśvaraṃ parivṛtya pariskṛtya dharmma śrotumupāśrayan  SvayambhuP tato brahmadayo devāḥ sarve lokādhipā api taṃ munīndraṃ samabhyarcya praṇatvā ca yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP parivṛtya puraskṛtya tatsabhāyāṃ samantataḥ saṃpaśyantaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste mānavāḥ sarve ṛṣi vipranṛpādayaḥ taṃ munīndraṃ samabhyarcya saṃpraṇatvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP tatsabhāṃ samupāśritya parivṛtya samantataḥ puraskṛtya samudvīkṣya saṃtasthire samāhitāḥ  SvayambhuP tatastān samupāsīnān dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavān mudā āryasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmma samupāsadit  SvayambhuP kramena bodhicaryāgamāryāṣṭāṃṅga ca satpathaṃ ādiśya bodhimārge tān sarvāllokān yojayet  SvayambhuP tatsaddharmmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ pravodhitāḥ saddharmma sādhanā yuktā babhūvu rbodhimānasāḥ  SvayambhuP tadā vikramaśīlākhye vihāre bhikṣurātmavit sasaṃghā vyaharad dharmmaśrīmitrākhyaḥ sudhīryatiḥ  SvayambhuP sa tatra sarvalokānāṃ hitārthena samāśritaḥ sa saṃghā nāmasaṃgītiṃ vyākhyātumabhyavāñchata  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa satmatiḥ sarvān saṃghā nāma prasādaraṃ sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnastasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP taṃ sabhāsana āsīnaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve pi sāṃghikāḥ tatsaddharmmāmṛtaṃ pātumicchataḥ samupāgatāḥ  SvayambhuP tatra ye yatiṃ natvā parivṛtya samantataḥ puraskṛtya samīkṣanta upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  SvayambhuP tatrānye pi samāyātā lokadvijanṛpādayaḥ vaiśyāśca mantrino mātyāḥ bhṛtyā sainyādhipā api  SvayambhuP śilpino vanijaścāpi sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ paurā jānapadāgrāmyāstathānyadeśavāsinaḥ  SvayambhuP sarve te samupāgatya praṇatvā taṃ yatiṃ mudā parivṛtya puraskṛtya sapaśyantamupāśrayan  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa yatirālokya sarvānstānsamupāśritān mañjuśrīnāma saṃgītiṃ samākhyātaṃ yathātkramāt  SvayambhuP tatsamādiṣṭamākarṇyaṃ sarve lokāḥ sabhāśritāḥ saṃbuddha guṇamahātmyaṃ matvānandapravodhitāḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ sarve pi lokāste brāhmaṇa bhūmipādayaḥ natvā taṃ yatimāmantrya svasvālayaṃ mudāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP tataste śrāvakā vijñā yatayo brahmacāriṇaḥ dvādaśākṣara guhyārthaṃ samyak śrotuṃmamīcchire  SvayambhuP tataste yoginaḥ sarve kṛtāñjali puṭā mudā śāstāraṃ taṃ yatiṃ natvā samāmatryaivamavruvan  SvayambhuP bhadanta dvādaśānāṃ yadakṣarāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ viśuddhiṃ śrotumicchāmastatsamādeṣṭumarhati  SvayambhuP iti tai rprārthitaṃ dharmmaśrī mitraḥ sasudhīrapi dvādaśākṣara guhyārthaṃ viśuddhiṃ na samādiśat  SvayambhuP taṃ viśuddhā nabhijñātā viṣaṇṇātmā sa utthitaḥ dhyānāgāraṃ samāsīno dhyātvaivaṃ samacintayan  SvayambhuP naitadakṣaraṃ guhyārthaṃ viśuddhirjñāyate mayā tatkathaṃ upadekṣyāmi hāhā kutra bhrameyahi  SvayambhuP iti cintā viṣarṇṇo tmā lajjā saṃmohitāśayaḥ smṛtvā ratnatrayaṃ dhyātvā tasthau dhairyasamāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP tatkṣaṇe sa triratnānāṃ smṛti puṇyānubhāvataḥ evaṃ matiṃ mahāvīrya mahotsāhinimāptavān  SvayambhuP tatastatmati śauṇḍau sauḥ puna dhyātvā samāhitaḥ manasā sarva lokeṣu vicārayan vyalokayan  SvayambhuP tadāpaśyanmahācīne uttarasyāṃ nagottame mañjuśrīyaṃ mahābhijñaṃ sarva vidyādhipeśvaraṃ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvaṃ sarva dharmmādhipaprabhuṃ sarva guhya viśuddhārtha vijñānajñānadāyakaṃ  SvayambhuP taṃ paśyan manasā dharmmaśrī mitraḥ samutsukaḥ sahasotthāya tānsaṃghān sabhāmantryaivamavravīt  SvayambhuP bho bhadanto gamiṣyāmi mahācīne nagottame mañjuśrīyaṃ mahāsattvaṃ draṣṭumicchāmi sāṃprataṃ  SvayambhuP etasyā nāmasaṃgītyā guhya viśuddhi vistaraṃ pṛṣṭā samyak vijñāya āgamiṣyāmyahaṃ drutaṃ  SvayambhuP yāvannāhamihāyāta stāvatsarve samāhitāḥ triratna bhajanaṃ kṛtvā tiṣṭhata mā viṣīdata  SvayambhuP ityuktvā sa mahābhijñastataḥ saṃprasthito drutaṃ sañcarannatra nepālaviṣaye samupāyayau  SvayambhuP tamāyātaṃ yatiṃ natvā mañjudevaḥ sa sarvavit svāntike samupādraṣṭumecchat ṛddhiṃ pradarśayan  SvayambhuP tataḥ maṃjudevo pi bhūtvā kṛṣikaraḥ svayaṃ śārdūla mṛgarājābhyāṃ halenākarṣayan mahīṃ  SvayambhuP taṃ dṛṣṭvā dūrato dharmmaśrīmitro ativismitaḥ kimetat mahadāścaryamitidraṣṭumuyācarat  SvayambhuP tataḥ samupāśritya dṛṣṭvā tanmahadadbhutaṃ kṛṣikaraṃ tamāmantryapapracchaiva vyavalokayan  SvayambhuP bho sādho ito deśānmahācīna nagoktamaḥ pañcaśīrṣaḥ kiyaddūre tadupadeṣṭumarhati  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śrutvā sa halavāhakaḥ suciraṃ taṃ yatiṃ paśyansādaramevamavravīt  SvayambhuP yattvaṃ kuta ihāyāsi kimarthamuktarāpathe mahācīnasya dūrato gantuṃ tvaṃ paripṛccha se  SvayambhuP adya pravartate sāyaṃ tad vihāre mamāśrame uṣitvā prāta rutthāya gaccha maddeśitātpathaḥ  SvayambhuP iti tenoditaṃ dharmaśrī mitro niśaṃmya saḥ tathetyanumataṃ dhṛtvā tūṣṇīṃ bhūtvā vyatiṣṭhataḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ saṃbodhitaṃ bhikṣu matvā sa halavāhakaḥ tau śārdula mṛgendro dvautatraivāntavyardhāpayet  SvayambhuP halaṃ tu sarvalokānāṃ saṃpravodhana hetunā tatraivocca sthala kṣetre yūpa vadavaropayat  SvayambhuP adyāpi tatmahīsthānaṃ mañjuśrībhūḥ prasidhyate sāvāceti prasiddhā ca yatrāvaropitaṃ halaṃ  SvayambhuP tatastaṃ yatimāhuya sāyaṃ sa halavāhakaḥ tatra praviśya dharmaśrīmitra saṃprati vismitaḥ  SvayambhuP tato mūlaphala skandha patrādi bhogamādarāt datvā tasmai svayaṃ bhuktvā tasthau sa halavāhakaḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa vividhāṃ dharmmaśrīmitrorajanī kathāṃ bhāṣitvā taṃ mahābhijñaṃ kṛṣikaraṃ vyanodayan  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa mañjudevastaṃ yati chātrālaye niśi preṣayitvā svayaṃ gahvāgāre śayyāṃ samāśrayat  SvayambhuP tatra praviśya dharmmaśrī mitra saṃprati vismitaḥ suptvākṣaṇaṃ samutthāya manasaivaṃ vyacintayat  SvayambhuP nādyātra śayanīyaṃ yadayaṃpumānmaharddhikaḥ bhāryāyā sahasākathyaṃ kiṃkiṃ kuryād vinodayaṃ  SvayambhuP iti dhyātvā sadharmmaśrīmitra yatirutthitaḥ saṃvara nibhṛtaṃ tasya dvāramūlamupāśrayet  SvayambhuP tatkṣaṇe mañjudevaṃ taṃ keśinī supriyā satī śayāsanasamāsīnā bharktāramevamavravīt  SvayambhuP svāminko yaṃ yati rdhīmānkimarthamasmadāśrame iha kutaḥ samāyāta statsamādeṣdumarhati  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthitaṃ devyā mañjudevo niśamya saḥ keśinīṃ tāṃ priyāṃ bhāryāṃ sampaśyannevamavravīt  SvayambhuP sādhu śṛṇu priye devī yadartha yamimihāgataḥ tadartha hi mahaddhetuṃ vakṣyāmi te vicārayat  SvayambhuP ayaṃ bhikṣu mahābhijño bodhisattvo mahāmatiḥ vikhyāto yo mahādharmmaśrīmitrobhidho yati  SvayambhuP vikramaśīla ākhyāte vihāre sa nivāsakaḥ nāmasaṃgīti vyākhyānaṃ śikṣebhyo vistaraṃ vyadhāt  SvayambhuP dvādaśākṣara guhyārtha viśuddhi jñāna vistaraṃ nāma samyagupākhyātuṃ śaknoti na sudhīrapi  SvayambhuP tadāyaṃ ca viṣaṇṇātmāḥ dhyānāgāre samāśritaḥ dhyātvā lokeṣu sarvatra vilokyaivaṃ vyacintayan  SvayambhuP mañjuśrī reva jānīyātsarva guhya viśuddhivit dvādaśākṣara guhyārtha viśuddhiṃ samupādiśat  SvayambhuP iti dhyātvā samutthāya sarvān śiṣyānsa sāṃghikān bodhayitvā mahotsāhaḥ vīryeṇa pracāraktataḥ  SvayambhuP uktarasyāṃ mahācīne pañcaśīrṣesmadāśrame gantumanena mārggeṇa carannīha samāgataḥ  SvayambhuP tamiha samayāyātaṃ dṛṣṭvā samṛddhibhāvataḥ bodhayitvaivamāhuyoḥ nayāmi svāśrame dhunā  SvayambhuP iti bhaktā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sā keśinī priyā svāminaṃ taṃ samālokya papracchaivaṃ samādarāt  SvayambhuP svāminahaṃ na jānāmi śṛṇomi na kadācana kathametadviśuddhyarthaṃ samupādiśa me dhunā  SvayambhuP iti saṃprāthitaṃ devyā mañjudevo niśamya saḥ keśinīṃ tāṃ priyāṃ bhāryā sampaśyannevamavravīt  SvayambhuP sādhu devī tava prītyā sāmpratamupadiśyate etadartha mahāguhyaṃ gopanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ  SvayambhuP ityuktvā mañjudevo sau tasyai devyai yathāvidhiḥ dvādaśākṣara guhyārthaṃ viśuddhi samupādiśat  SvayambhuP etatsarva samākhyātaṃ vistaraṃ sa mahāmatiḥ dharmaśrīmitra ākarṇya prātyananda pravodhitaḥ  SvayambhuP tata samudito dharmmaśrī mitra utthite mudā mañjuśrīrayameveti niścayaṃ samupāyayau  SvayambhuP tataḥ sasuprasannātmā dvāramūle kṛtāñjaliḥ aṣṭāṃga praṇatiṃ kṛtvā tasthau tadgata mānasaḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ prātaḥ samutthāya keśinī mokṣadāyanī dvārakapāramudadhāṭayaḥ vahirgantumupākramat  SvayambhuP tatra taṃ yatimālokya dvāramūle vyavasthitaṃ bhītā sā keśinī devī drutamupācaratprabhoḥ  SvayambhuP tāṃ pratyāgatāṃ dṛṣṭvā mañjudevaḥ sa sarvavit vibhinnāsyāṃ samālokya papracchaivaṃ adhīravat  SvayambhuP devī kiṃdvāramudhyāṭya sattvaraṃ tvamupāgatāḥ dṛṣṭvā kiṃ tatra bhītāsi tatsatyaṃ vada me puraḥ  SvayambhuP iti pṛṣṭe jagacchāstā bharktā sā keśinī virāt svāminaṃ taṃ samālokya śanairevaṃnyavedayet  SvayambhuP svāminyati namaskṛtvā dvāramūle nipātitaḥ jīvito vā mṛtau vāsau mayā na jñāyate khalu  SvayambhuP ityuktaṃ bhāryayā śrutvā mañjudevaḥ sa utthitaḥ upetya dvāramūle taṃ saṃdadarśa nipātitaṃ  SvayambhuP dṛṣṭvā sa mañjudevastaṃ yatiṃ dhyātvā jitendriyaṃ hastaṃ dhṛtvā samutthāya saṃpaśyannevavravīt  SvayambhuP yate kimarthamatraivaṃ dvāraṃ dhyātvāvatiṣṭhasi tatmamapurataḥ sabhyaṃ vadaya te samāhitaṃ  SvayambhuP ityuktvā mañjudeveṃna dharmaśrīmitra unmanāḥ mañjuśriyantamaṣṭāṃgainatvaivaṃ prārthayanmudā  SvayambhuP bhagavannātha sarvajña sarvavidyādhipa prabho bhavatpādāmbuje bhaktyā śaraṇe samupāśraye  SvayambhuP bhavāneva jagacchāstā mañjuśrīrbhagavānapi jñāyate dṛśyate hyatra jñānaratnanidhi rmayā  SvayambhuP tad bhavāhni vijānīte yadarthehamihā vraja tatmebhivāṃcchitaṃ śāstāḥ saṃpūrayitumarhati  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena mañjudeva niśamya sa vijñāya taṃ mahābhijñaṃ saṃpaśyannevamavravīt  SvayambhuP kathaṃ vinā abhiṣekaṃ te mantrārthamupadeśyate  SvayambhuP tāvadatrabhiṣeka tvaṃ gṛhvāṇhedaṃ yadīcchasi ityuktaṃ mañjudevena niśamya sa yatiḥ sudhīḥ  SvayambhuP mañjudevaṃ namostasya sāñjalirevamavravīt sarvajña bhagavāñchāstā nirdhano hamakiṃcanaḥ  SvayambhuP kiṃ dāsye bhavataṃ śāstre dakṣiṇāṃ guru bhaktimān iti tenoditaṃ śrutvāḥ mañjudevaḥ sasanmatiḥ  SvayambhuP saṃpaśyansteyatī dharmaśrīmitramevamavravīt yataḥ kiṃ dhanasaṃpatyā śraddhā te yadi vidyate  SvayambhuP tuṣyante guruvo bhaktimātreṇātra dhanenatu ityuktvā mañjudevena dharmaśrīmitra unmatāḥ  SvayambhuP aṣṭāṃgestaṃ guruṃ natvā prārthayadevamādarāt bhagavanyadi bhaktyaiva tuṣyate tra bhavān mama  SvayambhuP bhavatāṃ suśrūṣāmeṣa karomi bhaktimānahaṃ iti me kṛpayā śāsta abhiṣeka yathāvidhiḥ  SvayambhuP datvā dvādaśa mantrārthaṃ viśuddhi dātumarhasi iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena mañjudevaṃ sa sarvavit  SvayambhuP bhaktimanta tamālokya paṇyamevamabhāṣata dāsyāmi te mahābhāga bhakti śraddhāsti te yadi  SvayambhuP abhiṣeka prasannātmā samādatsva samāhitaḥ tataḥsa mañjudevaḥ śrī vajrācārya yathāvidhi  SvayambhuP saṃsthāpya maṇḍalaṃ dharmadhātuvāgīśvarābhidhaṃ tanmaṇḍalaṃ samārādhya samabhyarcya yathāvidhiṃ  SvayambhuP abhiṣekaṃ prasannāya tasmai dadau sa vajradhṛk tatastān maṇḍale devān saṃdarśayaṃ yathākramāt  SvayambhuP pūjayitvā yathāśakti śaraṇe samayojayet tatastasmai prasannāya mañjudevo yathāvidhi  SvayambhuP dvādaśākṣara guhyārtha viśuddhisamupādiśat tato labdhābhiṣeko sau dharmaśrīmitra utmanā  SvayambhuP dvādaśabhūmi guhyārtha viśuddhijñānamāptavān tasmai śāstre sabhāryāya svamātmānaṃ sa dakṣiṇāṃ  SvayambhuP saṃkalpya śraddhayā bhaktyā natvaivaṃ prārthayan mudā bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavat kṛpā prasādataḥ  SvayambhuP saṃprāptapūrṇa saṃkalpo bhavāmi śrīguṇārthabhṛt tat sadāhaṃ bhavatpādaśaraṇe samupāśritaḥ  SvayambhuP yathātra bhavādiṣṭaṃ tathaiva saṃcare bhave tat me nujñādi datvātra saṃbodhijñānasādhanaṃ  SvayambhuP sarvasattva hitārthena careyaṃ bodhisaṃvaraṃ iti saṃprārthya dharmaśrī mitra sa samupāśritaḥ  SvayambhuP śraddhābhakti prasannātmā gurusevā paro bhavat tataḥ sa mañjudevastaṃ mahāsattvaṃ vicakṣaṇaṃ  SvayambhuP matvā saṃbodhi caryāyāṃ niyoktuṃ saṃvyanodayan sādhu sādhu mahābhāgaḥ saṃcaratvaṃ jagaddhite  SvayambhuP saṃbodhi sādhanaṃ bodhicaryā vrata sadā bhava etatpuṇyābhi liptātmā pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahābhijñā bhaveḥ śrī sadguṇāśrayāḥ tatastvaṃ bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP niḥkleśo bodhiprāpto haṃ sambuddhapadamāpnuyāḥ iti me śāsanaṃ dhṛtvā smṛtvā dhyātvā samāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP triratnaṃ samupāśritya saṃcarasva jagaddhite yadi jagaddhitaṃ kartuṃ saṃbodhiṃ prāpnumicchasi  SvayambhuP saddharmaṃ samupādiśya sarvān lokān pravodhaya tatastān bodhitān sarvān kamena bodhisādhanaṃ  SvayambhuP bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya cārayasva jagaddhite tatasteṣāṃ samālokya cittaṃ saṃbodhi niścitaṃ  SvayambhuP triyānaṃ samupādiśya paramārthe niyojaye evaṃ kṛtvā mahaddharmamāśu sambodhisādhanaṃ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrī sadguṇāpannāṃ samāpnuyā jagacchubhe tenāśuḥ pariśuddhātmā sambuddhapadamāptavān  SvayambhuP jagaddharmmamayaṃ kṛtvā jinālayaṃ samāpnuyāḥ iti bhadravrataṃ dhṛtvā gatvā tvaṃ svāśrame punaḥ  SvayambhuP vyākhyāya nāma saṃgītiṃ saddharmmaṃ saṃpracāraye ahamapi mahāsattva śrotuṃ tvad dharmmadeśanāṃ  SvayambhuP sāṃghikāṃścāpi tāndruṣṭumāyāsyāmi tavāśrame iti śāstā samādiṣṭaṃ niśaṃmya sa mahāmatiḥ  SvayambhuP dharmaśrī mitra ālokyaḥ taṃ gurumevamavravīt maharddhiko bhagavāñchāsta vijñāsya te kathaṃ mayā  SvayambhuP iti cihnaṃ samādhāya tatrāgantuṃ samarhati iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā mañjudevaḥ sa sanmati  SvayambhuP dharmaśrī mitramālokyaḥ punarevamabhāṣata vatsāhamutpalaṃ dhṛtvā samāyāsyāmi te sabhāṃ  SvayambhuP tena cihnena māṃ yāta saṃjānīṣva samāgataṃ iti satyaṃ samādhāya dhṛtvānuśāsanaṃ mama  SvayambhuP saddharmma samupādeṣṭuṃ pravāhi testu maṃgalaṃ iti śāstā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa yatirutsukaḥ  SvayambhuP śāstāraṃ taṃ samālokya praṇatvaivamabhāṣataḥ prasīdatu bhagavāñchāstāḥ kṣantumarhati cāgasaṃ  SvayambhuP bhavatprasādataḥ sarve sidhyate me samīhitaṃ tadanuśāsanaṃ dhṛtvā bhavatāṃ tatra jagaddhite  SvayambhuP vyākhyātuṃ nāmasaṃgīti saṃcare sāmprataṃ guroḥ iti saṃprārthya dharmmaśrī mitra saḥ saṃprāsāditaḥ  SvayambhuP śāstustasya padāmbhojaṃ natvā saṃprasthito tataḥ mātrorācārya yāścāpi mokṣadā varadākhyayoḥ  SvayambhuP pādāmvujeṣu saṃnatvā saṃprasthitaḥ pramoditaḥ tataḥ sa sanmati dharmmaśrīmitraḥ sahasāvrajan  SvayambhuP āśu svāśramamāsādya vihāraṃ samupāviśat tatra taṃ yatimāyātaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve pi sāṃghikāḥ  SvayambhuP praṇatvā kuśalaṃ pṛṣṭavā praveśayan nijālaye tataḥ paredyurāmantraya sarvānsaṃghānsa sanmatiḥ  SvayambhuP vyākhyātuṃ nāmasaṃgīti sabhāsanaṃ samāśrayat taṃ sabhāsanamāsīnaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve pi sāṃdhikāḥ  SvayambhuP divja bhūpādayaścāpi sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ tatra sarve pi te lokāḥ praṇatvā taṃ yati kramāt  SvayambhuP parivṛtya puraskṛtya samantata upāśrayat tān sarvānsamupāsīnān dṛṣṭvā sa yatirātmavit  SvayambhuP vyākhyāya nāmasaṃgītiṃ sa viśuddhi samādiśat tadā tatra manastasya jijñāsituṃ sa mañjuvāk  SvayambhuP dhṛtvotpalaṃ vinidyāṃgaḥ kucīvaramupācarat tatra sa makṣikān kāye utpalena nivārayan  SvayambhuP samāgatya sabhaikānte paśyallokānupāśrayet samāśritaṃ sa dharmmaśrīmitro dṛṣṭvātmanā guruṃ  SvayambhuP utpalena parijñāya manasaivaṃ vyacintayat aho nūnamayaṃ śāstā mano jijñāsituṃ mama  SvayambhuP kucarā durbhagākāro dhṛtvotpalamihāgataḥ tatkathamahamutthāya pratyuṅgamya na meya hi  SvayambhuP atha paśyannamaskāraṃ nakuryāḥ gurave kathaṃ yadyatrāhaṃ samutthāya na meyamenamādarāt  SvayambhuP dṛṣṭvā lokā ime māṃ dhikkuryuḥ sarve vicārataḥ ete na jñāyate yaṃ hi mañjuśrī ṛddhimānapi  SvayambhuP īdṛgevāsya śāstā yaṃ miti me syād vihāsyatāṃ iti dhyātvā sa dharmmaśrīmitro lajjābhimohitaḥ  SvayambhuP manasaivaṃ namaskṛtvā śāstārantamamānayet tataḥ sa vimukhī bhūya paśyannapya vibhāvitaḥ  SvayambhuP ajñāta vānnivāpaśyan padamātramupādiśat tataḥ sarve pi te lokāḥ śrutvā tatsaddharmmadeśanāṃ  SvayambhuP utthāya taṃ yatiṃ natvā svasvālayamupācaran tata loke gate dharmmaśrī mitraḥ sa samutthitaḥ  SvayambhuP śāstāraṃ taṃ samālokya vandituṃ samupācarat taṃ dṛṣṭvā mañjudevo sau vandituṃ samupāgataṃ  SvayambhuP apaśyan vimukhī bhūya tataḥ saṃprasthito carat taṃ dṛṣṭvā vimukhī bhūta dharmmaśrī mitra ātmanaḥ  SvayambhuP aparādha mahatpāpamanusmṛtvāpatadbhuvi nipatantaṃ tamālokya mañjuśrīḥ sa kṛpānidhiḥ  SvayambhuP sahasā pāṇinā dhṛtvā samutthāya tathācarat tatra sa utthito dharmmaśrī mitrastaṃ mahāmatiṃ  SvayambhuP pracarantaṃ samālokya natvāhaivaṃ mṛṣā
