mudā tataścedaṃ sa saṃvīkṣya mañjudevasya nirmmitaṃ  SvayambhuP caityamabhyarcya saṃstutvā gītairnatvā bhajan mudā tato sau ca mahādevī yonirūpāṃ khagānanāṃ  SvayambhuP samālokya prasannātmā yathāvidhi samarccayet tatrāpi sa mahāsattva stutvā gītairmanoharaiḥ  SvayambhuP aṣṭāṅgaiḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇātyanekaśaḥ śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatvā smṛtvā dhyātvā samāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP tad vidyā dhāraṇīmantraṃ japitvā prābhyanandata tato sau ca mahāsattvo vāgmatīpramukhānyapi  SvayambhuP tīrthānyetāni sarvāṇi sa samīkṣya prābhyanandata tata sa teṣu tīrtheṣu sarveṣvapi yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP snātvā dānavratādīni kṛtvā bhajan pramoditaḥ tato ṣṭau vītarāgāṃśca dṛṣṭvā sa saṃpraharṣitaḥ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya stutvā natvā bhajan kramāt tataḥ pracaṇḍadevaḥ sa bodhisattvaḥ prasāditaḥ  SvayambhuP atraiva sarvadāśritya vrataṃ caritumaicchata tataḥ sa vimalālokya himālaye samantataḥ  SvayambhuP saddharma paramānandaṃ bhuktvotsahe sunivṛttau tataḥ sa mañjudevasya śiṣyaṃ śāsana sambhṛtaṃ  SvayambhuP sadguruṃ samupāśritya prārthayadevamānataḥ bhadantātra puṇyakṣetre mahāpīṭhe himālaye  SvayambhuP prabrajyāsambaraṃ dhṛtvā saṃsthātumutsahe sadāḥ tad bhavān kṛpayā mahayaṃ saṃbodhijñānasādhanaṃ  SvayambhuP prabrajyāsamvaraṃ dātuṃ samarhati jagaddhite iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena niśamya sa guṇākaraḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvaṃ suvijñaṃ taṃ sampaśyannevamabravīt ehi bhadra samīcchā te yadyasti bauddhasambare  SvayambhuP pravajyā vratamādhāya saṃcarasva samāhitaḥ ityuktvā sa mahābhijñaḥ pravrajitaṃ vidhāya taṃ  SvayambhuP bodhicaryāvrataṃ datvā pracārayejjagaddhite tatra sa muṇḍitapātrī surakta cīvarāvṛtaḥ  SvayambhuP brahmacārī yatirbhikṣuniḥ kleśorhan sudhīrabhūt śāntaśrībhikṣuriti nāmo bhūt tataḥ sa sarvavicchāstā bodhisattvā hitārthadik  SvayambhuP sa devāsuralokānāmapi vandyārcito bhavat tadārabhya sa śāntaśrīdharmadhāto jinālaye  SvayambhuP triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā tasthau bodhivrataṃ caran sa ekasmin dine cemaṃ jyotīrūpaṃ prabhāsvaraṃ  SvayambhuP ratnapadmāsanāsīnaṃ paśyannevaṃ vyacintayet aho hyayaṃ svayaṃ jāto jyotirūpo prabhāsvaraḥ  SvayambhuP ratnapadmāsanāsīnaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate jagaddhite kiyatkālamayaṃ śrīmān dharmmadhāturjinālayaḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ saṃbhāṣayan lokān saṃsthāsyate jagaddhite yataḥ kalau samayā te loka pañcakaṣāyite  SvayambhuP sarve lokā durācārā bhaviṣyanti durāśayāḥ madābhimānino duṣṭā lobhinaḥ kāmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP īrṣyālavaḥ pramattāśca mātsaryavyākulāśayāḥ kleśāhaṃkāragarvāndhā nirvivekāḥ pramādinaḥ  SvayambhuP kāmabhogātisaṃraktā daśākuśalacāriṇaḥ tadā kathamayaṃ śrīmān jyotīrūpaḥ prabhāsvaraḥ  SvayambhuP ratnapadmāsanāsīna evaṃ tiṣṭhejjagaddhite nūnaṃ ye lobhino duṣṭāḥ kleśavyākulamānasāḥ  SvayambhuP imaṃ caityaṃ pratikṣipya ratnāni saṃharet tadā duṣṭā ca tathānye pi duṣṭāḥ kleśābhimāninaḥ  SvayambhuP jyotīrūpamimaṃ caityaṃ dhvaṃsayiṣyanti sarvathā evaṃ tadā kalau kāle dhvaṃsite smin jinālaye  SvayambhuP mahāpātakasaṃbhūtaṃ mahotpātaṃ bhaved dhruvaṃ iti hetorahaṃ dharmadhātorasya surakṣaṇe  SvayambhuP guptikarttu śilāchādya caityaṃ kuryā mahochrayaṃ tadā sarve pi lokāste imaṃ stūpaṃ mahochritaṃ  SvayambhuP samīkṣya śraddhayā bhaktyā bhajiṣyanti prasāditāḥ tadaitat puṇyabhāvena sarvadātra samantataḥ  SvayambhuP subhikṣaṃ maṅgalotsāhaṃ nirutpātaṃ bhaved dhruvaṃ iti dhyātvā sa śāntaśrīḥ śāstāraṃ taṃ punarmudā  SvayambhuP upetya sāñjalirnatvā prārthayadevamādarāt bhadanta sadgurośāstaryadicchāmiha sāmprataṃ  SvayambhuP dharmmādhātumimaṃ caityaṃ gupti karttuṃ surakṣaṇe tadūrddha śilayāchādya svīṣṭikābhiḥ samuchritaṃ  SvayambhuP stūpaṃ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhāpya sthirīkarttuṃ samutsahe ityatra me bhavāñchāstā gupti kṛtvābhirakṣaṇe  SvayambhuP dharmmadhātoḥ jagadbhartturanujñāṃ dātumarhati iti saṃprārthite tena śāntaśriyā niśamya saḥ  SvayambhuP mahāmatirmahāsattvaṃ taṃ paśyannevamabravīt bhadrasvaṃyambhūvāṃstasya guptikarttuṃ yadīcchasi  SvayambhuP pratyekaṃ śrāvakaṃ yānaṃ muktvā mahati saṃśritaḥ vajrābhiṣekamādāya cara vajravrataṃ punaḥ  SvayambhuP tato mārān vinirjjitya samārādhya jineśvaraṃ saṃprārthya śilayācchādya kuru stūpaṃ samuchritaṃ  SvayambhuP iti śāstā samādiṣṭaṃ niśamya sa pramoditaḥ śāstāraṃ taṃ praṇatvā ca prārthayadevamādarāt  SvayambhuP sadgururme bhavāñchāstā dharmmadhātusurakṣaṇe vajracaryāvrataṃ datvā cāraya māṃ jagaddhite  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthite tena śāntaśriyā niśamya saḥ mahāmatirmahāsattvaṃ taṃ samīkṣyaivamabravīt  SvayambhuP yadi śraddhāsti te bhadra vajracaryā mahāvrataṃ yathāvidhi pradāsyāmi tad gṛhāṇa jagaddhite  SvayambhuP ityuktvā sa mahācāryastasmai śāntaśriye kramāt sābhiṣekaṃ mahāyāne vajracaryāvrataṃ dadau  SvayambhuP śāntaśrīvajrācārya iti sthāpitaḥ tatkṣaṇe rye cādhijñaprāpto bhūt tataḥ prāptābhiṣekaḥ sa śāntaśrī vajrayogavit  SvayambhuP sa svātmā dakṣiṇāṃ tasmai gurave pradadau mudā tataḥ sa vajradhṛg yogī mahābhijñaḥ susiddhimān  SvayambhuP svakuleśaṃ samārādhya sagaṇaṃ prābhajan mudā tataḥ sa vajradhṛg yogī mahābhijñaḥ susiddhimān  SvayambhuP saddharmmasādhanotsāhī sarvavidyādhipopyabhūt tataḥ sāsturanujñāṃ sa samāsādya prasāditaḥ  SvayambhuP dharmadhātuṃ samārādhya prārthayadevamānataḥ bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ rakṣaṇāya yat  SvayambhuP jyotīrūpaṃ samācchādya caityaṃ karttumihotsahe tad bhavān trijagannātha kṛpayā me prasīdatu  SvayambhuP yada trāpyaparārdha me tatsarva kṣantumarhati iti saṃprārthya sa prājña jyotīrūpaṃ jinālayaṃ  SvayambhuP sa ratnapadmāchādya śilayā samagopayat taduparīṣṭikābhiśca vidhāya caityamucchritaṃ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi pratiṣṭhāpya mahotsāhaiḥ sadābhajat tata idañca pucchāgraṃ mañjudevasya nirmmitaṃ  SvayambhuP caityaṃ sa śilayāchādya stūpaṃ vyadhāttathottamaṃ idaṃ stūpaṃ ca sa śāntaśrīḥ pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi  SvayambhuP sarvadā śraddhayā bhaktyā mahotsāhairmudābhajat tataścāsau mahācāryaṃ ārādhya pañcadevatāḥ  SvayambhuP pañca sutāḥ pureṣvevaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sadābhajat tad yathā devatā pañca prathamaṃ vāyudevatā  SvayambhuP vāyupure pratiṣṭhāpya vahnipuro gnidevatā nāgapure ca nāgendro vasupure vasundharāṃ  SvayambhuP śāntipure mahāśrīmatsambaraṃ sugaṇaṃ tathā etān sarvān samārādhya sa ācārya yathāvidhi  SvayambhuP mahotsāhaiḥ samabhyarcya prābhajan sarvadā mudā evaṃ kṛtvā sa ācārya śāntaśrīḥ kṛtakṛtyau maharddhikaḥ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrīmantrasaṃsiddhaḥ sarvavidyādhipo bhavat tato bhūyaḥ sa ācāryo bodhisattvā mahāmatiḥ  SvayambhuP sarvasattvahitotsāhī dhyātvaivaṃ samacintayat atraivamahamārādhya sarvān devān yathāvidhi  SvayambhuP pratiṣṭhāpya samabhyarcya mahotsāhairbhaje mudā tathātra sarvadā dharmmadhātuvāgīśvaraṃ sadā  SvayambhuP smṛtvā dhyātvā samārādhya saṃtiṣṭheyaṃ jagaddhite iti dhyātvā sa śāntaśrīrācāryastriguṇārthabhṛt  SvayambhuP sarvasattvahitārthena tathāvatraiva nanditaḥ evaṃ tā devatā bhaktyā bhajanti ye yathāvidhi  SvayambhuP te bhadraśrīguṇāpannā bhaveyurbodhicāriṇaḥ tad viśeṣaphalaṃ cāpi śṛṇu maitreya sāṃprataṃ  SvayambhuP sarva sattvānubodhārtha vakṣyāmyatra samāsataḥ tadyathā ye samārādhya sagaṇāṃ vāyudevatāṃ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya saṃbhajante samādarāt teṣāṃ vātamahotpātabhayaṃ kvāpi na vidyate  SvayambhuP nīrogyaṃ śrīsamāpannaṃ kāmabhojyaṃ sadā bhave ye cāpyevaṃ samārādhya sagaṇāṃ vahnidevatāṃ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya sambhajante samādarāt teṣāṃ vahnimahotpātaṃ bhayaṃ kvāpi na vidyate  SvayambhuP paripuṣṭendriyārogya mahāsaukhyaṃ sadā bhave ye cāpyevaṃ samārādhya sagaṇāṃ nāgadevatāṃ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya prabhajante sadā mudā teṣāṃ na vidyate kvāpi durbhikṣotpātajaṃ bhayaṃ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrīratnasaṃpattikāmabhojyaṃ sadā bhave ye cāpyevaṃ samārādhya sagaṇāṃ śrībasundharāṃ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya saṃbhajante samādarāt teṣāṃ dāridrayaduḥkhādi bhayaṃ nāsti kadācana  SvayambhuP bhadraśrīsadguṇāpannamahāsaṃpatsukhaṃ sadā ye cāpyevaṃ samārādhya sagaṇaṃ sambaraṃ jinaṃ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya saṃbhajante sadādarāt teṣāṃ mārāpasargga ca bhayaṃ kvāpi na vidyate  SvayambhuP saddharmmaratnasaṃpattimahaiśvaryasukhaṃ sadā ye cedaṃ caityamārādhya mañjudevasya nirmmitaṃ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya saṃbhajante samādarāt taddurbhbhagā durācārā duṣṭā syurna kadācana  SvayambhuP sarve dharmādhipā nāthā bhaveyuḥ śrīguṇākarāḥ ye cāpīdaṃ samārādhya dharmmadhātuṃ jinālayaṃ  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya sambhajante samādarāt te sarvve vimalatmāno bhadraśrīsadguṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahābhijñā bhaveyu bodhicāriṇaḥ ya etā devatāḥ sarvāḥ smṛtvā dhyātvāpi sarvadā  SvayambhuP nāmāpi ca samuccārya saṃbhajante samādritāḥ te pi sarve na yāsyanti durggatiṃ ca kadācana  SvayambhuP sadā sadgatisaṃjātā bhaveyuḥ śrīguṇāśrayāḥ tataste sukṛtāraktāḥ sadharmmaguṇalālasāḥ  SvayambhuP triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃcareran sadā śubhe tataste vimalātmānaḥ pariśuddhendriyāśayāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvāścaturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ sarvasattvahitādhānaṃ careyurbodhisambaraṃ  SvayambhuP tataste bodhisaṃbhāraṃ purayitvā yathākramaṃ daśabhūmīśvarā nāthā bhaveyuḥ sugatātmajāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste nirmmalātmānaḥ saṃsāragati niḥspṛhāḥ arhantaḥ savala māraṃ nirjitya syurniraṃjanāḥ  SvayambhuP trividhāṃ bodhimāsādya saddharmmaguṇabhāskarāḥ sarvasattvahitārthena saṃbuddhapadamāpnuyu  SvayambhuP yepyetadguṇamāhātmyaṃ śrutvāpyatyanumoditāḥ tathā tatpuṇyamāhātmyaṃ praśasanti samādarāt  SvayambhuP te pi sarve vikalmāṣāḥ pariśuddhitrimaṇḍalāḥ śrīmantaḥ sadguṇādhārā bhaveyu bodhimānasāḥ  SvayambhuP na yāyurdugatiṃ kvāpi sadā sadgatisambhavāḥ sarvasattvahitaṃ kṛtvā saṃcarerañjagaddhite  SvayambhuP tataḥ sarvādhipāste syu rdhammārthi saṃprapūrakāḥ bodhisaṃbhāraṃ saṃpūrya saṃbuddhapadamāpnuyuḥ  SvayambhuP iti satyaṃ parijñāya bauddhaṃ padaṃ yadīcchatha etān devān samārādhya bhajadhvaṃ sarvadā bhave  SvayambhuP etatpuṇyānubhāvena yūyamapyevamābhavaṃ durggatiṃ naiva yāyāta kadācin kutracid dhruvaṃ  SvayambhuP sadā sadgatisaṃjātā bhadraśrīsadguṇāśrayāḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhavata bodhicāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ saṃbodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ trividhāṃ bodhimāsādya saṃbuddhapadamāpsyatha  SvayambhuP iti matvātra ye lokā rvāñchanti saugataṃ padaṃ sa devān sagaṇāṃ sarvān samārādhya bhajantu te  SvayambhuP ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa niśamya te sabhāśritāḥ sarve tatheti vijñapya prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ  SvayambhuP tadā śāntaśriyā yaṃssaṃ guptikṛto jinālayaḥ ityādiśya munīndro pi samādhiṃ viddhekṣaṇaṃ  SvayambhuP iti śrīsvayaṃbhūdharmmadhātuvāgīśvara guptikṛta pravarttano nāma saptamo dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ aṣṭama adhyāyaḥ svayambhūcaityāśramanāma sādhanāsuvṛṣṭicaraṇo nāmaatha sa bhagavāñchāstā sa samādherutthitaḥ punaḥ maitreyaṃ taṃ sabhāṃ cāpi samālokyaivamādiśat  SvayambhuP śṛṇu maitreya bhūyo syā etad devānubhāvataḥ siddhabhūmeḥ pravakṣāpi mahatsiddhi prabhāvatāṃ  SvayambhuP tadyathātropachandohe siddhaloka himālaya nepāla iti vikhyāte etaddevānubhāvataḥ  SvayambhuP sadā bhadramahotsāhaṃ subhikṣaṃ nirupadravaṃ sarvadravyasamāpanna samṛddhādhamavarttata  SvayambhuP tadā sarvatra lokāśca daśakuśalacāriṇaḥ triratnabhajanāraktāḥ prācarantaḥ sahāśubha  SvayambhuP etatpuṇyānuliptāste caturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ bhadraśrīsadguṇādhīrā babhūvurbodhicāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP evameṣāṃ prasiddhābhūdṛddhisiddhiguṇārthadā ṛddhāsphītā subhikṣā śrīsamāśrayābhiśobhitāḥ  SvayambhuP tenātra yogino vijñā yatayo brahmacāriṇaḥ smṛtvā dhyātvā kuleśānaṃ samārādhya samāśrayan  SvayambhuP tathānye pi sulokāśca samāgatya prasāditāḥ dharmadhātumimaṃ bhaktyā bhajamānāḥ samāśrayan  SvayambhuP sarvaṣvapi ca tīrtheṣu snānadānādi saṃbaraṃ kṛtvāṣṭau vītarāgāṃśca bhajanta samupāśrayan  SvayambhuP etāśca devatāḥ pañca samārādhya yathāvidhi bhajamānā sadotsāhaiḥ prācaranta samāhitāḥ  SvayambhuP tadā khagānanādevīṃ samārādhya yathāvidhi bhajamānā mahotsāhaiḥ prācaranta sadā śubhaṃ  SvayambhuP evamimaṃ ca pucchāgraṃ caityaṃ mañjuśriyāpi te sarve lokāḥ samārādhya prābhajanta prasāditāḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ sarve pi lokāśca saddharmmābhiratā mudā sadā bhadrāṇi karmmāṇi kṛtvātra sarvvadāśrayan  SvayambhuP evameṣāṃ mahāsiddhi bhūmiḥ śrīsaṃpraśobhitāḥ mahājana samākīrṇṇā sarvabhūmyuttamā vabhau  SvayambhuP tataḥ kālāntareṇātra rājā bhūmi yatirnṛpaḥ śrīguṇakāmadevākhya śāstā lokādhipābhavat  SvayambhuP tadā sa nṛpatiḥ prauḍhā yuvā kāmātilālasaḥ yathā kāmarasaṃ bhuktvā prācaran svecchayāraman  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa kṣatriyāpyevaṃ kāmabhāgābhimohitāḥ pramadā guṇasaṃraktā nītidharme nirādaraḥ  SvayambhuP dṛṣṭvā sa sundarīṃ kāntāmagamyāmapi mohitaḥ balenāpi samākṛṣya vubhuje svecchayā mudā  SvayambhuP evaṃ sa nṛparājāpi kāmadharmmātilālasaḥ mantriṣu sarva rājyāṅga niveśya svecchayā ramet  SvayambhuP tataḥ ste mantriṇaḥ sarve nṛpaṃ taṃ pramadā vaśe pratiṣṭhāpya yathākāmaṃ bhuktvā caran yathecchayā  SvayambhuP tathā bhṛtyā janāścāpi sarve pi kleśitāśayāḥ saddharmmāṇi pratikṣipya prācaran kāmabhāginaḥ  SvayambhuP brāhmaṇāśca tathā sarve daśākuśala cāriṇaḥ svakuladharmmamaryādaṃ tyaktvā caran yathecchayā  SvayambhuP vaiśyāścāpi tathā dharmmadravyasaṃgrahalālasāḥ svakulavṛttimutsṛjya bhuktvā caran yathepsitaṃ  SvayambhuP mahājanāstathā sarvepyanyāyadravyasādhinaḥ svakuladharmamutsṛjya bhuktvaiva prācaran sukhaṃ  SvayambhuP vaṇijo pi tathā sarve mithyārthasādhanodyatāḥ satyadharma pratikṣipya ceruḥ kleśābhimānitāḥ  SvayambhuP śilpino pi tathā sarve kavalabhṛtilālasāḥ avidhijñāḥ pramādāndhāścakruḥ karmma yaṃthecchayā  SvayambhuP tathā nārījanāścāpi kāmakleśāḥ kulāśayāḥ svakuladharmamṛtsṛjya prācaranta yathepsitaṃ  SvayambhuP evaṃ sarve pi lokāśca daśākuśalasaṃratāḥ svakulācāramutsṛjya prācaranta yathecchayā  SvayambhuP tīrthikāścāpi ye duṣṭāste dṛṣṭvaivaṃ jinālayaṃ ninditvā paribhāṣantaḥ prācaranta yathecchayā  SvayambhuP tadātra vahavo duṣṭā caurā dhūrttāḥ pragalbhikāḥ sādhujanāḥ pratikṣipya ceru mattadvīpā iva  SvayambhuP sādhavaḥ sajjanāścāpi nīcakarmānucāriṇaḥ saddharmmaviratotsāhāśceru bhuktvaiva nīcavat  SvayambhuP tadaivaṃ pāpasaṃcārāt sarvatrāpyacarat kaliḥ saddharmmo durvalī bhūto nīcavadvilayaṃ yayau  SvayambhuP tadātra pravarībhūte kalisaṃcāra varttate dṛṣṭvā lokādhipāḥ sarve bhavanruṣṭaparānmukhāḥ  SvayambhuP tato tra vimukhībhūya sarvalokādhipā api dhignṛpamiti bā danto draṣṭumapi na cecchire  SvayambhuP tadātra lokapālānāṃ sudṛṣṭiviratotsave ītayaḥ samupākramya prāvarttitumupācarat  SvayambhuP tato devā api krūrā ye duṣṭā mārapākṣikāḥ sarve tatra rūpālokya mahotpātaṃ pracakrire  SvayambhuP vahnirapi tathālokya duṣṭavat kopitāśayaḥ dhūmākulārciṣā dagdhā mahotpātaṃ vyadhādiha  SvayambhuP dharmarājāpi ruṣṭābhūn nirdayāṃ nirujānapi nihantuṃ prāṇinaḥ sarvān mahāmārīmacārayat  SvayambhuP naiṛtyā rākṣasendro pi prakopitātinirdayaḥ sarvatrāpi praviṣṭo tra mahotpātaṃ vyadhātsadā  SvayambhuP varuṇo nāgarājāpi praduṣṭaḥ krūracakṣuṣā dṛṣṭvā vārivahān meghān sarvān vṛṣṭiṃ nyavārayet  SvayambhuP maruto pi tathālokya praruṣṭā nirdayā sthitāḥ asādhyaṃ pracarantātra mahotpātaṃ pracakrire  SvayambhuP tathā yakṣāśca ye duṣṭāḥ kinnarā guhyakā api gṛhe gṛhe praviśyāpi rogotpātaṃ pracakrire  SvayambhuP tathā bhūtāḥ piśācāśca vetālāḥ kaṭapūṭināḥ ḍākiṇyaḥ pramathāścāpi śākinyaḥ sagaṇā api  SvayambhuP rudrā api sagandharvā kumbhāṇḍā garuḍā api sarvatra pracaranto tra mahotpātaṃ pracakrire  SvayambhuP mātṛkā api sarvāśca sagaṇā aprasāditāḥ suduṣṭavālokya sarvān stān drakṣituṃ na samāhire  SvayambhuP grahāstārāgaṇāḥ sarve viruddhā aprasāditāḥ anusaṃdarśanaṃ vāpi kartu naivāvavāṃñchire  SvayambhuP kuleśā api sarvāśca devatā aprasāditāḥ saṃtrāta samarthāstān paśyaṃtya eva tasthire  SvayambhuP evamanyepi devāśca sarvatrāṇaparāṅmukhāḥ teṣāṃ saṃdarśanaṃ kartumapi naiva vāṃchire  SvayambhuP teṣāṃ trātuṃ tadekāpi na śaśāka kathaṃcana evamatra mahotpātaṃ prāvarttata samantataḥ  SvayambhuP evamatra mahotpātaṃ prarvarttate pi sarvataḥ sarvakleśā hatātmānaḥ pracakru vigrahaṃ mithaḥ  SvayambhuP tadevaṃ kalisaṃraktān sarvān lokān vilokya saḥ nṛpatiḥ suciraṃ dhyātvā manasaivaṃ vyacintayat  SvayambhuP hā kaṣṭaṃ pāpajaṃ dhoraṃ jāyate trādhunā mama tatpāpaśamanāyāyaṃ ko dadhānmahitāśayaḥ  SvayambhuP kathamiha mahadduḥkhaṃ śamīkarttuṃ vidhāsyate paśyannevamupekṣyaiva rameyaṃ sāmprataṃ ca kiṃ  SvayambhuP yo hi rājā prajāduḥkhamupekṣya ramate sukhaṃ sa kiṃ rājā prabhurbhattāṃ duṣṭāhivadvigarhyate  SvayambhuP yatra rājā prajāduḥkhamupekṣya na vicārayet svayameva sukhaṃ bhuktvāramaṃścareyathecchayā  SvayambhuP tatra sarvaprajā lokāḥ kleśavyākulamānasāḥ satyadharmakulācāraṃ hitvā careyurauddhaṭāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste duritāraktā daśakuśalacāriṇaḥ mahāpāpe pi nirlajjāḥ saṃcareran yathecchayā  SvayambhuP etat sarva mahatpātaṃ rbhujīyānnṛpatirdhruvaṃ iti satyaṃ samākhyātaṃ nītivijñairmaharṣibhiḥ  SvayambhuP ityetatpāpavaipākyaṃ bhoktavyaṃ hi mayā bhava tadatra kiṃ kariṣyāmi yadupāyaṃ na manyate  SvayambhuP dhig janma me tra saṃsāre yasya rājye sadā kaliḥ durbhikṣādi mahātpātaṃ pravarttate divāniśaṃ  SvayambhuP dhanyāste puruṣā ye hi niḥkleśā vimalāśayā vimukta bhava saṃcārā bhikṣavo brahmacāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP kiṃ me tra janma saṃsāre sukulamapi prabhornṛṇāṃ yadahaṃ paśuvad bhuktvā kāmameva rame gṛhe  SvayambhuP tadetatapāpalipto haṃ kleśavyākulamānasaḥ narakeṣu bhraman duḥkhaṃ bhuṃjīyāṃ vividhaṃ sadā  SvayambhuP tadā ko me suhṛt mitraṃ saṃrakṣitumupācarat dharmameva tadā trāṇaṃ sarvaduḥkhāpahaṃ bhave  SvayambhuP dharmāṇāṃ pravaraṃ bauddhaṃ dharmaṃ sarvabhayāpahaṃ sarvārthasādhanaṃ siddhamityākhyātaṃ jagaddhitaṃ  SvayambhuP ityahaṃ sāmprataṃ gatvā gośṛṅge parvate sthitaṃ śāntaśriyaṃ mahācāryaṃ prārthayeyaṃ samādarāt  SvayambhuP sa eva hi mahācārya etadutpātaśāntaye vidhānaṃ samupādiśya kuryānme tra hitaṃ sadā  SvayambhuP iti niścitya bhūpālaḥ purohitaṃ samantriṇaḥ mahājanāna sapaurāṃśca samāmantrayaivamādiśat  SvayambhuP bho bhavanto yadatraivaṃ mahotpātaṃ pravarttate tacchāntikaraṇaṃ dharmaṃ karttumicchāmi sāṃprataṃ  SvayambhuP tadācārya mahābhijñaṃ śāntiśriyaṃ samādarāt prārthayitvā tadā deśād dharttumicchāmi sadṛśaṃ  SvayambhuP iti sarve vayaṃ tatra gośṛṅge gre samādarāt śāntaśriyaṃ mahācārya saṃprārthituṃ vajrāvahai  SvayambhuP ityādiṣṭaṃ narendraṇa śrutvā purohitādayaḥ sarve tatheti vijñapya prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā samantrijanapaurikāḥ purohitaṃ purodhāya gośṛṅge gre mudācarat  SvayambhuP tatra dṛṣṭvā tamācārya nṛpatiḥ saṃpramoditaḥ sametya sāñjalirnatvā pādābje samupāśrayat  SvayambhuP tathā sarve pi lokāśca samīkṣyenaṃ prasāditāḥ sametya pādayornatvā samupatasthire mudā  SvayambhuP tān sarvān samupāsīnān samīkṣya sa mahāmatiḥ śāntaśrīstaṃ mahīpālaṃ sampaśyannevamādiśat  SvayambhuP rājan sadāstu vo bhadraṃ sarvatrāpi nirantaraṃ kimarthamiha prāyāsi tat me gre vaktuṃmarhasi  SvayambhuP iti śāntaśriyā prokte nṛpatiḥ sa kṛtāñjaliḥ praṇatvā taṃ mahācārya paśyannevaṃ nyavedayet  SvayambhuP bho śrīśāstayadarthe haṃ bhavaccharaṇamāvraje tadartha prārthayāmyatra me samupādeṣṭumarhati  SvayambhuP yat me tra pāpato rājye mahotpātaṃ pravarttate tacchāntikaraṇopāyaṃ samupādeṣṭumarhati  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthite rājñā śāntaśrī mantravit sudhīḥ nṛpate taṃ mahāsattvaṃ samālokyaivamādiśat  SvayambhuP nṛpate pāpato traivaṃ mahotpātaṃ pravarttate tatpāpaśamanopāyaṃ vakṣāmi te śṛṇuṣva tat  SvayambhuP yatvamatra nṛpā rājā sarvadharmānupālakaḥ nītidharmmānusāreṇa saṃpālayasi na prajāḥ  SvayambhuP mantriṇo pi tathā sarvanītidharmaparāṅmukhāḥ bhuktvā kāmasukhānyeva pracaranti yathecchayā  SvayambhuP tathā bhṛtyā janāścāpi paurāścāpi mahājanāḥ svakuladharmamutsṛjya pracaranti yathecchayā  SvayambhuP evaṃ sarve pi lokāśca daśākuśalacāriṇaḥ saddharmāṇi pratikṣipya pracaranti pramādataḥ  SvayambhuP tadaitat pāpavaipākyaṃ bhoktavyaṃmeva hi bhava yenaiva yatkṛtaṃ karmma bhoktavyaṃ tena tatphalaṃ  SvayambhuP evaṃ matvā nṛpaḥ svāmī svayaṃ nītyā vicārayan bodhayitvā prayatnena lokān saṃpālayat sadā  SvayambhuP yadyatra nṛpatiḥ samyaga vicārya pramādataḥ svayaṃ kāmasukhānyeva bhuktvā caradyathecchayā  SvayambhuP tathā sarve pi lokāśca nṛpacaryānucāriṇaḥ bhuktvā kāmasukhānyeva pracareyuryathecchayā  SvayambhuP tadā tatra mahotpātaṃ pravarttat pāpato dhruvaṃ pravarttite mahotpāta lokā syuḥ pāpaduḥkhitāḥ  SvayambhuP tatra tān nṛpatiḥ paśyannupekṣyaṃ nirdayaścarat lokasaṃrakṣaṇe asaktaḥ sa sarvapāpabhāg bhavet  SvayambhuP sarvāṇyapi hi pāpāni sarvalokaiḥ kṛtānyapi patitvā nṛpateragre pradadyustatphalāni hi  SvayambhuP iti satyaṃ samākhyātaṃ sarvairapi munīśvaraiḥ natvā rājā svayaṃ nītyā vicārayan samācaret  SvayambhuP iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ śāntaśriyā sumantriṇā śrutvā sa nṛpatīrbhītyā saṃtāpatāpitāśayaḥ  SvayambhuP śāntaśriyaṃ tamācārya samīkṣya śaraṇaṃ gataḥ natvā pādāmbuje bhūyaḥ prārthayadevamādarāt  SvayambhuP śāstaḥ sadā cariṣyāmi bhavadājñāṃ śirāvahan tat me yaducitaṃ dharmma tat samādeṣṭumarhati  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvācāryaḥ sa satmatiḥ nṛpatiṃ taṃ mahāsattvaṃ sampaśyannevamādiśat  SvayambhuP rājañchṛṇu samādhāya vakṣyāmi śubhakāraṇaṃ yadyasti te kṛpā loka tat kuru yanmayoditaṃ  SvayambhuP tadyathaiteṣu tīrtheṣu snātvā nityaṃ yathāvidhi śuciśīlasamācāraḥ samāhitaḥ trimaṇḍalaḥ  SvayambhuP sambodhiṃ praṇidhānena sarvasattvahitārthabhṛt triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā carasva poṣadhaṃ vrataṃ  SvayambhuP tata imaṃ jagannāthaṃ dharmadhātuṃ jinālayaṃ yathāvidhi samārādhya saṃbhajasva sadādarāt  SvayambhuP tathā sarvā imā pañca devatāśca yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcya saṃbhajasva sadādarāt  SvayambhuP imaṃ mañjuśrīyaṃścāpi caityamārādhya sarvadā yathāvidhi samabhyarcya saṃbhajasva mahotsavaiḥ  SvayambhuP tathāṣṭau vītarāgāṃśca samārādhya yathāvidhi samabhyarcya mahotsāhaiḥ saṃbhajasva sadādarāt  SvayambhuP tathā māheśvarīṃ devī khagānanāṃ samādarāṃ samārādhya samabhyarcya saṃbhajasva yathāvidhiṃ  SvayambhuP ete sarve pi devā hi sarvalokādhipeśvarāḥ sarvasattvahitārthena prādurbhūtāḥ svayaṃ khalu  SvayambhuP tadatraiteṣu deveṣu sarveṣu śraddhayā sadā vidhinā bhajanaṃ kṛtvā saṃcarasva jagaddhite  SvayambhuP lokāṃścāpi tathā sarvān bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ sarveṣveteṣu tīrtheṣu snānadānādikaṃ sadā  SvayambhuP kārayitvā mahatpuṇyaṃ jagadbhadrasukhārthadaṃ saṃbuddhaguṇasatsaukhyaṃ cāraya poṣadhaṃ vrataṃ  SvayambhuP eteṣāṃ ca triratnādidevānāṃ bhajanaṃ sadā kārayitvā mahotsāhairbodhimārge pracāraya  SvayambhuP tadaitatpuṇyabhāvena sarvatrāpi caracchubhaṃ tadā sarvamahotpātaṃ sarvatra vilayaṃ vrajet  SvayambhuP tadā brahmamarendrādyāḥ sarve lokādhipā api sudṛśātra samālokya pālayeyuḥ sadā mudā  SvayambhuP tadā saṃpālite smiṃna taiḥ savairlokādhipaiḥ punaḥ subhikṣaṃ śrīśubhotsāhaṃ pravarttayeddhi sarvadā  SvayambhuP tadā sarbe pi lokāśca nīrogāḥ śrīguṇāśrayāḥ viramya pāpamārgebhyaḥ saṃcareran sadā śubhe  SvayambhuP evaṃ dhṛtvā sadā rājan mahāpuṇya prabhāvataḥ ante bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadamāpnuyuḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ mahattaraṃ puṇyaṃ triratnabhajanād bhavaṃ vijñāyādau triratnānāṃ bhajasva śraddhayā smaran  SvayambhuP tataḥ sarveṣu tīrtheṣu snātvā śuddhendriyāśayaḥ triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajasva poṣadhaṃ vrataṃ  SvayambhuP tataḥ sarvānimān devān dharmmadhātumukhān sadā yathāvidhi samārādhya saṃbhajasva samarcayan  SvayambhuP lokānapi tathā sarvān bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ sarveṣveteṣu tīrtheṣu snāpayitvā yathāvidhiṃ  SvayambhuP triratnaśaraṇe sthāpya saṃbodhijñānasādhanaṃ bhadśrīsatguṇādhāraṃ cāraya poṣadhaṃ vrataṃ  SvayambhuP eteṣāmapi devānāṃ kārayitvā sadārcanaṃ bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya cāraya pālayañchubhe  SvayambhuP evaṃ kṛtvā mahatpuṇyaṃ prāpya śrīsadguṇāśrayaḥ bodhisattva mahāsattva mahābhijñā bhaveddhruvaṃ  SvayambhuP tataḥ saṃbodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ arhan bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadamāpnuyāḥ  SvayambhuP iti śāntaśriyā śāstā samādiṣṭaṃ niśamya saḥ nṛpastatheti vijñapya kartumevaṃ samaicchata  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa nṛpatiḥ sarvān mantriṇassacivāñjanān paurān mahājanāścāpi samāmantrayaivamādiśat  SvayambhuP bho mantriṇo janāḥ sarve mātyāḥ paurā mahājanāḥ ācāryena yathādiṣṭaṃ tathā caritumarhatha  SvayambhuP ahamapi tathā dhṛtvā sarvadā bhadrakāraṇaṃ triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā vrataṃ caritumutsahe  SvayambhuP ityādiṣṭaṃ narendreṇa śrutvā te mantriṇo janāḥ paurā mahājanāḥ sarva tatheti pratiśuśruvuḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa nṛpatiḥ sarveḥ sapurohitamantribhiḥ amātyaiḥsacivaiḥ paurairmahājanaiḥ samanvitaḥ  SvayambhuP sarveṣveteṣu tīrtheṣu snātvā yathāvidhi kramāt śuddhaśīlaḥ samādhāya prācarat poṣadhaṃ vrataṃ  SvayambhuP tatassa vimalātmāna triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ dharmadhātuṃ samārādhya samabhyarcyabhijanmudā  SvayambhuP tathā vāyupure vāyudevatāṃśca yathāvidhi agnipure gnidevaṃ ca nāgapure phaṇeśvarān  SvayambhuP vasupure vasundhārāṃ saddharmmaśrīguṇapradāṃ śāntapure maheśānaṃ sambaraṃ sagaṇaṃ kramāt  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi samabhyarcya śraddhayā samupāśritaḥ tathā mañjuśrī yaścaityaṃ samabhyarcyābhajan sadā  SvayambhuP tathāṣṭau vītarāgāṃśca śrīdevīṃśca khagānanāṃ yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyābhajat sadā  SvayambhuP tathā sarve pi lokāste nṛpavṛttānucāriṇaḥ snātvā sarveṣu tīrtheṣu śuddhaśīlā samādarāt  SvayambhuP triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā carantaḥ poṣadhaṃ vrataṃ dharmmadhātumukhān sarvān devāṃścābhyarcya prābhajan  SvayambhuP tadaitatpuṇyabhāvena sarvatra śubhamācarat tataḥ sarva mahotpātaṃ krameṇa praśamaṃ yayau  SvayambhuP tadā sarve pi te lokā nīrogāḥ puṣṭitendriyāḥ mahānandaṃ sukhaṃ prāpya babhūvu dharmmalālasāḥ  SvayambhuP tad dṛṣṭvā na nṛpo rājā pratyakṣaṃ dharmasatphalaṃ aho saddharmamāhātmyamityuktvā nanditācarat  SvayambhuP tadā suvṛṣṭirevātra na babhūva kathaṃcana tad dṛṣṭvā na nṛpaścāsīd durbhikṣaśaṃkitāśayaḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa karuṇāviṣṭahṛdayaḥ sa nṛpaḥ punaḥ śāntaśriyaṃ tamācārya natvaiva prāha sāñjaliḥ  SvayambhuP ācārya kṛpayā te tra carate śubhatādhunā sarvadāpi mahotpātaṃ saṃśāmyata samantataḥ  SvayambhuP suvṛṣṭireva nādyāpi pravarttate kathaṃcana suvṛṣṭikaraṇopāyaṃ tat samādeṣṭumarhati  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvācāryaḥ sa satmatiḥ nṛpatiṃ taṃ mahāsattvaṃ saṃpaśyannevamabravīt  SvayambhuP sādhu rājañchṛṇuṣvātra sadā subhikṣakāraṇaṃ suvṛṣṭikaraṇopāyamupadekṣyāmi sāṃprataṃ  SvayambhuP likhitvā maṇḍalaṃ nāgarājānāṃ yadyathāvidhi tatra nāgādhipān sarvānāvāhyārādhayevahi  SvayambhuP tadatra tvaṃ mahāvīrā bhavasvāttaraḥ sādhakaḥ yathā māyopadiṣṭāni tathā sarvāṇi sādhaya  SvayambhuP ityācārya samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa nṛpatirmudā tatheti prativijñapya tathā bhavitumaicchata  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa vajradhṛg vārā nāgapuraṃ yathāvidhi likhitvā maṇḍalaṃ ramyaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya samārccayat  SvayambhuP tatra nāgādhipān sarvānācāryaḥ sa yathākramaṃ samārādhya samāvāhya pūjayituṃ samālabhat  SvayambhuP tatra nāgādhipāḥ sarve samāgatya yathākramaṃ svasvāsanaṃ samāśritya saṃtasthire prasāditāḥ  SvayambhuP karkoṭako hirāḍeka eva na lajjayāgataḥ tatsamīkṣya sa śāntaśrīrmahācāryā maharddhimān  SvayambhuP nṛpatiṃ taṃ mahāvīraṃ mahāsattvaṃ maharddhikaṃ mahābhijñaṃ samālokya samāmantrayaivamādiśat  SvayambhuP rājan nāgādhipāḥ sarve samāgatā ihādhunā eka karkkoṭako nāgarāja eveha nāgataḥ  SvayambhuP virūpo haṃ kathaṃ nāgarāja mahāsabhāsane gatvā tiṣṭheyamityevaṃ dhyātvā nāyāti lajjayā  SvayambhuP atastaṃ sahasā rājan gatvā tatra mahāhrade karkkoṭakaṃ tamāmantraya saṃprārthyeha samānaya  SvayambhuP yadi saṃprārthyamānāpi nāgachediha so hirāṭ tadā balena dhṛtvāpi sarvathā taṃ samānaya  SvayambhuP ityācārya samādiṣṭaṃ śṛtvā sa nṛpatiḥ sudhīḥ śāntaśriyaṃ tamācārya paśyannevaṃ nyavedayat  SvayambhuP ācārya kathamako haṃ tatrāgāḍhamahāhrade gatvā balena nāgendraṃ dhṛtvā netuṃ praśaknuyāṃ  SvayambhuP iti nivedya taṃ rājñā śrutvācāryaḥ sa mantravit nṛpatiṃ taṃ mahāvīraṃ sampaśyannevamabravīt  SvayambhuP haridaśvaṃ samāruhya puṣpamatmantraśodhitaṃ dhṛtvā braja praśaknoṣi mama mantrānubhāvataḥ  SvayambhuP durvākuṇḍamidaṃ puṣpaṃ tatrādau kṣipa māṃ smaran bhraman yatra caren puṣpaṃ tat yathānusaran baja  SvayambhuP ityupadeśya duvīkaṃ kuṇḍaṃ mantrābhiśodhitaṃ puṣpaṃ datvā narendrāya punarevamupādiśat  SvayambhuP gatvaivaṃ nṛpate tatra nāgapure sametya taṃ karkoṭakaṃ samāmantraya madgiraivaṃ nivedaya  SvayambhuP bho karkkoṭaka nāgendra yadarthedamihāvraja tadbhavānapi jānīyāt tathāpi vakṣyate mayā  SvayambhuP gośṛṅge mahācāryaḥ śāntaśrī rvajrabhṛt kṛtī durbhikṣaśamanaṃ karttuṃ suvṛṣṭicāraṇe sadā  SvayambhuP tatra nāgapure sarvān nāgādhipān yathāvidhi samārādhya samāvāhya pūjayituṃ samārabhat  SvayambhuP sarve nāgādhipāstatra varuṇādyāḥ samāgatāḥ tvameva nāgataḥ kasmāt sahasā gantumarhati  SvayambhuP evaṃ saṃprārthyamāno pi nāgachet so hirāḍ yadi valenāpi samākṛṣya sahasā nīyatāṃ tvayā  SvayambhuP iti śāntaśriyā śāstā samādiśya samādarāt preṣito haṃ tadarthetra tat samagantumarhati  SvayambhuP ityādiśya sa ācāryaḥ puṣpaṃ mantrābhiśodhitaṃ datvā taṃ nṛpatiṃ vīraṃ preṣayat tatra satvaraṃ  SvayambhuP ityācārya samādiṣṭaṃ niśamya sa mahāmatiḥ durvāmuṇḍaṃ samādāya tathetyuktvā tato carat  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa nṛpatirvīraḥ śāstu rājñāṃ śirāvahan haridaśvaṃ samāruhya saṃcaranstad hadaṃ yayau  SvayambhuP tatra tīraṃ samāsādya paśyaṃ nṛpaḥ sa taṃ hadaṃ natvācāryamanusmṛtvā durvvākuṇḍaṃ jale kṣipat  SvayambhuP tanprakṣiptaṃ jale gāḍhe bhraman nāgapure carat rājāpyaśvaṃ samāruhya tatpuṣpānusaran yayau  SvayambhuP evaṃ nāgapure gatvā nṛpatiḥ sa vilokayan karkoṭaka mahīndraṃ taṃ sahasā samupācarat  SvayambhuP tatra sametya sa vīrastaṃ karkoṭakamahīśvaraṃ yathācāryāya saṃdipṭaṃ tathā sarvaṃ nyavedayat  SvayambhuP tat sanniveditaṃ sarva śrutvā nāgādhipāpi saḥ kiñcidapyuttaraṃ naiva dadau tasmai mahībhuje  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa nṛpatiścaivaṃ nivedya taṃ mahīśvaraṃ saṃpaśyan samupāmantraya prārthayadamādarāt  SvayambhuP nāgendro tra prasīda tvaṃ śāsturājñāṃ śirovahaṃ tvadāmantra na evāhaṃ prāgatastat samāvraja  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthyamāno pi rājā sa bhujagādhipaḥ kiñcitprāpyuttaraṃ naiva dadau tasmai mahībhuje  SvayambhuP tato sau nṛpativīraḥ śāstrādiṣṭaṃ yathā tathā sarva nivedya tasyāgre punarevamabhāṣata  SvayambhuP nāgendra nāparādhaṃ me yattvayā na śrutaṃ vacaḥ tanme śāstrā yathādiṣṭaṃ tathā nūnaṃ careya hi  SvayambhuP ityuktepi narendreṇa karkoṭako hi yo pi saḥ kiñcidapyuttaraṃ naiva dadau rājñe mahībhṛte  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa nṛpativīraḥ śāsturājñāṃ śirovahan dhṛtvā tamahimākṛṣya gurutmāniva prācarat  SvayambhuP tato hayāt samānītāḥ guṇakāmadevena saḥ ānīte tena mārgeṇa vaśikācala ucyate  SvayambhuP evaṃ dhṛtvā samākṛṣya sa vīrastaṃ mahīśvaraṃ sahasā nāgapure nītvā śāsturagre samācarat  SvayambhuP ācārya bhavadādeśāt tathā karkkoṭako hirāṭ dhṛtvākṛṣya mayānītastaṃ samīkṣya prasīdatu  SvayambhuP iti niveditaṃ rājñā śrutvācāryaḥ samāditaḥ nṛpatiṃ taṃ mahāvīraṃ sampaśyannevamādiśat  SvayambhuP sādhu rājan mahāvīra yadānītastvayāhirāt tadenamāsane nītvā saṃsthāpaya yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP ityācārya samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa nṛpatistathā nāgarājaṃ tamāmantraya svāsane saṃnyaveśayat  SvayambhuP taṃ dṛṣṭvā svāsanāsīnāṃmācāryaḥ sa yathāvidhiṃ nāgendrān stān samāvāhya samārādhya samārcayat  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa vrajadhṛkājña ācāryaḥ sa mahīpatiḥ sarvān nāgādhipān stutvā prārthayuccaivamādarāt  SvayambhuP bho bhavanto mahānāgarājāḥ sarve mayāgrataḥ samārādhya samāvāhya yathāvidhi samarcitāḥ  SvayambhuP tanme sadā prasīdantu dātumarhanti vāñchitaṃ sarvaloka hitārtheva ārādhyayāmi nānyathā  SvayambhuP yadatra pāpasaṃcārād durbhikṣaṃ varttate dhunā tena sarve pi duḥkhārttā lokaścaranti pātakaṃ  SvayambhuP taddurbhikṣābhiśāntyartha subhikṣakāraṇaṃ sadā suvṛṣṭicaraṇopāyaṃ karomīdaṃ jagaddhite  SvayambhuP te bhavanto tra sarve pi sarvasattvābhirakṣaṇe cārayituṃ samarhanti suvṛṣṭimatra sarvadā  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śāntaśriyā niśamyata sarve nāgādhipāstasya tatheti pratiśuśruvuḥ  SvayambhuP taistatheti pratijñātaṃ nāgarājairniśamya saḥ śāntaśrī nāgarājān stān prārthayadevamādarāt  SvayambhuP bhavanto me prasīdantu yadahaṃ prārthaye punaḥ sarvasattvahite dātuṃ tadapyarhanti vāñchitaṃ  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthite tena śāntaśriyā niśamyate sarvvanāgādhipā tasmai tatheti pratiśuśruvuḥ  SvayambhuP sarve nāgādhipaistaiḥ sampratijñātaṃ niśmya saḥ ācāryastānahīndrāṃśca prārthayedevamādarāt  SvayambhuP bhavantaḥ śrūyatāṃ vākyaṃ yat mayā prārthyate punaḥ tadbhavadbhiḥ pratijñātaṃ saṃdhātavyaṃ tathā sadā  SvayambhuP yadātra pāpasaṃcārād durvaṣṭiśca bhaved dhruvaṃ tadā suvṛṣṭisaṃsiddhirsādhanaṃ tat pranīyatāṃ  SvayambhuP tadyathā bhavatāṃ paṭṭe likhitvā maṇḍalaṃ śubhaṃ yathāvidhi pratiṣṭhāpya saṃsthāpituṃ samutsahe  SvayambhuP durvṛṣṭiḥ syādyadāpyatra tadevaṃ paṭṭamaṇḍalaṃ prasārya vidhinārādhya samāvāhya samarcayat  SvayambhuP evaṃ prasārya paṭṭesmin saṃpūjite yathāvidhi suvṛṣṭiratra yuṣmābhiḥ saṃbharttavyā jagaddhite  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthite tena śāntaśriyā niśamyate sarvanāgādhipāstasmai tatheti pratiśuśruvuḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa mantravit prājñaḥ sarvanāgādhipājñayā likhitvā maṇḍalaṃ paṭṭe pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi  SvayambhuP paścāt kāle tra durvṛṣṭivṛtte suvṛṣṭisādhane nāgapure tra saṃsthāpya nirdagdha saṃpragopitaṃ  SvayambhuP tato vajrī sa ācāryaḥ sarvān stān bhujagādhipān saṃprārthya vinayaṃ kṛtvā visasarjja vinodayan  SvayambhuP tataḥ sarve pi te nāgarājāḥ svasvālayaṃ gatāḥ meghamālāṃ samutthāpya sarvatra samavarṣayan  SvayambhuP tadā suvṛṣṭisaṃcārād durbhikṣaṃ vilayaṃ yayau subhikṣamaṃgalotsāhaṃ prāvarttata samantataḥ  SvayambhuP tadā sarve pi lokāste mahānandapramoditaḥ triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā prācaranta sadā śubhe  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa nṛpati rājā dṛṣṭasatyaḥ prasāditaḥ śāntiśriyaṃ tamācāryaṃ samabhyarcya yathāvidhi  SvayambhuP natvāṣṭāṅgaiḥ prasannātmā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāni ca kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ paśyan prārthayaccaivamādarāt  SvayambhuP bho bhagavan mahācārya bhavaddharmmānubhāvataḥ sarvotpātaṃ śamībhūta suvṛṣṭiḥ saṃpravarttate  SvayambhuP tadatra sarvadā nūnaṃ nirutpātaṃ samantataḥ dharmaśrīmaṃgalotsāhaṃ bhavadeva nirantaraṃ  SvayambhuP evaṃ sadā kṛpā dṛṣṭayā saṃpaśyan viṣaye mama nirutpātaṃ śubhotsāhaṃ kartumarhati sarvathā  SvayambhuP sāmprataṃ saphalaṃ janma saṃsārajīvitaṃ ca me yallokāśca sukhībhūtāḥ saṃcaranta sadā śubhe  SvayambhuP tadahaṃ sāmprataṃ śāstarbhavadājñāṃ śirāvahan svarājyāśramamāśritya careyaṃ pālayañjagat  SvayambhuP tanmenugrahamādhāya kṛpayā saṃprasāditaḥ saṃbodhisādhane cittaṃ sa sthitiṃ karttumarhati  SvayambhuP iti vijñapya bhūpālasta sya śāstuḥ padāmbuje natvānujñāṃ samāsādya mahotsāhaiḥ puraṃ yayau  SvayambhuP tatra sa nṛpa āśritya samantri sacivo mudā bodhicaryāvrataṃ dhṛtvā tasthau kurvan sadā śubhaṃ  SvayambhuP iti svayambhū caityāśramanāmasādhanasuvṛṣṭicāraṇo nāmāṣṭamo dhyāyaḥ navama adhyāyaḥ śrīmahācārya śāntikaraguṇasaṃsiddhimahātmyānubhāva prakathanapravartano nāmaatha maitreya ālokya samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ bhagavantaṃ tamānamya prārthayaccaivamādarāt  SvayambhuP kadā śāntikaraṃ nāma tasyābhavat kathaṃ punaḥ taddhetuṃ śrotumicchāmi samupādeṣṭumarhati  SvayambhuP iti saṃprārthite tena maitreyeṇa sa sarvavit bhagavāstaṃ mahāsattvaṃ sampaśyannevamādiśat  SvayambhuP śṛṇu maitreya vakṣyāmi śāntaśriyāṃ mahadguṇaṃ saddharmmasādhanotsāhaṃ bhadraśrīsadgurṇārthadaṃ  SvayambhuP yo sau rājā mahāsattvaḥ sadharmmaguṇalālasaḥ tyaktvā kāmasukhaṃ rājyaṃ tīrthayātrāmupācarat  SvayambhuP sa sarveṣvapi tīrtheṣu snātvā dānaṃ vidhāya ca trisamādhisamācāraḥ saṃcara poṣadhaṃ vrataṃ  SvayambhuP evaṃ sarveṣu pīṭheṣu bhraman saddharmmamānasaḥ yogacaryāvrataṃ dhṛtvā pracacāra samāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP puṇyakṣetreṣu sarveṣu bhramannaivamihāgatāḥ dṛṣṭvaimaṃ maṇḍalaṃ ramye vismitaṃ samupāyayau  SvayambhuP atraimaṃ dūrato dṛṣṭvā dharmmadhātuṃ jinālayaṃ mudāṣṭāṅgaiḥ praṇatvāśuḥ saṃdraṣṭuṃ samupāyayau  SvayambhuP sametya saṃmahāsattvā jyotīrūpaṃ jinālayaṃ dharmmadhātumimaṃ dṛṣṭvā praṇatvā samupāśrayat  SvayambhuP tataḥ samudito rājā nepāle tra manorame sarvatrāpi ca saṃdraṣṭuṃ pracacāra vilokayan  SvayambhuP teṣu sarveṣu tīrtheṣu snātvā datvā yathepsitaṃ yathāvidhi samādhāya vrataṃ cara samāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP tatoṣṭau vītarāgāṃśca dṛṣṭvā sa saṃpramoditaḥ yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcya sadābhajan  SvayambhuP tataścāsau mahādevī khagānanāṃ maheśvarīṃ yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyābhajanmudā  SvayambhuP tato mañjuśriyaścaityaṃ samīkṣya sa pramoditaḥ yathāvidhi samabhyarcya prābhajat samupasthitaḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ ścaitatmahatpuṇyaiḥ śāntiśrīśubhitendriyaḥ pravajyā saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā brahmacārī babhūva saḥ  SvayambhuP yattasya supraśāntaśrīśobhitānīndriyāni ṣaṭ taṃ nanāma prasiddhaṃ ca śāntaśrīrityabhūdyataḥ  SvayambhuP tato sau satmatirvijño bodhisattvo jagaddhite vajracaryāvrataṃ gṛhaya pracacāra samāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP tataśca śilayāchādya dharmmadhātuṃmimaṃ jinaṃ iṣṭikābhirmahatstūpaṃ vidhāya samagopayat  SvayambhuP tataḥ pañcapureṣvatra sthāpitā pañca devatāḥ mañjuśrīyāmidaṃ caityamanena ca mahatkṛtaṃ  SvayambhuP evaṃ kṛtvātra kāryāṇi sarvāṇi sa mahāmatiḥ bodhisattvā mahābhijñaḥ pracacāra jagaddhite  SvayambhuP tataścātra mahatpātaṃ śamīkṛtya samaṃtataḥ bhadraśrīmaṅgalotsāhaṃ na śāntaśrīḥssadā vyadhāt  SvayambhuP tataścāsau mahābhijño durvṛṣṭi parivarttate nāgarājān samārādhya suvṛṣṭi samacārayat  SvayambhuP evaṃ sa triguṇābhijñāṃ mahotpāta praśāntikṛt śubhaṃkara sadā tena śāntikare iti smṛtaḥ  SvayambhuP īdṛgmantrī mahābhijño vajrācāryā mahāmatiḥ samṛddhisiddhisaṃpannā na bhūtā na bhaviṣyati  SvayambhuP evaṃ vidhāya sarvatra nirutpātaṃ śubhotsavaṃ bodhisattva sa śāntaśrīstrailokyamahitobhavat  SvayambhuP evamasya mahatpuṇyaṃ bhadraśrīguṇasādhanaṃ vijñāya śaraṇaṃ gatvā savitavyaṃ śubhārthibhiḥ  SvayambhuP yadyasya śaraṇaṃ gatvā śraddhayā samupāśritāḥ yathāvidhi samārādhya bhajeyuḥ sarvadā mudā  SvayambhuP te sarve vimalatmāno niḥkleśā vijitendriyāḥ bhadraśrīguṇasaṃpattiṃ sarddhisiddhiṃ samāyayuḥ  SvayambhuP ye ca tasya sadā smṛtvā dhyātvāpi ca samāhitāḥ nāmāpi ca samuccārya bhajeyuḥ śraddhayā sadā  SvayambhuP te pi sarve vikalmāṣāḥ pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ tadguṇaśrīsamāpannā bhaveyu bodhicāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP ityevaṃ tatmahatpuṇyaṃ vijñāya tadguṇārthinaḥ tasyaiva śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajantu te sadā mudā  SvayambhuP ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa sarve pi te sabhāśritāḥ lokāstatheti vijñapya prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ  SvayambhuP evamasau mahāsattvo bhadraśrīsadguṇārthabhṛt sarvasattvahitaṃ kṛtvā saṃtasthe suciraṃ tathā  SvayambhuP tataḥ kāle gate rājā vṛddhobhijīrṇṇitendriyaḥ niḥkleśo viratābhāgo dhyātvaiva samacintayat  SvayambhuP ahaṃ vṛddhotijīrṇṇāṅgaḥ sthāsyāmyevaṃ kiyāccaraṃ avaśyaṃ daivayogeṇa yāsyāmi maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  SvayambhuP tadatrāhaṃ svaputrāya yūne lokānupālane sābhiṣekamidaṃ rājyaṃ dātumarhāmi sāmprataṃ  SvayambhuP iti dhyātvā sa bhūpālo narendradevamātmajaṃ abhiṣiṃcya nṛpaṃ kṛtvā bodhayannevamaṃnvaśāt  SvayambhuP rājan putra samādhāya dharmanītyā samācaran triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā saṃcarasva sadā śubhe  SvayambhuP adyārabhyāsi sarveṣāṃ lokānāmadhipaḥ prabhuḥ sarvadharmānuśāstā ca sarvasattvahitārthabhṛt  SvayambhuP tadatra sakalān lokān dharmanītyānupālayan triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā saṃcaraṃsva sadā śubhe  SvayambhuP ityanuśāsya tanputraṃ pitā sa bhavanispṛhaḥ sarvaparigrahānstyaktvā vanaprasthasamāśrayan  SvayambhuP tatrasthāsau mahābhijñaḥ pariśuddhitrimaṇḍalaḥ samādhinihitaḥ svāntaḥ sasaṃcare bahmasaṃbaraṃ  SvayambhuP tataḥ kāle gate mṛtyusamaye sa samāhitaḥ triratnaṃ sa smaraṃstyaktvā dehaṃ yayau sukhāvatīṃ  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā narendradeva indravat saṃbodhayan prayatnena sarvān lokānapālayat  SvayambhuP so pi rājā viśuddhātmā saddharmmaguṇalālasaḥ śāntikaraṃ tamācārya sametya śaraṇaṃ yayau  SvayambhuP tatra sa samupāśritya śāsturājñāṃ śirovahan triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā prācarat sarvadā śubhe  SvayambhuP sadā sarveṣu tīrtheṣu snānaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi pitrebhyaḥ pradadau piṇḍaṃmarthibhyo pi yathepsitaṃ  SvayambhuP tathāṣṭau vītarāgāṃśca kṣatralokādhipāmapi yathāvidhi samārādhya samārcayat sa parvasuḥ  SvayambhuP tathā ca śrīmahādevīṃ khagānanāṃ yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcya mahotsāhairmudābhajat  SvayambhuP tathā mañjuśrīyaścaitye pṛcchāgresminnupāśrayat yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyābhajat sadā  SvayambhuP tathā vāyupure vāyudevatāḥ sagaṇā api yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyābhajat sadā  SvayambhuP tathā vahnipure vahnidevatāḥ sagaṇā api yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyābhajat sadā  SvayambhuP tathā nāgapure nāgadevatāḥ sagaṇā api yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyābhajat sadā  SvayambhuP tathā vasupure devīṃ vasudhārāṃ samaṇḍalām yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyā sadābhajat  SvayambhuP tathā śāntipure śrīmatsambaraṃ sagaṇaṃ jinaṃ yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyā sadābhajat  SvayambhuP tathā tasya dharmadhātoḥ sa narendraḥ samupāśritaḥ yathāvidhi samārādhya prābhajan sarvadārcayan  SvayambhuP evaṃ sa nṛpatī rājā saddharmaguṇalālasaḥ triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā saṃprācarat sadā śubhe  SvayambhuP evaṃ sa nṛpa eteṣu tīrthayātrādikarmasu bodhayitvā prayatnena sarvān lokān yayā jayat  SvayambhuP tathā sarve pi te lokā dhṛtvā nṛpānuśāsanaṃ eteṣu tīrthayātrādikarmasu saṃpracerire  SvayambhuP tathāṣṭau vītarāgāṃśca devīṃ khagānanāmapi pañcaitā devatāścāpi caityaṃ mañjuśriyo pi ca  SvayambhuP jagadīśaṃ jagannāthaṃ dharmadhātuṃ jinālayaṃ yathāvidhi samabhyarcya prābhajanta sadā mudā  SvayambhuP etaddharmānubhāvena sarvadātra sumaṅgalaṃ nirutpātaṃ mahotsāhaṃ prāvarttata samantataḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ sa nṛpatī rājā narendra deva ātmanaḥ bodhicaryāḥ vrataṃ dhṛtvā saṃpracara jagaddhite  SvayambhuP parānapi tathā sarvān lokān yatnena bodhayan bodhimārge samāyujya prācārayajjagaddhite  SvayambhuP evaṃ sa indravad rāja bodhisattvā jagatprabhuḥ sarvasattvahitaṃ kṛtvā tasthau ciraṃ śubhe raman  SvayambhuP tataḥ śrīmān sa ācāryaḥ śāntikaro maharddhikaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ pravṛddho pi nirvātuṃ nābhivāṃchati  SvayambhuP sarvasattvahitākāṃkṣī śāntipurāgratādhasi dhyānāgāre mahoddāre yājanaika pramāṇike  SvayambhuP āropya śrīmahojvāle cintāmaṇi mahādhvajaṃ sa prājñaḥ sa mahāsattvo bodhisattvā jinātmajaḥ  SvayambhuP samādhidhāraṇīvidyāyogadhyānasamāhitaḥ sambodhipraṇidhiṃ dhṛtvā tasthau niścaramānasaḥ  SvayambhuP yadā saddharmmahīṇe tra lokapaṃca kaṣāyite tadotthāya samādheḥ sa saddharmma deśayiṣyati  SvayambhuP yadā yadātra satmitraḥ śāstrā vidyādhipā na hi tadā tadā na sanmitraḥ śāstrāvidyādhipobhavan  SvayambhuP sarvānlokān prayatnena nivārya pāpamārgataḥ bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya cārayiṣyati saddharme  SvayambhuP evaṃ dhyātvā sa ācāryaḥ śāntikaraḥ samādhibhṛt sarvasattvahitārthena tasthau yogasamāhitaḥ  SvayambhuP evaṃ sa triguṇācāryaḥ sarvasattvahitārthabhṛt bodhisattvamahābhijña tiṣṭha tatra jagaddhita  SvayambhuP ye tasya śaraṇaṃ gatvā smṛtvā dhyātvā samādarāt nāmāpi ca samuccāryaṃ bhajanti śraddhayā sadā  SvayambhuP te pi sarve mahābhijñā bodhisattvā vicakṣaṇāḥ bhadraśrīguṇasaṃpannā bhaviṣyanti sadā bhave  SvayambhuP tataste vimalātmānaścaturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ bodhicaryāvrataṃ dhṛtvā cariṣyanti jagaddhite  SvayambhuP tataste bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ arhanto bodhimāsādya prāpsyanti saugataṃ padaṃ  SvayambhuP ye ca tadguṇamāhātmyaṃ śṛṇvanti śraddhayā mudā te pi tadguṇa saṃpatti saṃsiddhiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ  SvayambhuP iti vijñāya vāñchanti yastasya guṇasaṃpada te sadguṇamāhātmyaṃ śrotumarhati sādaraṃ  SvayambhuP ityādiṣṭaṃ muṇīndrena śrutvā sarvasabhāśritāḥ lokāstatheti saṃśrutya prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ  SvayambhuP iti śrīmahācāryaśāntikaraguṇasaṃsiddhimāhātmyānubhāvaprakathanapravṛtto nāmādhyāya navamaḥ daśama adhyāyaḥ śrī dharmmadhātusvayambhūtpattidharmmamāhātmyasubhāṣitasūtraṃ nāmaathāsau bhagavān bhūyo maitreyaṃ taṃ mahāmatiṃ samālokya sabhāṃ cāpi samāmantryaivamādiśat  SvayambhuP śṛṇu maitreya vakṣyāmi mañjuśriyo jagadguroḥ saddharmaguṇamāhātmyaṃ saṃbodhijñānadāyakaṃ  SvayambhuP yadiyaṃ bhikṣuṇī cūḍā suśīlā brahmacāriṇī idaṃ mañjuśriyaṃ ścaityaṃ śraddhayā samupāśritā  SvayambhuP śuddhotpalasrajo nityaṃ samabhyarcya yathāvidhi smṛtvā dhyātvā samārādhya sabhaktyā śraddhayā sadā  SvayambhuP ādyāṃ cale cule vande svāheti navamākṣaraṃ dhāraṇī paramāvidyāṃ paṭhantī bhajane sadā  SvayambhuP etanpuṇyānubhāvena cūṇḍeyaṃ bhikṣuṇī satī pañcābhijñāvatī varṣairdvādaśabhirbhaved dhruvaṃ  SvayambhuP tataśceyaṃ mahābhijñā śrīsamṛddhiguṇāśrayā sarvasattvahitaṃ kṛtvā pracared bodhisaṃvaraṃ  SvayambhuP tato rhantī mahāprājñā pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalā trividhāṃ bodhimāsādya saṃbuddhapadamāpsyati  SvayambhuP evamanyepi lokāśca caityamañjuśriyo traye paṭhantī dhāraṇīmenāṃ bhajanti śraddhayā sadā  SvayambhuP te pi sarve vikalmāṣāḥ pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ bhadraśrīsadguṇādhārā bodhisattvā jitendriyāḥ  SvayambhuP pañcābhijñapadaprāptāścaturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ sarvasattvahitādhārā careyurbodhisambaraṃ  SvayambhuP tataste bodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ jitvā māragaṇān sarvān niḥkleśā vimalendriyāḥ  SvayambhuP arhanto pi mahābhijñāḥ saṃbodhisādhanāratāḥ trividhāṃ bodhimāsādya saṃbuddhapadamāpnuyuḥ  SvayambhuP yūyamapiti matvātra caityamañjuśriyastathā paṭhanto dhāraṇīmenāṃ bhajadhvaṃ bodhimānasāḥ  SvayambhuP etatpuṇyābhiliptā hi pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ yūyamapi tathā sarve bhaveta sugatātmajāḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā bhadraśrīsadguṇāśrayāḥ mahābhijñā jagannāthā bhaveta bhadracāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ saṃbodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ jitvā māragaṇān sarvāścaturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP arhantastrividhāṃ bodhiṃ prāpya buddhā bhaviṣyatha iti satyaṃ parijñāya yadi saṃbodhimicchatha  SvayambhuP asmin mañjuśriyaścaityaṃ bhajadhvaṃ sarvadā mudā ityādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa niśamya te sasāṃdhikāḥ  SvayambhuP sarvalokāstathetyuktvā prābhyanandat prabodhitāḥ tataḥ sarve pi te lokā brahmāśakrādayo marāḥ  SvayambhuP sarve lokādhipāścāpi sārddhaṃ parijanairmudā bhagavantaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ sasaṃgha saṃprasāditāḥ  SvayambhuP natvā pradakṣiṇī kṛtvā svasvālayaṃ mudā yayuḥ sarve martyā nṛpādyāśca samantrijanapaurikāḥ  SvayambhuP sasāṃdhikaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ natvā svasvālayaṃ yayuḥ hārīti yakṣiṇīśāpi sātmajā bauddharakṣaṇī  SvayambhuP triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā dharmadhātorūpāśrayat tataḥ sa bhagavāṃścāpi samutthāya sasāṃdhikaḥ  SvayambhuP prabhāsayañjagadbhāsā jaṭodyānāśrame yayau tatra sa trijagannātho vihāre sahasāṃdhikaiḥ  SvayambhuP saddharmmasamupādiśya vijahāra jagaddhite iti te guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate  SvayambhuP śrutvāpyetanmahārājā śraddhayābhyanumodaya iti śāstrārhatādiṣṭaṃ niśamya sa narādhipaḥ  SvayambhuP prasāditastamarhanta natvā prāhaivamādarāt bhadantohaṃ samicchāmi saṃdraṣṭuṃ taṃ svayaṃbhuvaṃ  SvayambhuP tannaipāle pragacchāmi tadanujñāṃ pradehi me iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā sorhanyatirmudā  SvayambhuP nṛpatiṃ taṃ mahāsattvaṃ saṃpaśyannevamādiśyat sādhu rājan samicchā te yadyasti taṃ svayambhuvaṃ  SvayambhuP draṣṭuṃ gaccha samārādhya bhaja śraddhāsamanvitaḥ sarvatīrtheṣu ca snātvā datvā dānaṃ yathepsitaṃ  SvayambhuP vītarāgāṃ samārādhya samabhyarcyabhijādarāt dharmodayāṃ mahādevīṃ khagānanāṃ jineśvarīṃ  SvayambhuP śraddhayā samupāśritya samabhyarcya bhajādarāt pañcapurāsthitāḥ pañca devatāśca yathāvidhi  SvayambhuP samārādhya samabhyarcya bhaja bhaktyā samādarāt mañjudevasya caityaṃ ca samālokya yathāvidhi  SvayambhuP samārādhya samabhyarcya bhajenāṃ dhāraṇīṃ paṭhan ācārya ca guhāsīnaṃ samādhidhyānasaṃsthitaṃ  SvayambhuP dhyātvārādhya samabhyarcya natvā bhaja samādarāt evamanyān mahāsattvān dharmmadhātorūpāsakān  SvayambhuP sarvānapi samārādhya samabhyarcya praṇāmaya etatpuṇyaviśuddhātmā bhadraśrī sadguṇāśrayaḥ  SvayambhuP bodhisattvā mahāsattvā jagadbharttā bhavedapi tataḥ saṃbodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ  SvayambhuP arhansaṃbodhimāsādya saṃbuddhapadamāpsyasi iti satyaṃ parijñāya saṃbodhi yadi vāñchasi  SvayambhuP gatvā tatra mahotsāhairdharmmadhātuṃ vilokya taṃ yathāvidhi samārādhya bhajasva samupāśritaḥ  SvayambhuP gaccha te maṅgalaṃ bhuyāt sidhyatu te samīhitaṃ yathecchayā samālokya samāyāhi pramoditaḥ  SvayambhuP iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa nṛpatirmudā taṃ guruṃ sāñjalirnatvā prāpyānujñāmanandataḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā samantrijanapaurikāḥ rājarddhi maṃgalotsāhaiḥ saṃprasthito mudācarat  SvayambhuP tatra mārge sa rājendraḥ sarvān lokān prasādayan mahotsāhaiścarannāśu naipālaṃ samupāyayau  SvayambhuP tatra prāptaḥ samālokya dūrāt taṃ śrīsvayaṃmbhuvaṃ sāñjali praṇatiṃ kṛtvā pramanāḥ sahasā caret  SvayambhuP tatra sarvatra saṃvīkṣya śubhotsāhapravarttitaṃ vismayānanditānsā sa nṛpatiḥ samupāsaret  SvayambhuP tatra sarveṣu tīrtheṣu krameṇa sa narādhipaḥ snātvārthibhyo yathākāmaṃ dadau dānaṃ caran vrataṃ  SvayambhuP tato ṣṭau vītarāgān sa nṛpatirvīkṣya harṣitaḥ yathāvidhi samārādhya bhajatyarcya yathāvidhi  SvayambhuP tato mudācaran vīkṣya dharmmadhātuṃ jinālayaṃ yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyābhajan kramāt  SvayambhuP tato vāyupure vāyudevatāṃ sagaṇāṃ mudā yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyacyanitobhajata  SvayambhuP tataścāgnipure vahnidevatāḥ sagaṇāmapi yathāvidhi samārādhya saṃpūjyābhajadādarāt  SvayambhuP tato nāgapure nāgadevatāḥsagaṇā api yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyā mudābhajat  SvayambhuP tato vasupure devīṃ sagaṇāṃ śrīvasundharāṃ yathāvidhi samārādhya bhajatyarcya samādarāt  SvayambhuP tataḥ śāntipure śrīmatsambaraṃ sagaṇaṃ tathā yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcya mudābhajat  SvayambhuP tataḥ śāntikarācārya samādhidhyānasaṃsthitaṃ dhyātvārādhya samabhyarcya prābhajan saṃpramoditaḥ  SvayambhuP tato dharmmodayā devī khagānanāṃ maheśvarīṃ yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcya mudābhajat  SvayambhuP sambuddhaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sarvajña karuṇāspadaṃ samantabhadraśāstāraṃ śākyasiṃhaṃ namāmyahaṃ  SvayambhuP śrīghanaṃ śrīmatiṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śīlarāśiṃ śivakaraṃ śrīmantaṃ śrīkaraṃ śāntaṃ śāntimūrti namāmyaham  SvayambhuP nairātmavādinaṃ siṃhaṃ niravadyaṃ nirāśravaṃ nītijñaṃ nirmalātmānaṃ niṣkalaṃkaṃ namāmyaham  SvayambhuP nirdvandvaṃ nirahaṃkāraṃ nirvikalpaṃ tathāgataṃ nirddhūtanikhilakleśaṃ niṣprapaṃcaṃ namāmyahaṃ  SvayambhuP viśveśvaraṃ viśeṣo haṃ viśvarūpaṃ vināyakaṃ viśvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇṇa vītarāgaṃ namāmyahaṃ  SvayambhuP vidhāvareṇa saṃpannaṃ viśveśamvimalaprabhaṃ vinītavegaṃ vimalaṃ vītamohaṃ namāmyahaṃ  SvayambhuP dudantidamakaṃ śāntaṃ śuddhaṃ pañcajinālayaṃ sugatiṃ suśrutaṃ saumyaṃ śubhrakīrtti namāmyahaṃ  SvayambhuP yogīśvaraṃ daśabalaṃ lokajñaṃ lokapūjitaṃ lokācārya lokamūrtiṃ lokānāthaṃ namāmyahaṃ  SvayambhuP kalaṃkamuktiṃ kāmāriṃ sakalaikaṃ kalādharaṃ kāntamūrti dayāpātraṃ kanakābhaṃ namāmyahaṃ  SvayambhuP tato mañjuśriyaścaityaṃ dharmadhātumupāśrayan yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyānatobhajat  SvayambhuP tato mudā caran vīkṣya dharmadhātuṃ jinālayaṃ yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyābhajan mudā  SvayambhuP bhaktyā paramayāstauṣījinālayaṃ svayaṃbhuvaṃ jyotīrūpāya caitanyaṃ rūpāya bhavate namaḥ  SvayambhuP murādinidhanāya śrīdātre praṇavarupiṇe viśvatomukharupāya bhaktavatsala te namaḥ  SvayambhuP pṛthvyādibhūtanirmātre jagadvaṃdyāyate namaḥ jagatsraṣṭe jagatpātre jagaddhartre namo namaḥ  SvayambhuP dhyānagamyāya dhyeyāya cartuvargapradāyine evaṃ stutvā aśokaḥ sa punaḥ kṣamāpanaṃ vyadhāt  SvayambhuP evaṃ sa nṛpatiḥ sarvān dharmadhātorupāsakān mahāsattvān samabhyarcya satkṛtya samatoṣayat  SvayambhuP evaṃ sa nṛparājaḥ śrī dharmadhatorūpāśritaḥ triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā prācarad bodhisambaraṃ  SvayambhuP tataḥ sa nandito rājā samantrijanapaurikaḥ natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya dharmmadhātuṃ mudācarat  SvayambhuP tataścaran sa bhūmīndro mahotsāhaiḥ pramoditaḥ sahasā puramāsādya vihāra samupācarat  SvayambhuP tatropetya tamarhantamupaguptasasāṃdhikaṃ samīkṣya sañjalirnatvā sabhaikāntaṃ samāśrayat  SvayambhuP taṃ samāyātamālokya so rhe śāstā prasannadṛk svāgataṃ kuśalaṃ kaccinnṛpatiṃ paryapṛcchata  SvayambhuP tacchutvā sa mahīpālaḥ śāstāraṃ taṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ praṇatvā suprasannāsyaḥ saṃpaśyannevamabravīt  SvayambhuP samāgatosmyahaṃ śāstarbhavatkṛpānubhāvataḥ kuśalaṃ me kathaṃ na syāt sarvatrāpi sadāpi hi  SvayambhuP bhavatkṛpānubhāvena nepāle haṃ mudācaran dṛṣṭvā sarveṣu tīrtheṣu snātvā dānaṃ yathepsitaṃ  SvayambhuP tathāṣṭau vītarāgāśca samālokya pramāditaḥ yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyabhijaṃ kramāt  SvayambhuP tataḥ samīkṣya taṃ śrīmaddharmmadhātuṃ svayaṃbhuvaṃ yathāvidhi samārādhya samabhyarcyābhajan mudā  SvayambhuP tato vāyupure vāyudevatābhyarccitā mayā tataścāgnipure vahnirdevatāpi mayārccitā  SvayambhuP tathā nāgapure nāgarājāṃścāpi mayārccitā tathā tathā vasupure devī vasundharāṃ samarccitā  SvayambhuP tataḥ śāntipure śrīmatsambaraśca samarccitaḥ tataḥ śāntikarācāryaḥ samālokya mayārcitaḥ  SvayambhuP devīṃ khagānanāṃ cāpi samārādhya samarcitā mañjudevasya caityaṃ ca yathāvidhi samarcitaṃ  SvayambhuP evaṃ bhadanta tatropacchandohe puṇyabhūtale yathāvidhi samārādhya sarvadevā mayārcitāḥ  SvayambhuP etatpuṇyaṃ mayā labdhaṃ bhavatkṛpānubhāvataḥ tadatra janmasāphalyaṃ jīvitaṃ cāpi me dhunā  SvayambhuP tathātra sarvadā śāsta dharmadhātuṃ jinālayaṃ smṛtvā nāma samuccārya dhyātvā bhajeya mā bhavaṃ  SvayambhuP iti rājñā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā so rha prasāditaḥ nṛpati taṃ samālokya punarevaṃ samādiśat  SvayambhuP dhanyo si yatmahārājadharmadhātuṃ jinālayaṃ smṛtvā dhyātvāpi saṃbhaktuṃmicchase tra sadā bhaja  SvayambhuP etatpuṇyaviśuddhātmā bhadraśrīsadguṇāśrayaḥ bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvadharmādhipo bhaveḥ  SvayambhuP tataḥ saṃbodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ arhanstribodhimāsādya dhruvaṃ buddhapadaṃ labheḥ  SvayambhuP samutpattikathāṃ tasya dharmadhātoḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ śrutvāpi yatmahatpuṇyaṃ saṃbodhisādhanaṃ labhet  SvayambhuP iti matvā samutpattikathāṃ tasya svayaṃbhuvaḥ satkṛtya śraddhayā martyāḥ śrotumarhanti sarvathā  SvayambhuP samutpattikathāṃ tasya dharmadhātoḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ śṛṇvanti ye narā bhaktyā satkṛtya śraddhayā mudā  SvayambhuP durgatiṃ te na gacchanti kutrāpi hi kadācan sadā sadgatisaṃjātā bhadraśrīsadguṇāśrayāḥ  SvayambhuP sarvasattvahitādhānabodhicaryāvratāratāḥ mahābhijñā jagannāthā bhaveyuḥ sugatātmajāḥ  SvayambhuP krameṇa bodhisambhāraṃ pūrayitvā jagaddhite arhantatrividhāṃ bodhiṃ prāpyeyuḥ saugataṃ padaṃ  SvayambhuP iti matvā mahārāja śrotavyaṃ śraddhayādarāt svayambhūguṇamāhātmyaṃ durllabhaṃ bodhivāñchibhiḥ  SvayambhuP śṛṇvanti ye narā bhaktyā satkṛtya śraddhayā mudā svayaṃbhūguṇamāhātmyasaddharmaśrīguṇārthadaṃ  SvayambhuP te pi na durgatiṃ yāyuḥ sadāsadgatisaṃgatāḥ bhadraśrīsadguṇādhārā bhaveyurbodhilābhinaḥ  SvayambhuP tasmādetatmahatpuṇyaṃ śrutvā dhyātvā sadādarāt smṛtvā nāma samuccārya saṃbhaktavyaṃ svayaṃbhuvaṃ  SvayambhuP ahamapi purā rājan dharmmadhātoḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ śrutvā sadguṇasāṃkathyaṃ babhūva saṃpramoditaḥ  SvayambhuP tato haṃ sahasā tatra nepāle samupācaraṃt snātvā sarveṣu tīrtheṣu dadau dānaṃ yathepsitaṃ  SvayambhuP aṣṭau tān vītarāgāṃśca samārādhya mayārcitāḥ devīṃ khagānanāṃ cāpi samārādhya samarcitā  SvayambhuP mañjudevasya caityaṃ ca samārādhya samarcitaṃ pañca purā sthitā pañca devatāśca samarcitāḥ  SvayambhuP tathā śāntikarācāryaḥ samālokya samarcitaḥ tataḥśaraṇamāśritya dharmadhāto svayaṃbhuvaḥ  SvayambhuP satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ samārādhya mudā bhajaṃ evaṃ tatra sadāśritya dharmadhātorūpāsakaḥ  SvayambhuP triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā prācaran bodhisaṃbaraṃ etatpuṇyaviśuddhātmā pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalaḥ  SvayambhuP ahaṃ bodhiṃ samāsādya jinātmajā bhave dhunā iti vijñāya mānuṣyā vāñchanti ye sunirvṛtiṃ  SvayambhuP dharmadhātuṃ samārādhya bhajantu te sadā mudā smṛtvā dhyātvā ca nāmāpi samuccārya samādarāt  SvayambhuP samālokya praṇatvāpi bhajantu taṃ jinālayaṃ ye bhajanti sadā smṛtvā dhyātvā natvā jinālayaṃ  SvayambhuP drutaṃ saṃbodhimāsādya saṃbuddhapadamāpnuyuḥ iti satyaṃ samākhyātaṃ sarvairapi munīśvaraiḥ  SvayambhuP śrutvānumodya taṃ dharmadhātuṃ smṛtvā bhajantvalaṃ subhāṣitamidaṃ yepi śrutvānumoditāśayāḥ  SvayambhuP dharmadhātumanusmṛtvā dhyātvā bhajanti sarvadā te pi caitatmahatpuṇyapariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ  SvayambhuP bhadraśrīsadguṇādhārāścaturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ bodhisattvā mahāsattvā mahābhijñāḥ śubhendriyāḥ  SvayambhuP drutaṃ saṃbodhimāsādya saṃbuddhapadamāpnuyuḥ iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate  SvayambhuP tvamapīdaṃ sadā lokā śrāvayitvānumodaya etatpuṇyānubhāvena sarvatra sarvadāpi te  SvayambhuP nirutpātaṃ śubhotsāhaṃ bhavennūnaṃ narādhipaḥ iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśoko nṛpo mudā  SvayambhuP tatheti prativijñapya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ tataḥ sarve pi te lokā niśamyaitatsubhāṣitaṃ  SvayambhuP anumodya mahotsāhaiḥ saṃcerire śubhe sadā tadaitatpuṇyabhāvena sarvatra tatra sarvadā  SvayambhuP nirutpātaṃ śubhotsāhaṃ prāvarttata nirantaraṃ ityādiśya mahābhijño jayaśrīḥ sa mahāmatiḥ  SvayambhuP sarvānstān sāṃdhikān paśyan punarevaṃ samādiśat yatredaṃ dharmmasāṃkathyaṃ prāvarttayet kalāvapi  SvayambhuP bhāṣetya śṛṇuyādyaśca śrāvayedyaḥ pracārayet eteṣāṃ tatra sarveṣāṃ saṃbuddhāḥ sakalāḥ sadā  SvayambhuP kṛpā dṛṣṭyā samālokya prakuryurbhadramābhavaṃ sarvā pāramitā devyasteṣāṃ tatra sadā śivaṃ  SvayambhuP kṛtvā saṃbodhisaṃbhāraṃ pūrayeyuryathākramaṃ sarve pi bodhisattvāśca pratyekasugatā api  SvayambhuP arhanto yoginasteṣāṃ prakuryurmaṅgalaṃ sadā sarve lokādhipāścāpi sarve cāpi maharṣayaḥ  SvayambhuP tatra teṣāṃ hi sarveṣāṃ kuryuḥ samīkṣya maṅgalaṃ sarve devādhipāścāpi sarvadaityādhipā api  SvayambhuP tathā sarve pi gandharvāḥ sarvayakṣādhipā api garuḍā nāgarājāśca kumbhāṇḍādhīśvarā api  SvayambhuP samīkṣya sarvadā teṣāṃ rakṣāṃ kuryuḥ samantataḥ sarvāśca mātṛkā devyaḥ sabhairavagaṇā api  SvayambhuP kṛtvā rakṣāṃ sadā teṣāṃ kuryurbhadraṃ samantataḥ sarve grahāśca tārāśca siddhā vidyādharā api  SvayambhuP sādhyāścāpi sadālokya teṣāṃ kuryuḥ sumaṅgalaṃ bhūtapretapiśācāśca duṣṭā māragaṇā api  SvayambhuP vīkṣya teṣāṃ prasannāste rakṣāṃ kuryuḥ sadā mudā svayambhūguṇamāhātmya sāṃkathyaṃ yo likhet mudā  SvayambhuP tenāpi likhitaṃ sarva mahāyānasubhāṣitaṃ lekhāpitaṃ ca yenedaṃ dharmadhātusubhāṣitaṃ  SvayambhuP tenāpi sakalaṃ sūtraṃ lekhāpitaṃ bhaved dhruvaṃ likhitaṃ cāpi yecedaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi  SvayambhuP śuddhasthāne gṛhe sthāpya pūjāṅgaiḥ sarvadārcitaṃ tenārhanto jināḥ sarve pratyekasugatā api  SvayambhuP sasaṃghā bodhisattvāśca bhavanti pūjitāḥ khalu yaścāpīdaṃ svayaṃ dhṛtvā parebhyo pi samādiśat  SvayambhuP bhāvayet satataṃ smṛtvā dhyātvāpi praṇamenmudā tasya sarvamunīndro hi pratyekasugatā api  SvayambhuP arhanto bodhisattvāśca tuṣṭā dadyuḥ samīhitaṃ yaścaitadupadeṣṭāraṃ sarvāśca śrāvakānapi  SvayambhuP yathāvidhi sa samabhyarcya bhājanaiḥ samatoṣayet tena sarve pi saṃbuddhāḥ pratyekasugatā api  SvayambhuP arhanto bhikṣavaḥ sarve yogino brahmacāriṇaḥ bodhisattvāśca sarve pi vratino yatayo pi ca  SvayambhuP arcitā bhojitāstuṣṭā bhaveyuranumoditāḥ kimevaṃ vahunoktena sarve buddhā munīśvarāḥ  SvayambhuP sarvāstārāśca devyo pi sarvasaṃghā jinātmajāḥ nityaṃ teṣāṃ kṛpā dṛṣṭayā samālokyānumoditāḥ  SvayambhuP rakṣāṃ vidhāya sarvatra varaṃ dadyuḥ samīhitaṃ  SvayambhuP sarve lokādhipāścāpi sarve devā surādhipāḥ rakṣāṃ kṛtvā varaṃ dadyusteṣāṃ saddharmasādhane  SvayambhuP rājāno pi sadā teṣāṃ rakṣā kṛtvānumoditāḥ yathābhivāñchitaṃ datvā pālayeyuḥ sadādarāt  SvayambhuP mantriṇo pi sadā teṣāṃ sāmātyasacivānugāḥ sabhṛtyasainyabhaṭṭāśca bhaveyurhitakāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP sarve vaiśyāśca sarvārthabharttāraḥsyu suhṛnpriyāḥ śreṣṭimahājanāḥ sarve bhaveyurhitakāriṇaḥ  SvayambhuP dviṣopi dāsatāṃ yāyurdṛṣṭāśca syurhitāśayāḥ evamanyepi lokāśca servva syurmaitramānasāḥ  SvayambhuP paśavaḥ pakṣiṇaścāpi sarvakīṭāśca jantavaḥ naiva teṣāṃ viruddhā syuḥ bhaveyurhitaśaṃsina  SvayambhuP evaṃ sarvatra lokeṣu teṣāṃ saddharmasādhināṃ nirutpātaṃ śubhotsāhaṃ saumāṅgalyaṃ sadā bhavet  SvayambhuP evaṃ bhadrataraṃ puṇyaṃ svayabhūṃbhavanodbhavaṃ natvā taṃ trijagannāthaṃ bhajadhvaṃ sarvadā mudā  SvayambhuP ye tasya śaraṇe sthitvā smṛtvā dhyātvā samāhitāḥ nāmāpi ca samuccārya bhajanti śraddhayā sadā  SvayambhuP teṣāṃ trinyapi ratnāni suprasannāni sarvadā kṛpā dṛṣṭayā samālokya kṛtvā deyuḥ sadā śubhaṃ  SvayambhuP iti śāstrāsamādiṣṭaṃ jayaśriyā niśamyate jineśvarī pramukhāḥ saṃghā sarve nandanprabodhitāḥ  SvayambhuP sarvāvatī sabhā sāpi śrutvaitat saṃprasāditāḥ tatheti prativijñapya prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ  SvayambhuP tataste sakalā lokāḥ samutthāya prasāditāḥ jayaśriya sasaṃghaṃ taṃ natvā svasvāśramaṃ yayuḥ  SvayambhuP tatra nityamupetyatyarddhyā sasaṃghaḥ sajinātmajā snātvā sarveṣu tīrtheṣu dhṛtvā vrataṃ yathāvidhi  SvayambhuP tato ṣṭau vītarāgāṃśca devīṃ cāpi khagānanāṃ pañcamā devatāścāpi yathāvidhi samarccayan  SvayambhuP tathā śāntikarācārya caitya mañjuśriyo pi ca dharmādhātuṃ samārādhya dhyātvābhyarcya sadābhajat  SvayambhuP tadaitatpuṇyabhāvena viṣaye tatra sarvadā nirutpātaṃ śubhotsāhaṃ prāvarttata samaṃtataḥ  SvayambhuP tataścāsau mahābhijñā jayaśrīḥ sugatātmajaḥ sarvānstān sāṃdhikān paśyan punarevaṃ samādiśat  SvayambhuP yatredaṃ dharmasāṃkathyaṃ pracāritaṃ svayaṃbhuvaḥ tatraittpuṇyabhāvena bhavatu sarvadā śubhaṃ  SvayambhuP saṃbuddhāstatra sarve pi pratyekasugatā api arhanto bodhisattvāśca kurvantu maṃṅgalaṃ sadā  SvayambhuP sarve lokādhipāścāpi sarve cāpi maharṣayaḥ samālokya sadā tatra prakurvantu sumaṅgalaṃ  SvayambhuP kāle varṣantu meghāśca bhūyācchaśyavatī mahī nirutpātaṃ subhikṣyaṃ ca bhavantu tatra sarvadā  SvayambhuP rājā bhavatu dhārmmiṣṭho mantriṇo nīticāriṇaḥ sarve lokāḥsuvṛttiṣṭhā bhavantu dharmasādhinaḥ  SvayambhuP sarve sattvāḥ samācārāḥ saṃbodhivihitāśayāḥ triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā saṃcarantāṃ sadā śubhe  SvayambhuP iti jayaśriyādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sarve pi sāṃdhikāḥ evamastviti prābhāṣya prābhyanandanprasāditāḥ  SvayambhuP iti śrī dharmmadhātusvayambhūtpattidharmmamāhātmyasubhāṣitasūtraṃ daśama adhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ ye dharmmā hetuprabhāvā hetu steṣāṃ tathāgataḥ hyavadat teṣāṃ ca yo nirodha evaṃ vādī mahāśramaṇaḥ śubhamastu  deyadharmo yaṃ pravaramahāyāyinaḥ śrīmatrudravarṇṇamahāvihārāvasthitaḥ paramopāsakaśrīśākyavaṃśodbhavaḥ śrīrāmānandena likhito gamat saṃpūrṇṇa śubhamastu sarvadāḥ nepāle hāyane yātaḥ nāgamunīrasānviteḥ cāṣāḍhe kṣīnacandre tu pañcamyāñca tithau śubhe   saṃpūrṇṇamagamat tasmiṃ śrīrāmānandena lekhitaḥ yadi śuddhamaśuddhaṃ vā śodhanīyaṃ dahadvudhaiḥ   yatpuṇyalikhite proktaṃ yatpuṇyapātane tathā tatpuṇyena jagat sarva prāpnuyād bodhimuttamāṃ   śrīrāmānandayā pustaka juro śubhaṃ upasargga maharādaharāścaiva śītarāpūṭaloka vā upasarggī mahāmārī saptaite lokahārakaḥ saṃvat  śrāvaṇa śukla  samāptam
